French Academy

July 28, 2025

almond_cream_cake.txt - Almond Cream Cake (Crème d'Amande)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French almond cream filling for cakes
  • Understand the importance of gentle mixing techniques for delicate pastry creams
  • Master the art of assembling and baking a delicious almond cream cake using puff pastry

Ingredients

Pastry Cream (Crème Pâtissière) - 1/2 cup milk - 1 teaspoon vanilla extract - 2 egg yolks - 1/4 cup sugar - 1 tablespoon cornstarch - 1.5 ounces (40 grams) butter

Almond Cream (Crème d'Amande) - 4 ounces (110 grams) softened butter - 1/2 cup powdered sugar - 1/4 cup almond flour - 1 teaspoon cornstarch - 1 egg

Other Ingredients - 1 sheet of puff pastry - 1 egg for egg wash - 1 tablespoon water - 1 tablespoon honey

Instructions

  1. Make the Pastry Cream:
  2. Heat the milk in a saucepan over low heat with vanilla extract.
  3. In a separate bowl, whisk together the egg yolks, sugar, and cornstarch until light and fluffy.
  4. Slowly whisk in the warm milk into the egg yolk mixture, passing through a fine mesh sieve.
  5. Return the mixture to the saucepan and cook over medium heat, stirring constantly, until thickened.
  6. Remove from heat and whisk in the butter.
  7. Strain the pastry cream through a fine mesh sieve to remove any lumps.

  8. Let cool at room temperature.

  9. Make the Almond Cream:

  10. In a bowl, cream together the softened butter and powdered sugar until light and fluffy.
  11. Gradually add the almond flour, cornstarch, and egg, mixing gently with a spatula.

  12. Fold in the cooled pastry cream until well combined.

  13. Assemble the Cake:

  14. Preheat oven to 400°F (220°C).
  15. Roll out the puff pastry sheet into a rectangle.
  16. Cut the rectangle in half lengthwise.
  17. Brush the edges of one rectangle with egg wash.
  18. Spread a generous layer of the almond cream over the bottom rectangle, leaving a small border around the edges.
  19. Carefully place the second rectangle on top of the first, making sure the edges are sealed.
  20. Press the edges together with a fork to create a tight seal.
  21. Brush the top of the cake with egg wash.
  22. Use a fork to create a decorative pattern on the top.

  23. Refrigerate for 15 minutes.

  24. Bake the Cake:

  25. Bake for 10 minutes at 400°F (220°C).

  26. Reduce oven temperature to 340°F (170°C) and bake for an additional 20 minutes.

  27. Glaze the Cake:

  28. In a small saucepan, combine the honey and hot water.
  29. Heat until the honey is melted and smooth.
  30. Brush the glaze over the top of the cake.
  31. Let cool for 15 minutes before slicing and serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vTSdsoEYjMI

almond_cream.txt - Almond Cream

Objectives

  • Learn how to make almond cream, a versatile pastry filling
  • Discover the importance of room temperature ingredients for successful almond cream
  • Explore various applications of almond cream in pastries, from tarts to biscuits

Ingredients

  • 100 grams unsalted butter, softened
  • 100 grams ground almonds
  • 100 grams confectioners' sugar
  • 2 eggs (50 grams each)
  • 1 teaspoon vanilla extract
  • 1 drop bitter almond extract
  • 15 grams all-purpose flour (optional)
  • Pears, for tart filling (optional)
  • Apricots, for tartlets (optional)
  • Glaze (e.g., maple syrup)

Instructions

  1. Soften the butter until it is very soft and spreadable.
  2. Cream the softened butter with the confectioners' sugar until light and fluffy.
  3. Gradually add the eggs, whisking well after each addition, to ensure proper emulsification.
  4. Incorporate the ground almonds, vanilla extract, and bitter almond extract.
  5. Fold in the flour (optional) for a smoother consistency.
  6. Transfer the almond cream to a piping bag and pipe it into your desired pastry base.
  7. Arrange your chosen fruit filling (e.g., pears, apricots) on top of the almond cream.
  8. Bake at 200°C (396°F) for 20-40 minutes, depending on the size and type of pastry.
  9. Once cooked, glaze the pastries with maple syrup or your preferred glaze.
  10. Allow the pastries to cool before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=P6x_oWJM9Rc

alumet_of_homage.txt - Alumet of Homage (Cheesy Matchsticks)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple French aperitif snack called Alumet of Homage
  • Understand the importance of using pre-made puff pastry
  • Discover a simple cheese sauce recipe that can be used for other dishes

Ingredients

  • 1 sheet of pre-made puff pastry (enough for 6 pockets)
  • 1/2 cup butter
  • 1/4 cup flour
  • 1 cup milk
  • 1 egg yolk
  • 1/2 cup grated cheese (Cheddar, Gruyère, or other)
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Nutmeg
  • Cayenne pepper (optional)

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 230 degrees Celsius (450 degrees Fahrenheit).
  2. Divide the puff pastry sheet into 6 equal rectangles.
  3. Make a border around each rectangle with water to prevent sauce from leaking.
  4. In a saucepan, melt butter over low heat.
  5. Whisk in flour and cook for 3 minutes.
  6. Gradually whisk in half of the milk until a paste forms.
  7. Increase heat to medium and whisk until the sauce thickens.
  8. Remove from heat and stir in the cheese until melted.
  9. Stir in the egg yolk.
  10. Season the sauce with salt, pepper, nutmeg, and cayenne pepper (optional).
  11. Transfer the sauce to a piping bag with a straight nozzle.
  12. Pipe a small amount of sauce into the center of each puff pastry rectangle.
  13. Top with grated cheese strips.
  14. Place another puff pastry rectangle on top of each filled rectangle.
  15. Trim the edges with a sharp blade.
  16. Cut a small chimney in the top of each pocket to allow steam to escape.
  17. Brush with egg wash (optional).
  18. Reduce oven temperature to 200 degrees Celsius (400 degrees Fahrenheit).
  19. Bake for 25 minutes.
  20. Serve warm.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=-KiC52nHAjk

anisee_cream_sauce.txt - Anisee Cream Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn to make a traditional French cream sauce with anise flavor.
  • Understand the importance of using fresh fennel and pastis for optimal flavor.
  • Master the technique of using a vegetable mill for a smooth, creamy sauce.

Ingredients

  • 1 fennel bulb
  • 1 tablespoon rock salt
  • 4 eggs
  • 1/2 lemon
  • 1 tablespoon olive oil
  • 1 teaspoon Dijon mustard
  • 1/2 teaspoon pastis
  • 1 cup heavy cream
  • Butter lettuce (for garnish)
  • Dill (for garnish)
  • Salt and pepper to taste

Instructions

  1. Bring a large pot of water to a boil. Add 1 tablespoon of rock salt to the water.
  2. While the water is heating, prepare the fennel by trimming the outer leaves and cutting the bulb in half.
  3. Place the fennel halves in the boiling water and cook for 25-30 minutes, or until very soft.
  4. Meanwhile, bring another pot of water to a boil.
  5. Add the eggs to the boiling water and cook for 10 minutes.
  6. Immediately after cooking, transfer the eggs to a bowl of ice water to cool and make peeling easier.
  7. Drain the fennel and place it on a kitchen towel to absorb excess moisture.
  8. Press the fennel to extract as much water as possible.
  9. Once the fennel has cooled, use a vegetable mill to puree the fennel and hard-boiled eggs.
  10. Add 1 teaspoon of Dijon mustard, a pinch of salt, and a good grind of black pepper to the fennel and egg puree.
  11. Slowly whisk in the olive oil until the sauce becomes creamy.
  12. Add a squeeze of lemon juice to the sauce to brighten the flavor and prevent oxidation.
  13. Place the sauce in the refrigerator to chill.
  14. In a chilled bowl, whisk the heavy cream and pastis together until the cream thickens.
  15. Gently fold the whipped cream into the chilled fennel puree.
  16. Taste the sauce and adjust the seasoning as needed.
  17. To plate, arrange the sauce in the center of a plate, crossing the plate.
  18. Place the fish on the plate, crossing the sauce.
  19. Garnish with butter lettuce, dill, and a drizzle of olive oil and lemon juice.
  20. Serve chilled.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LR_8QGZRiro

apple_hunger_timer.txt - Apple Hunger Timer

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple, delicious apple-based dessert.
  • Explore a new recipe for Thanksgiving.
  • Understand the importance of resting batter for a better texture.

Ingredients

  • 200 grams of plain flour
  • 100 grams of granulated sugar
  • 2 tablespoons of oil
  • a pinch of salt
  • 3 apples
  • 2 eggs
  • 250 ml of full cream milk
  • apple liqueur (optional)

Instructions

  1. In a bowl, beat 2 eggs and 50 grams of sugar together.
  2. Add a pinch of salt and then gradually add the flour, mixing gently until a paste forms.
  3. Incorporate half of the oil into the mixture.
  4. Slowly add the milk, whisking continuously to prevent clumps.
  5. Continue adding milk until a smooth batter is achieved.
  6. Optional: add a splash of apple liqueur to the batter.
  7. Cover the batter and let it rest for 2 hours.
  8. After 2 hours, grate the apples using a food processor or cut them into small cubes.
  9. Gently fold the grated apples into the rested batter.
  10. Heat a pan over very low heat and melt a small amount of butter.
  11. Pour the batter into the pan, creating a thick pancake.
  12. Cook the pancake for 12-15 minutes until the bottom is hardened.
  13. Carefully flip the pancake and cook for another 5 minutes.
  14. Repeat flipping every 5 minutes until the pancake is fully cooked.
  15. Serve the pancake with a sprinkle of sugar and a dollop of cream, if desired.
  16. Optionally, you can create a second layer of pancake for a thicker, more cake-like texture.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=XlwmwyYpLjo

apple_recipes.txt - 3 Apple Recipes: Stewed, Compote & Pockets

Objectives

  • Explore three different ways to cook apples: stewed, compote, and pockets.
  • Learn how to create a delicious stewed apple recipe with no added sugar.
  • Discover how to make a smooth apple compote for use in other recipes.
  • Master the art of baking apple pockets using puff pastry.

Ingredients

Stewed Apples: - Apples (pink lady or royal gala) - 1-2 tablespoons of water

Apple Compote: - Stewed apples - 2-3 tablespoons of water - 2-3 tablespoons of sugar

Apple Pockets: - Pre-made puff pastry - Apple compote - 1 egg - 1 tablespoon of water - Cookie cutters

Instructions

  1. Prepare the apples:
  2. Use an apple corer to remove the core of the apples.
  3. Peel the apples and cut them into quarters.
  4. Stew the apples:
  5. Place the apple quarters in a saucepan, ensuring they are not stacked on top of each other.
  6. Add 1-2 tablespoons of water to the pan.
  7. Cover the pan with a lid and cook over low heat for 15 minutes.
  8. Monitor the apples during cooking, adding more water if needed to prevent burning.
  9. Make the apple compote:
  10. Once the apples are stewed, add 2-3 tablespoons of water and 2-3 tablespoons of sugar to the pan.
  11. Cook over low heat for 10 minutes, stirring occasionally.
  12. Continue cooking until the apples are soft and have transformed into a puree.
  13. If necessary, use a potato masher or a stick blender to help break down the apples.
  14. Prepare the apple pockets:
  15. Preheat the oven to 200 degrees Celsius (400 degrees Fahrenheit).
  16. Create an egg wash by whisking together 1 egg and 1 tablespoon of water.
  17. Unroll the puff pastry sheet and use a cookie cutter to cut out circles.
  18. Place 6 circles on a baking sheet.
  19. Spoon a tablespoon of apple compote onto each circle.
  20. Place the remaining 6 circles on top, egg wash side down.
  21. Gently press the edges of the circles together to seal the pockets.
  22. Use a cookie cutter to further seal the edges.
  23. Refrigerate the pockets for 5-10 minutes.
  24. Bake the apple pockets:
  25. Once chilled, use a smaller cookie cutter to press down on the edges of the pockets to ensure a tight seal.
  26. Brush the tops of the pockets with egg wash.
  27. If desired, use a fork to create decorative patterns on the top.
  28. Refrigerate the pockets for another 10 minutes.
  29. Place the pockets on a baking sheet and use a cookie cutter or pegs to prevent them from rising too high.
  30. Bake in the preheated oven for 20 minutes.
  31. Serve and enjoy:
  32. Allow the apple pockets to cool slightly before serving.
  33. If desired, add additional apple compote to the pockets.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=jZQbjEcO6hI

apricot_almond_tart.txt - Apricot Almond Tart

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious and easy apricot almond tart.
  • Understand the importance of using room temperature ingredients for almond cream.
  • Discover a zero-waste pastry technique for rectangle-shaped tarts.

Ingredients

  • 100 grams (3.5 oz) sugar
  • 100 grams (3.5 oz) ground almonds
  • 100 grams (3.5 oz) butter, softened
  • 80 grams (2.8 oz) eggs
  • 1 tablespoon flour
  • Apricots (fresh or in syrup)
  • Fine sugar
  • 3 tablespoons apricot jam
  • 2-3 teaspoons hot water

Instructions

  1. Soften the butter: If necessary, microwave the butter for a few seconds to soften it until it can be creamed with a spatula.
  2. Combine butter and sugar: In a medium bowl, cream together the softened butter and sugar until light and fluffy.
  3. Add eggs gradually: Slowly incorporate the beaten eggs into the butter-sugar mixture, mixing well after each addition.
  4. Incorporate almonds: Gently fold in the ground almonds until evenly distributed.
  5. Add flour: Stir in the tablespoon of flour to help with the almond cream's cooking.
  6. Refrigerate almond cream: Cover the bowl and place it in the refrigerator to chill while you prepare the apricots and pastry.
  7. Prepare apricots: If using fresh apricots, quarter them. If using apricots in syrup, drain them and quarter them.
  8. Prepare pastry: Unroll the puff pastry sheet on a baking sheet lined with parchment paper.
  9. Form the tart: Fold the edges of the pastry to create a rectangle-shaped tart.
  10. Spread almond cream: Spoon the chilled almond cream into the center of the pastry, spreading it evenly.
  11. Arrange apricots: Arrange the apricot quarters on top of the almond cream, leaving some space for the cream to puff up.
  12. Sprinkle sugar: Sprinkle fine sugar over the apricots and along the edges of the pastry.
  13. Bake: Bake the tart in a preheated oven at 350°F (175°C) for 35 minutes, or until the apricot is caramelized and the almond cream is puffed and cooked.
  14. Make apricot glaze: In a small bowl, mix the apricot jam with hot water until syrupy.
  15. Glaze the tart: Brush the warm apricot glaze over the baked tart to create a shiny finish.
  16. Slice and serve: Once cooled, slice the tart and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6wsk4qGUXuA

artichoke_barigoule.txt - Artichokes Barigoule

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare artichokes for cooking
  • Master a classic French artichoke recipe
  • Understand the importance of freshness in artichoke dishes

Ingredients

  • 4-5 artichokes
  • 1/2 lemon
  • 1 tablespoon olive oil
  • 1/2 onion, thinly sliced
  • 1 carrot, thinly sliced
  • 2 garlic cloves, bruised
  • 1 sprig thyme
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 1/4 cup white wine
  • 1/4 cup water
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • 1 tablespoon chopped fresh parsley
  • 1 tablespoon chopped fresh basil
  • 1 tablespoon chopped fresh garlic

Instructions

  1. Fill a bowl with water and add the juice of half a lemon.
  2. Trim the stems of the artichokes, removing the tough outer layer with a peeler.
  3. Pluck off the outer leaves of the artichokes, stopping when the leaves become pale and expose the inner flower.
  4. Using a spoon, carefully remove the hairy "choke" from the center of each artichoke.
  5. Cut the artichokes in half lengthwise.
  6. Heat the olive oil in a sauté pan over medium heat.
  7. Add the onion and carrot and cook for 1-2 minutes, until softened.
  8. Add the artichoke halves, thyme, bay leaf, garlic, salt, and pepper to the pan.
  9. Pour in the white wine and water, making sure the artichokes are barely covered with liquid.
  10. Bring to a simmer, cover, and cook for 15 minutes.
  11. Remove the lid and cook for an additional 10 minutes on high heat, reducing the liquid to a syrupy consistency.
  12. Turn off the heat and stir in the chopped parsley, basil, and garlic.
  13. Serve warm or cold.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=wneNc5_JMhE

asparagus_sauce_florian.txt - Asparagus with Sauce Florian

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare asparagus with a delicate Sauce Florian
  • Master the technique of peeling and tying asparagus
  • Discover the simplicity of a one-pot sauce recipe

Ingredients

  • 1 bunch white asparagus
  • 1 bunch green asparagus
  • 1 egg yolk
  • 2 tablespoons lemon juice
  • 1/2 cup cold butter, cubed
  • 1/4 cup heavy whipping cream
  • Salt
  • Black pepper
  • Cayenne pepper (optional)

Instructions

  1. Fill a large pot with water and add 12 grams of salt per liter. Bring to a boil.
  2. While the water is heating, peel the asparagus.
  3. Hold the asparagus flat on a chopping board.
  4. Use a vegetable peeler to remove a thin layer of skin from the asparagus, starting from the bottom and working towards the head.
  5. Tie the asparagus together in bunches using kitchen twine.
  6. Make three turns in front and three turns in the back.
  7. Trim the ends of the asparagus so that they are all at the same height.
  8. Plunge the white asparagus into the boiling water. Cook for 20 minutes.
  9. After 5 minutes, add the green asparagus to the pot.
  10. Add a few drops of lemon juice to the water to prevent discoloration.
  11. After 20 minutes, remove the asparagus from the pot and immediately plunge them into a bowl of ice water to stop the cooking process.
  12. Drain the asparagus and pat them dry with a paper towel.
  13. Place the asparagus in the refrigerator to cool while you make the sauce.
  14. To make the sauce, place a bowl over a pot of simmering water (double boiler).
  15. Add the heavy cream and egg yolk to the bowl and whisk until foamy.
  16. Gradually add the cold butter cubes, whisking constantly until the sauce thickens.
  17. Add a few drops of lemon juice, black pepper, and a pinch of cayenne pepper (optional).
  18. Serve the sauce warm over the chilled asparagus.
  19. Garnish with radishes and a sprinkle of cayenne pepper (optional).

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=RM506j3tgY4

aubergine_caviar.txt - Aubergine Caviar

Objectives

  • Learn how to properly cook an aubergine in the oven
  • Make a simple aubergine dip called Aubergine Caviar
  • Understand the importance of cooking onions properly for the dip

Ingredients

  • 1 aubergine
  • 2-3 tablespoons of olive oil
  • 1 small onion, thinly diced
  • 2 cloves of garlic, minced
  • 1 teaspoon of mustard
  • 1 tablespoon of chopped tomato
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • 1/4 teaspoon of smoked paprika (optional)
  • Lemon juice (optional)

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 200 degrees Celsius (400 degrees Fahrenheit).
  2. Cut the aubergine in half lengthwise.
  3. Make shallow incisions in the flesh of the aubergine with a small knife.
  4. Brush the aubergine halves with olive oil, salt, and pepper.
  5. Place the aubergine halves skin side up on a baking sheet.
  6. Place the baking sheet on the top shelf of the oven, about 5 centimeters (2 inches) from the grill.
  7. Grill for 20-25 minutes, or until the aubergine is cooked through and the skin is slightly charred.
  8. While the aubergine is grilling, prepare the onion and garlic mixture.
  9. Heat a tablespoon of olive oil in a sauté pan over medium heat.
  10. Add the onion and garlic to the pan and cook for 10-15 minutes, or until softened and translucent.
  11. Add the chopped tomato, salt, and pepper to the pan and mix well.
  12. Remove the aubergine from the oven and let it cool.
  13. Once the aubergine is cool enough to handle, scoop out the flesh and place it in a bowl.
  14. Add the onion and garlic mixture, mustard, lemon juice (optional), smoked paprika (optional), and salt and pepper to the bowl.
  15. Mix all the ingredients together until well combined.
  16. Add olive oil gradually, mixing until the desired consistency is reached.
  17. Refrigerate the aubergine caviar for at least 2 hours before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=JtvRIKmpgLM

baby_cherry_cloti.txt - Baby Cherry Cloti

Objectives

  • Learn to make a small version of the classic French dessert, Cherry Cloti.
  • Discover how to marinate cherries in cherry liquor and sugar.
  • Master the art of creating a smooth and creamy butter base for the Cloti.

Ingredients

  • 450g black cherries, pitted
  • 3 tbsp castor sugar
  • 3 tbsp cherry liquor (brandy cherry liquor)
  • 2 eggs
  • 1 egg yolk
  • 1 vanilla bean
  • 1/2 cup double cream
  • 1/4 cup full cream milk
  • 1 tbsp melted unsalted butter
  • 1 tbsp chestnut butter, melted
  • 1 tbsp flour

Instructions

  1. Pit the black cherries and place them in a bowl.
  2. Add 3 tablespoons of castor sugar and 3 tablespoons of cherry liquor to the cherries.
  3. Stir well to combine and let marinate in the refrigerator for 2 hours.
  4. In a separate bowl, whisk together 2 eggs and 1 egg yolk.
  5. Add the sugar, vanilla bean, double cream, and full cream milk to the egg mixture and whisk until smooth.
  6. Gently melt 1 tablespoon of unsalted butter and add it to the batter.
  7. Melt 1 tablespoon of chestnut butter until it reaches a chestnut color and add it to the batter.
  8. Stir in 1 tablespoon of flour to thicken the batter.
  9. Pass the batter through a sieve to remove any lumps.
  10. Preheat oven to 180°C (350°F).
  11. Generously butter small individual dishes.
  12. Sprinkle sugar over the buttered dishes.
  13. Add the marinated cherries to the dishes.
  14. Pour the batter over the cherries, ensuring to coat the sides of the dishes.
  15. Bake for 30 minutes at 180°C (350°F).
  16. Once cooked, allow the Baby Cherry Cloti to cool slightly before serving.
  17. Sprinkle with icing sugar, if desired.
  18. Serve warm with a spoon.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=BcO-mgsPgU0

bacon_cheese_profiteroles.txt - Bacon and Cheese Profiteroles

Objectives

  • Learn to make savory cheese puffs filled with bacon and cheese sauce.
  • Understand the importance of using milk for a softer, less-crack prone choux pastry.
  • Master the technique of incorporating eggs into choux pastry.

Ingredients

Choux Pastry - 250 ml milk - 100 g butter - Pinch of salt - Pinch of nutmeg - 200 g flour - 2 eggs - 40 g cream cheese

Cheese Sauce - 20 g butter - 20 g flour - 200 ml cold milk - 40 g cheese (cheddar or French comté) - 1 egg yolk

Other - Bacon - Roham (optional) - Porket (optional)

Instructions

  1. Combine milk, butter, salt, and nutmeg in a saucepan.
  2. Heat over medium heat, stirring until the butter melts and the milk reaches a boil.
  3. Reduce heat to low and add all the flour at once, stirring vigorously until a smooth paste forms.
  4. Continue cooking over low heat, stirring constantly, until the paste dries slightly and a film forms on the bottom of the pan.
  5. Remove from heat and let cool slightly.
  6. Beat eggs together and gradually add to the cooled paste, incorporating each addition thoroughly. The mix will initially appear lumpy, but it will smooth out as you continue mixing.
  7. Fold in the cream cheese.
  8. Preheat oven to 200°C (400°F).
  9. Pipe choux pastry onto a baking sheet, flattening the tops slightly.
  10. Brush the tops with a mixture of egg and milk.
  11. Bake for 25 minutes, then leave the oven door slightly ajar for 5-10 minutes to allow the choux to dry further.
  12. While the choux is baking, prepare the cheese sauce.
  13. Melt the butter in a saucepan over low heat.
  14. Add the flour and cook, stirring constantly, until the mixture turns white.
  15. Gradually whisk in the cold milk until the sauce thickens.
  16. Cook for 5 minutes over low heat, stirring constantly, to remove the raw flour taste.
  17. Remove from heat and let cool slightly.
  18. Stir in the cheese until melted.
  19. Whisk in the egg yolk.
  20. Fry bacon until crisp and drain on paper towels to remove excess fat.
  21. Transfer the cheese sauce to a piping bag.
  22. Fill the cooled choux pastry with cheese sauce using the piping bag.
  23. Add a piece of bacon or roham to each profiterole.
  24. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=GPCBPHVGP1Q

bacon_eggs_custard.txt - Bacon and Eggs Custard in a Pot

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a savory custard with bacon and cheese.
  • Discover a unique way to cook bacon and eggs in a pot.
  • Explore the versatility of this recipe with different toppings.

Ingredients

  • 2 Eggs (for 2 servings)
  • 1/2 cup Heavy Cream
  • 1/4 cup Milk
  • 2 slices Bacon
  • 1/4 cup Grated Cheese (any kind you like)
  • Salt and Pepper to taste
  • Butter for greasing ramekins

Instructions

  1. Cook the bacon in a pan over medium heat until crispy.
  2. Drain the bacon on paper towels, reserving some of the bacon fat in the pan.
  3. Grate the cheese to your desired size.
  4. Beat the eggs in a bowl until light and frothy.
  5. Combine the eggs, cream, milk, salt, pepper, bacon, and cheese in a bowl.
  6. Grease two ramekins with butter.
  7. Pour the custard mixture into the ramekins, filling them about 3/4 full.
  8. Prepare a bain-marie by filling a baking dish with boiling water.
  9. Place the ramekins in the baking dish, ensuring the water level reaches about halfway up the sides of the ramekins.
  10. Bake in a preheated oven at 200 degrees Celsius (400 degrees Fahrenheit) for 15 minutes.
  11. Carefully remove the ramekins from the bain-marie and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_mzn5Oz3D0k

bacon_hoof.txt - Bacon Hoof

Objectives

  • Learn the history and origin of the "Bacon Hoof" dish.
  • Understand the importance of marinating the meat for 24 hours.
  • Learn how to assemble and cook the dish using a traditional earthenware pot.

Ingredients

  • 1 kg potatoes, sliced thick
  • 1 onion, sliced
  • 3 types of meat (pork shoulder, lamb shoulder, beef chuck) cut in large pieces
  • 1 onion, sliced
  • 2 bay leaves
  • 1 clove garlic
  • juniper berries
  • black pepper
  • salt
  • Alsatian Riesling wine
  • water
  • bread flour
  • water

Instructions

  1. Marinate the meat for 24 hours.
  2. Combine pork shoulder, lamb shoulder, beef chuck, 1 onion, juniper berries, black pepper, salt, and garlic in a large bowl.
  3. Pour in enough Alsatian Riesling wine to cover the meat.
  4. Prepare the vegetables.
  5. Peel and slice the potatoes into thick slices.
  6. Reserve the potatoes in water.
  7. Slice the onion.
  8. Assemble the dish in an earthenware pot.
  9. Layer potatoes in the bottom of the pot.
  10. Add a layer of marinated meat, including a bay leaf, some onion, and a bit of garlic.
  11. Add another layer of onion.
  12. Continue layering potatoes, meat, and onion until all ingredients are used.
  13. Pour the marinade over the ingredients.
  14. Top up with a small amount of water.
  15. Seal the pot with bread dough.
  16. Mix bread flour and water to create a dough.
  17. Roll the dough into a long string.
  18. Place the dough around the edge of the pot to create a seal.
  19. Ensure there is a small hole for steam to escape.
  20. Cook the dish in a cold oven.
  21. Place the pot in a cold oven at 150 degrees Celsius (300 degrees Fahrenheit).
  22. Cook for 3 hours.
  23. Break the seal and serve.
  24. Once the dish is cooked, carefully break the seal of the dough.
  25. Serve the dish hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=N_Lqn5zOFLI

bacon_potatoes.txt - Bacon Potatoes

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a simple, comforting side dish of bacon potatoes.
  • Understand the importance of using the right type of potato for the dish.
  • Discover a unique twist on the classic Pomme Banger recipe.

Ingredients

  • 1 kg all-round potatoes, peeled and cut into quarters
  • 1 large onion, sliced
  • 1 slab of bacon, cut into thick lardons
  • 1 tablespoon of lard
  • 250-300 ml chicken stock or dry white wine
  • Salt and pepper to taste

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 180°C.
  2. Melt lard in a saute pan over medium-high heat.
  3. Add sliced onion and cook for 5 minutes, stirring regularly, until translucent.
  4. Remove onions from pan and set aside.
  5. Increase heat to high and add bacon to pan. Cook until bacon is crispy and fat is rendered.
  6. Remove bacon from pan and set aside.
  7. Reduce heat to medium.
  8. Dry potatoes thoroughly and add to pan.
  9. Season potatoes with salt and pepper.
  10. Cook potatoes for a few minutes, stirring occasionally, until they start to color.
  11. Deglaze the pan with chicken stock or white wine.
  12. Add onions and bacon back to the pan and stir to combine.
  13. Transfer pan to oven and bake for 35-40 minutes, or until potatoes are cooked through.
  14. Optional: Broil for 5 minutes to crisp up the potatoes.
  15. Serve immediately.

baguette_flour_types.txt - Baguette: Flour Types Explained

Objectives

  • Understand the difference between various flour types for bread making
  • Learn how flour type impacts the taste and texture of baguettes
  • Explore the French flour classification system (T-number)

Ingredients

  • T55 flour (all-purpose baker style)
  • T65 flour (tradition, two types of flour mix)

Instructions

  1. Prepare two batches of baguette dough, one using T55 flour and the other using T65 flour.
  2. Allow the dough to rest for 30-40 minutes.
  3. Shape the baguettes.
  4. Score the baguettes with three slashes along the sides.
  5. Bake the baguettes in a preheated oven with steam.
  6. Observe the difference in the baguettes' appearance, texture, and taste. The T55 flour baguette will rise higher and have a thinner crust, while the T65 flour baguette will be denser with a more pronounced crust.
  7. Enjoy your baguettes!

baked_apple_caramel_sauce.txt - Baked Apple with Caramel Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare and bake apples for a delicious dessert
  • Master the art of making a rich caramel sauce with Calvados
  • Create a flavorful garnish with candied almonds and pistachios

Ingredients

  • White bread
  • 4-5 apples (Biscotti Baked Apple variety)
  • Pistachios
  • Flaked almonds
  • Icing sugar
  • Castor sugar
  • Plain butter
  • Apple juice
  • Calvados (apple brandy)
  • 1 tablespoon of water
  • 50 grams of sugar
  • Arrowroot (tapioca flour)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the apples:
    • Use a paring knife to flatten the bottom of each apple so it can stand upright.
    • Core each apple, leaving a small portion of the core intact at the top.
  2. Brush and sugar the apples:
    • Melt a small amount of butter in a pan.
    • Brush each apple with the melted butter.
    • Sprinkle castor sugar over the apples and remove any excess.
    • Place the apples on a baking tray.
  3. Bake the apples:
    • Place a small piece of butter on top of each apple.
    • Bake in a standard convection oven at 170 degrees Celsius (338 degrees Fahrenheit) for 35-40 minutes.
    • Monitor the apples while baking to ensure they don't crack or fall apart.
  4. Make the caramel sauce:
    • In a small pan, combine 1 tablespoon of water and 50 grams of sugar.
    • Heat over medium-high heat, stirring until the sugar and water are fully combined.
    • Continue heating until the mixture caramelizes, being careful not to burn it.
    • Add apple juice to the caramel and bring to a boil.
    • Optionally, add 1-2 tablespoons of diced fresh apple to the sauce.
    • Reduce heat to low and add 1 tablespoon of Calvados.
  5. Thicken the caramel sauce:
    • Mix arrowroot (tapioca flour) with a small amount of water.
    • Add the arrowroot mixture to the caramel sauce.
    • Cook for a minute or so, allowing the sauce to thicken.
    • Remove from heat and let cool.
  6. Prepare the garnish:
    • Combine pistachios, flaked almonds, icing sugar, and a small amount of Calvados in a bowl.
    • Toss the mixture to combine.
    • Spread the mixture on a baking tray and toast under the grill for 8-10 minutes, until caramelized.
  7. Assemble and serve:
    • Place a baked apple on a plate.
    • Sprinkle the candied almond and pistachio mixture over the apple.
    • Drizzle caramel sauce over the apple and plate.
    • Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=mCUMiZ7n4Dk

baked_apple_caramel.txt - Baked Apples with Caramel Sauce

Objectives

  • Explore Michelin star chef recipes and their unique qualities.
  • Understand how simple ingredients can be transformed into extraordinary dishes.
  • Learn the key elements that contribute to Michelin star cuisine.

Ingredients

  • 1 apple
  • 1/2 cup of Calvados (apple brandy)
  • 1/2 cup of sugar
  • 1/4 cup of water
  • 1/4 cup of flaked almonds
  • 1/4 cup of pistachios
  • 1 tablespoon of butter

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 350 degrees Fahrenheit.
  2. Select a ripe, firm apple suitable for baking.
  3. Core the apple and carefully cut a small hole in the top.
  4. In a saucepan, combine sugar and water over medium heat.
  5. Stir constantly until the sugar dissolves and the mixture begins to simmer.
  6. Add Calvados (apple brandy) to the simmering sugar mixture.
  7. Continue to cook until the caramel sauce thickens.
  8. Pour a small amount of the caramel sauce into the hollow of the apple.
  9. Place the apple in a baking dish and add a small amount of water to the bottom of the dish.
  10. Bake the apple for 45-60 minutes, or until tender.
  11. While the apple is baking, toast the flaked almonds and pistachios in a dry skillet until fragrant.
  12. Once the apple is cooked, carefully remove it from the oven and let it cool slightly.
  13. Garnish the baked apple with the toasted almonds, pistachios, and additional caramel sauce.
  14. Serve the baked apple warm.

baked_quinces.txt - Baked Quinces

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare and bake quinces in the oven.
  • Discover the unique flavor profile of quinces, resembling apple and passion fruit.
  • Create a delicious and easy dessert using readily available ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 2 quinces
  • Granulated white sugar
  • Cream
  • Apricot nectar

Instructions

  1. Clean the quinces by removing the fur with a towel.
  2. Core the quinces using an apple corer, leaving a cavity in the center.
  3. Remove the seeds from the core using a spoon.
  4. Peel the quinces using a peeler.
  5. Roll the quinces in granulated sugar to coat them.
  6. Mix cream and sugar in a bowl.
  7. Fill the cavities of the quinces with the cream and sugar mixture.
  8. Pour half of the apricot nectar into a baking dish.
  9. Place the quinces in the baking dish.
  10. Bake in a preheated oven at 200°C (400°F) for 45 minutes to 1 hour, basting with the apricot nectar every 15-20 minutes.
  11. Once the quinces are cooked, remove them from the oven and pour the remaining apricot nectar into the baking dish.
  12. Place the quinces on a plate and add a knob of butter to the baking dish.
  13. Return the baking dish to the oven to melt the butter and create a caramel glaze.
  14. Pour the caramel glaze over the quinces.
  15. Serve and enjoy!

basque_style_terrine.txt - Basque Style Terrine

Objectives

  • Learn to make a Basque-style terrine using pork belly, pork scotch, and black cherry jam.
  • Discover the unique flavors and spices of Basque cuisine.
  • Understand the importance of using fresh ingredients for optimal flavor.

Ingredients

  • 1 kg pork belly, minced
  • 500 g pork scotch, cut into large cubes
  • 1 tablespoon black cherry jam
  • 1 teaspoon Piment d'Espelette (Basque chili pepper)
  • 1 teaspoon spice mix (optional)
  • 1 egg
  • 1 tablespoon cream
  • Salt and pepper to taste

Instructions

  1. In a bowl, combine the minced pork belly, salt, pepper, and spice mix.
  2. Mix well for 2-3 minutes using a stand mixer or by hand.
  3. Add the egg and cream to the pork belly mixture and continue mixing until well combined.
  4. Add the pork scotch cubes, Piment d'Espelette, and black cherry jam to the mixture.
  5. Mix everything together for 2-4 minutes on low speed.
  6. Transfer the mixture to a terrine mold, pressing down firmly to ensure it is packed tightly.
  7. Cover the terrine with a piece of parchment paper and place a weight on top.
  8. Refrigerate the terrine for at least 2 hours or overnight.
  9. Preheat the oven to 80°C (175°F).
  10. Place the terrine in the oven and cook for 1-2 hours until the internal temperature reaches 80°C (175°F).
  11. Let the terrine cool completely before slicing and serving.

bavaroise_creme.txt - Bavarian Cream

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic Bavarian cream dessert
  • Understand the importance of using high-quality ingredients
  • Discover the proper techniques for achieving a smooth and creamy texture

Ingredients

  • 1 cup heavy cream
  • 1/2 cup milk
  • 1/4 cup sugar
  • 2 tablespoons cornstarch
  • 1/4 teaspoon vanilla extract
  • 1/4 cup cold water
  • 1 packet (1/4 ounce) unflavored gelatin
  • 1/2 cup whipped cream (for topping)
  • Fresh berries (for garnish)

Instructions

  1. In a saucepan, combine the heavy cream, milk, and sugar.
  2. Heat over medium heat, stirring constantly, until the sugar dissolves and the mixture comes to a simmer.
  3. In a small bowl, whisk together the cornstarch and 1/4 cup cold water until smooth.
  4. Gradually whisk the cornstarch mixture into the simmering cream mixture.
  5. Continue to cook, stirring constantly, until the mixture thickens.
  6. Remove from heat and stir in the vanilla extract.
  7. In a small bowl, sprinkle the gelatin over the remaining 1/4 cup cold water.
  8. Let stand for 5 minutes, then stir until the gelatin is dissolved.
  9. Gradually whisk the gelatin mixture into the hot cream mixture.
  10. Pour the mixture into a bowl and cover with plastic wrap, pressing the wrap directly onto theblocked: candidate: FinishReasonRecitation

bbq_skewers.txt - Barbecue Skewers

Objectives

  • Recreate a barbecue experience at home using a cast iron grill
  • Tenderize meat with a quick marinade
  • Pre-cook vegetables to make them tender
  • Achieve barbecue-like marks on the meat

Ingredients

  • 1 filet mignon (or beef tenderloin)
  • 1 bell pepper (red or green)
  • 1-2 handfuls of cherry tomatoes
  • 1 handful of mushrooms
  • 1 white onion
  • 3 tablespoons tarragon
  • 3 tablespoons parsley
  • 3 tablespoons chives
  • 100 ml grapeseed oil
  • Salt & pepper
  • Olive oil

Instructions

  1. Combine tarragon, parsley, chives, and grapeseed oil in a food processor. Blend until well combined.
  2. Cut the filet mignon into 1-inch pieces.
  3. Place the meat in a bowl and add the herb oil, salt, and pepper. Marinate for 30 minutes.
  4. Cut the bell pepper into 1.5-inch squares.
  5. Pan-fry the mushrooms in a little olive oil until softened.
  6. Sauté the bell pepper, onion, and mushrooms in a saute pan with a little olive oil until softened (about 10 minutes).
  7. Assemble the skewers by alternating meat, bell pepper, cherry tomatoes, and mushrooms.
  8. Preheat the cast iron grill pan over medium-high heat for 5-10 minutes.
  9. Place the skewers on the hot grill pan and cook for 7-8 minutes, ensuring the flat side of the skewers touches the grill to create marks.
  10. Cook for an additional 2 minutes on each side to ensure the meat is cooked to your liking.
  11. Serve immediately.

beef_bourguignon_one_pot.txt - Beef Bourguignon (One-Pot)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple, one-pot Beef Bourguignon
  • Understand the key ingredients and techniques for a delicious result
  • Explore the history of the dish and its traditional methods

Ingredients

  • 1 tablespoon oil (sunflower or grapeseed)
  • 1 Chuck steak (cut into smaller chunks)
  • 1-2 beef short ribs (cut in half)
  • 1 piece bacon rind
  • 1 piece bacon (soaked in Madeira wine for 30 minutes)
  • 1/2 cup pearl onions (peeled)
  • 1/2 cup mushrooms (quartered)
  • 2 cloves garlic (crushed)
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 1 piece leek leaf
  • 1 sprig parsley
  • 1 piece celery
  • 1 teaspoon tomato paste
  • 1 tablespoon toasted flour
  • 1 bottle red wine
  • Water (to cover meat)
  • Salt and pepper (to taste)

Instructions

  1. Season the Chuck steak and short ribs with salt and pepper.
  2. Heat oil in a large cast iron pot over high heat.
  3. Sear the meat on all sides in batches until nicely browned.
  4. Remove the meat and set aside.
  5. Add the mushrooms and onions to the pot and cook until slightly colored.
  6. Remove the mushrooms and onions and set aside.
  7. Add the bacon to the pot and cook until slightly colored.
  8. Remove the bacon and set aside.
  9. Return the meat to the pot.
  10. Stir in the tomato paste and cook until slightly browned.
  11. Add the Madeira wine and cook until almost dry.
  12. Stir in the toasted flour and mix well.
  13. Return the mushrooms, onions, and bacon to the pot.
  14. Pour in the red wine and enough water to cover the meat.
  15. Add the bacon rind, bouquet garni, and garlic to the pot.
  16. Bring the mixture to a light boil, skimming off any impurities that float to the surface.
  17. Preheat oven to 160 degrees Celsius (320 degrees Fahrenheit).
  18. Transfer the pot to the oven and cook for 2.5-3 hours, or until the meat is tender and falls apart easily.
  19. Serve the Beef Bourguignon with carrots and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=KnNoGeNoW6o

beef_broth.txt - Beef Broth

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a delicious and flavorful beef broth from scratch.
  • Understand the importance of roasting bones for a richer flavor.
  • Learn how to properly simmer the broth for optimal results.

Ingredients

1 kilo of bone 1 Celery Stock 1 carrot 1 white onion 1 mix of salt and pepper 3 or 4 garlic cloves 1 homemade handmade buuk Garney Vegetable stock

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 200°C (400°F).
  2. Place bones in a roasting tray and roast for 15 minutes or more, turning occasionally.
  3. While bones are roasting, prepare garnish:
    • Peel and remove germ from garlic cloves.
    • Roughly chop carrots, onion, and celery.
  4. Remove bones from oven and add prepared garnish to the roasting tray.
  5. Return to oven for 5-10 minutes to sweat vegetables.
  6. Remove bones and vegetables from oven and transfer to a stock pot.
  7. Add vegetable stock and any juices from the roasting tray.
  8. Bring to a boil over high heat.
  9. Add bouq garni and garlic cloves.
  10. Reduce heat to a simmer and cook for 3-4 hours.
  11. Remove bones and vegetables from the broth and strain through a sieve.
  12. Season to taste.
  13. Serve with spring onions and coriander for garnish.

beef_carrot_onion_stew.txt - Beef, Carrot, and Onion Stew

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French beef, carrot, and onion stew.
  • Master the technique of slow cooking for rich flavors.
  • Understand the importance of balancing sweet and savory flavors in a stew.

Ingredients

  • 6 carrots, sliced 1 cm thick
  • 3 onions, sliced
  • 1 tbsp fresh shallots, finely chopped
  • 1 tbsp tomato paste
  • 20 cm dry white wine (Pinot Grigio or Pinot Gris)
  • 800 g beef, chopped (for stews)
  • Bay leaves
  • Thyme sprigs
  • Parsley sprigs
  • 1 tbsp flour
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Oil

Instructions

  1. Heat a pan with oil over medium-high heat.
  2. Add the onions and brown them lightly.
  3. Add the beef and cook until it browns nicely.
  4. Sprinkle in the flour and mix well to thicken the sauce.
  5. Add 20 cm of water and 20 cm of white wine.
  6. Add the tomato paste, 1 bay leaf, thyme sprigs, and 2 cloves of garlic.
  7. Bring to a simmer, cover, and cook for 1 hour.
  8. After 1 hour, add the carrots and mix well.
  9. Add a little water if the stew seems dry.
  10. Add parsley and shallots.
  11. Season with salt and pepper.
  12. Cover and cook for another hour.
  13. Serve hot, garnished with fresh parsley.

beef_stew_orange_thyme.txt - Beef Stew with Orange and Thyme

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple, flavorful French-style beef stew.
  • Understand the importance of browning meat and sweating vegetables.
  • Master the technique of deglazing and creating a rich sauce.

Ingredients

  • 1 beef shank
  • 1 parsnip, roughly chopped
  • 1 carrot, roughly chopped
  • 1 onion, chopped
  • 2 tablespoons tomato paste
  • 4-5 cloves
  • 1 orange, peel only
  • 2-3 tablespoons honey
  • 1 tablespoon flour
  • Salt and pepper
  • Red wine stock
  • Red wine
  • Oil
  • Butter (optional)

Instructions

  1. Season the beef shank with salt and pepper.
  2. Lightly dust the beef shank with flour.
  3. Heat 2 tablespoons of oil in a cast iron pot over medium-high heat.
  4. Brown the beef shank on all sides, about 2-3 minutes per side.
  5. Remove the browned beef shank from the pot and set aside.
  6. Add chopped garlic, onion, carrot, and parsnip to the pot.
  7. Sweat the vegetables over low heat for 2-3 minutes, adding a little oil or butter if needed.
  8. Stir in the tomato paste and cook for 1 minute.
  9. Deglaze the pot with red wine, scraping up any browned bits from the bottom.
  10. Add red wine stock to the pot.
  11. Bring the mixture to a simmer.
  12. Add thyme, cloves, orange peel, and honey to the pot.
  13. Stir well to combine.
  14. Return the browned beef shank to the pot.
  15. Cover the pot and simmer over low heat for 1.5-2 hours, or until the meat is tender.
  16. Remove the meat from the pot and shred or slice as desired.
  17. Serve the beef stew with pasta, rice, potatoes, or bread.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=CaZH6K_WkoU

beef_stroganoff.txt - Beef Stroganoff

Objectives

  • Learn how to use a saute pan for cooking.
  • Create a simple and delicious Beef Stroganoff recipe.
  • Understand the importance of proper heat control and pan selection.

Ingredients

  • 1 tablespoon of oil
  • 1 knob of butter
  • 1 onion, thinly sliced
  • 1 package of mushrooms, thinly sliced
  • 1 pound of beef, cut into strips
  • 1 tablespoon of cognac (optional)
  • 1 tablespoon of paprika
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • 1 cup of cream
  • Fresh parsley, for garnish

Instructions

  1. Heat a tablespoon of oil and a knob of butter in a saute pan over medium heat.
  2. Add thinly sliced onions to the pan and saute for 5 minutes, until translucent.
  3. Remove the onions from the pan and set aside.
  4. Add a little more butter to the pan and saute the thinly sliced mushrooms for 3.5 minutes, until the water has evaporated.
  5. Return the onions to the pan and mix well.
  6. Remove the onions and mushrooms from the pan and set aside.
  7. Add a tablespoon of oil to the pan and heat over medium heat.
  8. Add the beef strips to the pan and cook for 2 minutes, until browned.
  9. Return the onions and mushrooms to the pan and mix well.
  10. Add a tablespoon of cognac (optional) and deglaze the pan.
  11. Add a tablespoon of paprika, salt, and pepper to taste.
  12. Pour in the cream and reduce the heat to low.
  13. Simmer for a few minutes, until the sauce has thickened.
  14. Garnish with fresh parsley and serve.

beetroot_preparation.txt - Beetroot Preparation

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare beetroot for cooking.
  • Explore different methods for cooking beetroot.
  • Discover various ways to cut and utilize cooked beetroot.

Ingredients

  • Beetroot

Instructions

  1. Trim off the root end of the beetroot.
  2. Wash the beetroot thoroughly with a brush to remove any dirt.
  3. Choose a cooking method:
    • Boiling: Place beetroot in boiling salted water for 20-25 minutes.
    • Steaming: Steam beetroot until tender, which may take longer than boiling.
    • Oven: Wrap beetroot in foil and bake at 180 degrees Celsius for 25-30 minutes.
  4. Once cooked, peel the beetroot, discarding the skin.
  5. Cut the beetroot into desired shapes:
    • Slices: For salads or other uses.
    • Squares: To create cubes or butternut shapes.
    • Cubes: For salads or other dishes.
  6. Use the beetroot in various ways:
    • Salads: Add sliced or cubed beetroot to salads.
    • Roasted: Roast beetroot with herbs and spices.
    • Pickled: Pickle beetroot for a tangy flavor.
  7. Enjoy your prepared beetroot!

bell_pepper_preparation.txt - Bell Pepper Preparation

Objectives

  • Learn two different methods for preparing bell peppers: cold and warm.
  • Discover the French technique for peeling bell peppers using a peeler.
  • Understand the proper way to cut and remove seeds from both raw and cooked bell peppers.

Ingredients

  • Bell Peppers (capsicum)
  • Water
  • Paper towels
  • Vegetable peeler
  • Utility knife or paring knife
  • Oven (for warm preparation)
  • Plastic wrap (for warm preparation)

Instructions

  1. Wash the bell peppers thoroughly under running water or in a bowl of water.
  2. Dry the bell peppers with a paper towel.

Cold Preparation

  1. Use a vegetable peeler to gently remove the skin from the bell pepper.
  2. Cut off the stem of the bell pepper with a utility knife or paring knife.
  3. Remove the seeds from the bell pepper by hand or with the help of a knife.
  4. Cut the bell pepper into the desired shape and size.

Warm Preparation

  1. Preheat oven to 250 degrees.
  2. Place the bell pepper on a baking sheet and drizzle with a small amount of oil.
  3. Bake for 5-10 minutes, or until the skin is slightly blistered.
  4. Remove the bell pepper from the oven and place it in a container.
  5. Cover the container with plastic wrap to create steam.
  6. Let the bell pepper cool for a few minutes.
  7. Remove the bell pepper from the container and peel off the skin by hand.
  8. Cut off the stem of the bell pepper with a utility knife or paring knife.
  9. Remove the seeds from the bell pepper by hand or with the help of a knife.
  10. Cut the bell pepper into the desired shape and size.

bernese_sauce.txt - Bernese Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French Bernese Sauce.
  • Understand the importance of using fresh herbs for authentic flavor.
  • Master the technique of emulsifying butter into a sauce.

Ingredients

  • 1/2 cup white wine
  • 1/4 cup white vinegar
  • 1 shallot, chopped
  • 1 tablespoon fresh tarragon
  • 1 tablespoon fresh chervil
  • 1/4 teaspoon black peppercorns
  • 2 egg yolks
  • 1 tablespoon cold water
  • 1/2 cup clarified butter
  • Salt to taste

Instructions

  1. Combine white wine, vinegar, shallots, tarragon, chervil, and black peppercorns in a saucepan over low heat.
  2. Bring the mixture to a simmer and cook until reduced to a tablespoon of liquid.
  3. Remove from heat and let cool completely.
  4. In a heatproof bowl, whisk together egg yolks and cold water until pale and frothy.
  5. Place the bowl over a saucepan of simmering water (make sure the bottom of the bowl doesn't touch the water).
  6. Whisk constantly until the mixture thickens to a creamy consistency.
  7. Remove the bowl from the heat and continue whisking until the mixture is cool.
  8. Slowly whisk in the clarified butter, a tablespoon at a time, until the sauce is emulsified and smooth.
  9. Season with salt to taste.
  10. Stir in a little more fresh tarragon and chervil for extra flavor.
  11. Serve immediately over red meat, fish, or potato dishes.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=UO-cE9PGb5Y

beurre_blanc.txt - Beurre Blanc

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a classic beurre blanc sauce.
  • Understand the key ingredients and techniques involved.
  • Discover the versatility of beurre blanc for various fish dishes.

Ingredients

  • 1 cup Chardonnay (dry white wine)
  • 1/4 cup white wine vinegar
  • 1 shallot, finely diced
  • 1/2 teaspoon salt
  • 1 cup unsalted butter, cut into cubes
  • Pinch of cayenne pepper (optional)

Instructions

  1. Soften the butter at room temperature.
  2. Finely dice the shallot using a filleting knife.
  3. Melt a small amount of butter in a saucepan over low heat.
  4. Add the diced shallots and cook gently until softened.
  5. Add the white wine vinegar and white wine.
  6. Increase the heat slightly and simmer until the liquid reduces to about a tablespoon.
  7. Reduce the heat to very low.
  8. Gradually whisk in the cubed butter, a few pieces at a time, allowing each piece to melt before adding more.
  9. Continue whisking until the sauce thickens and emulsifies, resembling a mayonnaise or hollandaise consistency.
  10. Season with salt and optional cayenne pepper.
  11. Strain the sauce through a fine-mesh sieve to remove any solids.
  12. Serve immediately over fish or other desired dishes.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=O9aFDEhIs4E

Instructions

bistro_sauce.txt - Bistro Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French bistro sauce.
  • Understand the importance of precise chopping techniques.
  • Discover how to create a tangy sauce perfect for grilled pork.

Ingredients

  • 1 large onion, finely chopped
  • 1 large shallot, finely chopped
  • 100 ml white wine vinegar
  • 100 ml demi-glace (video link in description)
  • 1 tablespoon tomato paste
  • 1/2 cup chopped mushrooms (optional)
  • 2 tablespoons butter
  • 1/4 cup chopped ham
  • 1 tablespoon capers
  • 1 tablespoon chopped gherkins
  • 1 tablespoon chopped parsley
  • Salt and pepper to taste

Instructions

  1. Finely chop the onion, shallot, and mushrooms.
  2. Melt butter in a small pan over medium heat.
  3. Add the chopped onion, shallot, and mushrooms.
  4. Cook gently for 5-10 minutes, until softened but still slightly crunchy.
  5. Add the white wine vinegar and bring to a boil.
  6. Reduce the vinegar by half, about 3-4 minutes.
  7. Add the demi-glace and tomato paste.
  8. Bring to a boil and reduce for 5 minutes, skimming off any excess fat.
  9. Turn off the heat and stir in the chopped ham, capers, gherkins, and parsley.
  10. Season with salt and pepper to taste.
  11. Warm the sauce slightly before serving and add the garnish just before serving.
  12. Serve over grilled pork chops or other roasted meats.

bistro_style_saute_potatoes.txt - Bistro Style Sauté Potatoes

Objectives

  • Learn how to make perfect bistro-style sauté potatoes.
  • Understand the importance of potato selection and preparation.
  • Master the technique of pre-cooking and pan-frying potatoes.

Ingredients

  • Baby Royal Blue potatoes (yellow flesh, ideal for roasting)
  • 1 onion
  • Fresh parsley
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Peanut oil

Instructions

  1. Cut the potatoes in half, then in half again to create quarters. This ensures even cooking.
  2. Pre-cook the potatoes by blanching them in salted water.
    • Start with cold water and add salt (10-15 grams per liter).
    • Bring the water to a boil.
    • Immediately turn off the heat once the water boils.
    • Drain the potatoes in a sieve and let them dry for a few minutes.
  3. Heat a black steel pan over medium to high heat.
  4. Add peanut oil and heat until very hot.
  5. Add the potatoes to the hot oil and season with salt and pepper.
  6. Cook for 10 minutes on high heat to achieve browning.
  7. Add sliced onions and reduce the heat to medium-low.
  8. Continue cooking until the onions are soft.
  9. Turn off the heat and add a generous amount of fresh parsley.
  10. Toss everything together and serve.

boiled_eggs.txt - Boiled Eggs

Objectives

  • Learn how to boil eggs to different levels of doneness.
  • Understand the importance of using fresh eggs for optimal results.
  • Explore different egg types and their uses in cooking.

Ingredients

  • Eggs (chicken, quail, duck)
  • Water
  • Ice water
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Butter
  • Bread

Instructions

  1. Gather your ingredients: eggs, water, ice water, salt, pepper, butter, and bread.
  2. Fill a pot with water and bring it to a boil.
  3. Gently place the eggs into the boiling water using a spoon or slotted spoon to prevent cracking.
  4. Set a timer for the desired cooking time:
    • Soft-boiled eggs: 2.5-3.5 minutes
    • Medium-boiled eggs: 5.5-6.5 minutes
    • Hard-boiled eggs: 9-11 minutes
  5. Once the timer goes off, immediately plunge the eggs into a bowl of ice water to stop the cooking process.
  6. For soft-boiled eggs, carefully remove the egg from the ice water and place it in an egg cup.
  7. To enjoy a soft-boiled egg the French way, prepare a small piece of bread with a bit of butter, salt, and pepper.
  8. Gently dunk the bread into the egg yolk and enjoy.

bouchon_lyonnais.txt - Bouchon Lyonnais

Objectives

  • Understand the unique features of a bouchon lyonnais
  • Explore the history and traditions of Lyonnais cuisine
  • Discover the specialty dish of "l'oreiller de la belle meunière"

Instructions

  1. Visit a bouchon lyonnais, a small, traditionally decorated bistro in Lyon.
  2. Expect a convivial atmosphere with shared tables and platters of simple, generous dishes.
  3. Enjoy comforting dishes like tripe, tablier de sapeur, bourguignon, and tripe in tomato.

  6. Share the pie with others, as it is served on a large plate with a small salad.
  7. Use a serrated knife with a straight blade to cut the pie, ensuring a clean cut through the crust.
  8. Consider visiting La Meunière, a bouchon lyonnais located at 11 Rue Neuve in Lyon.
  9. Experience the charm and history of this 100-year-old establishment.

bouquet_garni.txt - Bouquet Garni

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a bouquet garni
  • Understand the difference between a basic bouquet garni and a white stock bouquet garni
  • Discover the uses of the bouquet garni in French cooking

Ingredients

  • Parsley
  • Thyme
  • Bay leaves
  • Celery
  • Leeks

Instructions

  1. Gather ingredients: parsley, thyme, bay leaves, celery, and leeks.
  2. For the basic bouquet garni, tie together a few branches of parsley, a few sprigs of thyme, and one bay leaf.
  3. For the white stock bouquet garni, add a few branches of celery and a piece of leek to the basic bouquet garni.
  4. Tie the ingredients together tightly with a string.
  5. For professional cooks, use a long string to attach the bouquet garni to the pot for easy removal.
  6. Use the bouquet garni in stocks, soups, poached meats, and sauces.

bourbon_sauce.txt - Bourbon Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn to make a foolproof Bourbon sauce using cream
  • Understand the difference between Bourbon and Bernonte sauces
  • Discover the best technique for incorporating butter into a sauce

Ingredients

  • 1/2 cup white wine vinegar
  • 1/2 cup shallots
  • 1/4 cup heavy cream
  • 1 cup unsalted butter, cold, cubed
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • Cayenne pepper (optional)

Instructions

  1. Combine the white wine vinegar and shallots in a saucepan over medium heat.
  2. Bring the mixture to a boil, then reduce the heat to low and simmer until the liquid is almost completely evaporated, leaving about 1 tablespoon.
  3. Add the heavy cream and continue to simmer for 1 minute.
  4. Turn off the heat and add the cubed butter, whisking vigorously until the butter is melted and the sauce is emulsified.
  5. Season with salt, pepper, and cayenne pepper to taste.
  6. Serve immediately over fish.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LGKXRGTmXks

braised_cabbage.txt - Braised Cabbage

Objectives

  • Learn how to braise cabbage using a French technique
  • Create a flavorful and tender cabbage dish using homemade stock and smoked pork belly
  • Understand the importance of blanching cabbage leaves and removing the stalk

Ingredients

  • 2 cups homemade stock
  • 1 mirepoix (carrot, onion, celery)
  • Smoked pork belly or bacon, cut into chunks
  • Cabbage
  • Fat back
  • Thyme
  • Bay leaves
  • Salt and pepper
  • Butter
  • Corn
  • Pig skins (optional)

Instructions

  1. Blanch the cabbage leaves and remove the stalk.
  2. Preheat oven to 180 degrees Celsius (356 Fahrenheit).
  3. Sweat the mirepoix, bacon, and butter in a pan over medium heat for 5 minutes.
  4. In a cast iron pan, layer the braising mix (mirepoix, bacon, thyme, bay leaves) at the bottom.
  5. Layer the cabbage leaves on top of the braising mix, pressing down to create a compact layer.
  6. Season with salt and pepper.
  7. Pour in the homemade stock, ensuring the cabbage is fully submerged.
  8. Bring the stock to a boil on the stovetop.
  9. Cover the pan with a lid and place in the oven for 1.5 hours.
  10. After 1.5 hours, remove the pan from the oven and add a layer of fat back on top of the cabbage.
  11. Return the pan to the oven for an additional 1.5 hours.
  12. Once cooked, remove the cabbage from the oven and allow it to cool slightly.
  13. Roll the cabbage leaves into individual portions and serve with the braising juices.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=aPw2yWIgmz4

braised_chicken_garlic_lemon.txt - Braised Chicken with Garlic and Lemon

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple French braised chicken dish with garlic and lemon.
  • Understand the importance of preparing ingredients and deglazing the pan.
  • Discover two sauce variations: classic and creamy.

Ingredients

  • 1 lemon
  • Provincial herbs (mixed herbs)
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 15 cloves garlic
  • Chicken (amount not specified)
  • Salt and pepper
  • Flour (for dusting)
  • White chicken stock
  • Wine
  • Olive oil
  • Butter
  • Shallots
  • Cream (optional)

Instructions

  1. Peel the lemon completely, removing all skin and white parts. Cut into slices.
  2. Prepare the herbs: gather provincial herbs, a bay leaf, and peel and halve 15 cloves of garlic.
  3. Season chicken with salt and pepper, then dust lightly with flour.
  4. Bring white chicken stock to a boil, then add rinsed garlic cloves and simmer for 1-2 minutes.
  5. Heat olive oil and butter in a Dutch oven over medium heat. Brown chicken for 5 minutes on each side.
  6. Remove chicken and discard excess fat from the pan.
  7. Add bay leaf to the pan and increase heat.
  8. Sauté shallots for 1-2 minutes until softened.
  9. Deglaze the pan with wine, scraping up browned bits. Reduce wine for a few minutes until slightly syrupy.
  10. Add garlic stock to the pan, bring to a boil, and reduce for a few minutes.
  11. Preheat oven to 190°C (375°F).
  12. After the stock has reduced, add pepper, salt, herbs, and lemon slices to the pan.
  13. Add chicken pieces to the pan, ensuring the skin side faces up.
  14. Drizzle remaining oil over the chicken to prevent dryness.
  15. Cover the pan and braise in the oven for 40-45 minutes.
  16. Remove chicken from the pan and finish the sauce.
  17. Option 1: Reduce the sauce slightly for a classic garlic and lemon flavor. Pour over chicken or serve on the side.
  18. Option 2: Add cream to the sauce and bring to a boil. Reduce until desired consistency is reached.
  19. Taste the sauce and adjust seasoning as needed.
  20. Serve chicken with the finished sauce. Decorate with lemon zest and herbs.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=uboVAlbMWyc

braised_chicken_lemon_thyme_sauce.txt - Braised Chicken with Lemon and Thyme Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn how to flavor a dish with native Australian herbs and spices
  • Discover the unique flavors of lemon myrtle and Tasmanian pepper berries
  • Create a delicious and aromatic braised chicken with a creamy lemon sauce

Ingredients

  • 1 chicken, cut into pieces
  • 2 lemons
  • 1 bunch lemon thyme
  • 1 tablespoon lemon myrtle (dried)
  • 1 tablespoon Tasmanian pepper berries
  • 1 tablespoon olive oil
  • 2-3 pinches of salt
  • 1.5 tablespoons olive oil (for cooking)
  • 1 cup chicken stock
  • 1/2 cup heavy cream

Instructions

  1. Prepare the marinade: In a large bowl, combine chicken pieces, lemon juice, lemon thyme sprigs, Tasmanian pepper berries, lemon myrtle, salt, and 2-3 tablespoons olive oil. Mix well and cover with plastic wrap. Refrigerate for at least 1 hour.
  2. Cook the chicken bones: Heat 1.5 tablespoons olive oil in a cast iron pot over medium heat. Add the chicken bones and cook until lightly browned, about 5 minutes. Remove bones from the pot.
  3. Brown the chicken: Add the marinated chicken pieces to the pot, one at a time. Cook until lightly browned on all sides. Remove chicken and set aside.
  4. Braise the chicken: Return the chicken bones to the pot. Add the chicken pieces on top. Pour in the chicken stock, ensuring the bones and chicken are submerged in the liquid. Bring to a simmer, cover, and cook for 35-45 minutes.
  5. Prepare the sauce: While the chicken is braising, remove the chicken pieces and set aside. Discard the chicken bones. Reduce the braising liquid over high heat until it thickens slightly.
  6. Finish the sauce: Add the remaining marinade to the reduced sauce. Bring to a boil. Add the heavy cream and bring back to a boil. Reduce heat to low and simmer for 5-6 minutes until the sauce thickens.
  7. Serve: Arrange the cooked chicken pieces on a plate. Pour the sauce over the chicken. Garnish with lemon zest. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=K_WTtO_ihdM

braised_fennel_wine_lemon_coriander.txt - Braised Fennel with Wine, Lemon, and Coriander

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare fennel from root to bulb.
  • Master the blanching technique for fennel.
  • Create a simple, flavorful braised fennel dish.

Ingredients

  • 1 fennel bulb
  • 1/2 cup white wine
  • 1/2 cup water
  • 1 tablespoon olive oil
  • 1/2 teaspoon coriander seeds
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 1/2 teaspoon thyme
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • 1 tablespoon lemon juice

Instructions

  1. Trim the fennel stalks and remove the outer layer of leaves.
  2. Cut the fennel bulb in half and then into quarters.
  3. Blanch the fennel quarters in boiling salted water for 3 minutes.
  4. Remove the fennel from the water and drain in a sieve.
  5. Optional: Grill the fennel lightly for aesthetic appeal and a slight roasty flavor.
  6. In a small saucepan, combine the wine, water, coriander seeds, bay leaf, thyme, salt, and pepper.
  7. Bring the mixture to a simmer.
  8. Add the fennel quarters to the simmering liquid.
  9. Drizzle with olive oil.
  10. Cover the pan and cook for 35-40 minutes, or until the fennel is tender.
  11. Remove the fennel from the pan and arrange on a plate.
  12. Baste the fennel with the cooking juices.
  13. Drizzle with lemon juice.
  14. Season with salt and pepper to taste.
  15. Serve immediately.

braised_lamb_shanks_with_port_sauce.txt - Braised Lamb Shanks with Port Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn the braising technique for lamb shanks
  • Master the art of creating a rich, flavorful port sauce
  • Discover a simple yet elegant recipe for braised lamb shanks

Ingredients

  • lamb shanks
  • port wine
  • stock
  • rosemary
  • shallots
  • garlic
  • bay leaf
  • onions
  • carrots
  • salt
  • pepper

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 170 degrees Celsius (338 degrees Fahrenheit).
  2. Season lamb shanks with salt and pepper.
  3. Heat a tablespoon of oil in a cast iron pot over medium heat.
  4. Sear lamb shanks on all sides until nicely browned.
  5. Remove lamb shanks from the pot and set aside.
  6. Add carrots and onions to the pot and sauté until softened.
  7. Add shallots, crushed garlic, and a teaspoon of tomato paste. Cook until fragrant.
  8. Deglaze the pot with port wine, bringing it to a boil to reduce the alcohol content.
  9. Return lamb shanks to the pot.
  10. Add stock, ensuring the liquid barely covers the meat.
  11. Bring the mixture to a simmer, then transfer the pot to the preheated oven.
  12. Braise for 3 hours, or until the lamb is tender and falls off the bone.
  13. Remove lamb shanks from the pot and place them in a tray with a little bit of sauce. Keep warm in the oven at 70 degrees Celsius (158 degrees Fahrenheit).
  14. Reduce the braising liquid over medium-high heat until it thickens and becomes syrupy.
  15. Strain the sauce through a fine mesh sieve to remove any solids.
  16. Return the strained sauce to the pot and adjust seasoning with salt, pepper, and a dash of port.
  17. Stir in a knob of butter, swirling the sauce until the butter is melted.
  18. Serve the braised lamb shanks with the port sauce, garnished with chopped rosemary.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=gdBKp302X5M

braised_pork_shoulder_with_prunes.txt - Braised Pork Shoulder Stuffed with Prunes

Objectives

  • Learn how to braise pork shoulder with cider and apples.
  • Master a simple trussing technique for a neat presentation.
  • Discover a unique flavor combination using chestnut and apple liquor.

Ingredients

  • 1 onion, roughly chopped
  • 2 cloves garlic
  • 1 piece thyme
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 2 apples
  • Oyster mushrooms
  • Prunes (macerated in chestnut and apple liquor)
  • Creme fraiche
  • Salt and pepper
  • Butter
  • Cider

Instructions

  1. Macerate prunes in chestnut and apple liquor.
  2. Make incisions in the pork shoulder and insert prunes.
  3. Pat the pork shoulder dry with paper towels.
  4. Season the pork shoulder with salt and pepper.
  5. Truss the pork shoulder using butcher string.
  6. Heat a cast iron pot over medium-high heat.
  7. Add a small amount of oil to the pot.
  8. Sear the pork shoulder on all sides until browned.
  9. Remove the pork shoulder from the pot.
  10. Add chopped onions to the pot and cook until softened.
  11. Add garlic, thyme, bay leaf, and mushrooms to the pot.
  12. Deglaze the pot with cider.
  13. Add a few extra prunes to the pot.
  14. Place the pork shoulder back in the pot.
  15. Add enough cider to barely cover the pork shoulder.
  16. Braise in the oven at 325°F for 50 minutes.
  17. Check the internal temperature of the pork shoulder (should be 160°F).
  18. If needed, cook for another 10-15 minutes.
  19. While the pork shoulder cooks, pan-fry the remaining mushrooms with butter, salt, and pepper.
  20. Pan-fry apples with butter, salt, and pepper.
  21. Remove the pork shoulder from the oven and let it rest.
  22. Reduce the braising liquid.
  23. Add creme fraiche to the braising liquid.
  24. Adjust seasoning.
  25. Glaze the pork shoulder with the chestnut and apple liquor.
  26. Assemble the dish:
    • Place a layer of sauce, mushrooms, and apples in the serving dish.
    • Place the pork shoulder on top.
    • Garnish with prunes.
  27. Slice the pork shoulder and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=3whz41vgoGI

braised_short_ribs_with_madera.txt - Braised Short Ribs with Madera

Objectives

  • Learn to braise short ribs using classic French culinary methods.
  • Understand the importance of marinating and searing meat properly.
  • Master the art of making a rich and flavorful Madera sauce.

Ingredients

  • Beef Short Ribs (Dexter cattle preferred)
  • Carrots
  • Onions or Shallots
  • Garlic
  • Bay Leaf
  • Thyme
  • Fat B (smoked and cured pork fat)
  • Parsley
  • Madera Wine (150-200 ml)
  • Beef Stock (approx. 3 cups)
  • Flour (for dusting)
  • Salt and Pepper
  • Butter
  • Fresh Mushrooms
  • Celery (optional)
  • Shallots (optional)

Instructions

  1. Marinate the short ribs overnight in a dish with Madera wine, carrots, onions or shallots, garlic, bay leaf, thyme, and fat B rolled in parsley.
  2. Prepare the beef stock in advance and refrigerate.
  3. The next day, remove the short ribs from the marinade and pat them dry.
  4. Discard the garnish from the marinade and strain the juices through a sieve, reserving the aromatics.
  5. Season the short ribs with salt and pepper.
  6. Dust the short ribs lightly with flour.
  7. Sear the short ribs in a hot pan with pork fat until they are well-colored on all sides.
  8. Remove the short ribs from the pan and set aside.
  9. Clean the pan and add butter.
  10. Sweat the fresh garnish (mushrooms, celery, shallots) for a few minutes.
  11. Add the reserved marinade juices and bring to a boil.
  12. Reduce the marinade juices by half.
  13. Place the seared short ribs back in the pan with the garnish and marinade juices.
  14. Warm the beef stock and add it to the pan, ensuring it barely covers the meat.
  15. Cover the pan with parchment paper and a lid.
  16. Braise the short ribs in a preheated oven at 170°C (338°F) for 2.5-3 hours, adding more stock if necessary.
  17. Once the meat is tender and easily pulls away from the bone, remove it from the pan and place it on a tray.
  18. Cover the tray with parchment paper and keep the meat warm in the oven.
  19. To make the Madera sauce, pour the braising juices from the pan into a bowl and filter them through a sieve.
  20. Heat a pan with butter and sauté the shallots and mushrooms until softened.
  21. Add the filtered braising juices and 1 cup of fresh beef stock.
  22. Bring the sauce to a boil and reduce until it reaches a syrupy consistency.
  23. Stir in a dash of fresh Madera wine.
  24. Taste and adjust the seasoning with salt and pepper.
  25. Serve the braised short ribs with the Madera sauce.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=WqXORquTd_c

breast_chicken_aoc.txt - Breast Chicken AOC

Objectives

  • Learn about the AOC label and its significance in French cuisine.
  • Compare the taste and quality of AOC breast chicken to standard chicken.
  • Prepare a simple yet flavorful breast chicken dish using AOC ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 1 breast chicken AOC
  • 1.7 kg
  • 1 bouquet garni
  • 1/2 carrot
  • 1/2 onion
  • 1 tablespoon parsley
  • AOC butter
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • 300 ml Savagnin wine (AOC)
  • 300 ml homemade chicken stock
  • 200 ml chanterelle mushroom soaking juice
  • 300-400 ml creme fraiche AOC
  • Chanterelle mushrooms

Instructions

  1. Rinse the chicken carcass in cold water.
  2. Bring the water to a boil, then immediately turn off the heat.
  3. Rinse the carcass in cold water again.
  4. Place the carcass back in a clean pan with cold water.
  5. Add the bouquet garni, half a carrot, half an onion, a tablespoon of parsley, and peppercorns to the water.
  6. Simmer the stock for 30-40 minutes.
  7. While the stock simmers, prepare the chicken.
  8. Pat the chicken dry and season with salt and pepper.
  9. Heat a pan over medium heat and add AOC butter.
  10. Sear the chicken skin-side down until golden brown.
  11. Reserve the breast and cook the legs for 15 minutes.
  12. Remove the legs and set aside.
  13. Remove excess fat from the pan.
  14. Add 300 ml of Savagnin wine to the pan.
  15. Bring the wine to a boil, then add 300 ml of chicken stock.
  16. Bring the mixture to a boil again, then add 200 ml of chanterelle mushroom soaking juice.
  17. Add 300-400 ml of creme fraiche AOC to the sauce.
  18. Simmer the legs in the sauce for 15-20 minutes.
  19. Add the breast to the sauce and simmer for 1 hour.
  20. After 45 minutes, remove the legs and breast from the sauce.
  21. Bring the sauce to a high heat and reduce until thickened.
  22. Add a handful of chanterelle mushrooms to the sauce and simmer for 5 minutes.
  23. Plate the chicken with boiled potatoes and toasted bread.
  24. Spoon the sauce over the chicken and garnish with chanterelle mushrooms.
  25. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=F-RTX_Ak1eg

broccoli_cauliflower_gratin.txt - Broccoli and Cauliflower Gratin (French Home Style)

Objectives

  • Explore a simple, quick French home-style recipe for broccoli and cauliflower gratin.
  • Compare the home-style method to the more complex restaurant-style gratin.
  • Discover a healthy and flavorful side dish option for various meals.

Ingredients

  • 1-2 tablespoons of rock salt
  • 1 head of broccoli
  • 1 head of cauliflower
  • 1 cup of heavy cream
  • 2 eggs
  • 1/2 cup of almond milk
  • 1 tablespoon of butter
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • Grated cheese (amount to taste)

Instructions

  1. Fill two separate pots with water and add 1-2 tablespoons of rock salt to each.
  2. Bring the water to a boil.
  3. Once boiling, add the broccoli to one pot and the cauliflower to the other.
  4. Cook for 10 minutes.
  5. Preheat oven to 210 degrees Celsius (410 degrees Fahrenheit).
  6. While the vegetables are cooking, prepare the custard mixture in a bowl.
  7. Add the heavy cream, eggs, almond milk, salt, and pepper to the bowl and whisk until well combined.
  8. Butter a baking dish.
  9. Drain the broccoli and cauliflower.
  10. Season the bottom of the baking dish with salt and pepper.
  11. Arrange the vegetables in the dish, layering cauliflower first and then broccoli.
  12. Pour the custard mixture over the vegetables.
  13. Top with grated cheese.
  14. Bake in the preheated oven for 15 minutes.
  15. Broil for an additional 2 minutes to crisp up the cheese.
  16. Let cool slightly before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=uC9iLiXmoAo

broccoli_prep.txt - Broccoli Preparation

Objectives

  • Learn how to properly prepare broccoli for cooking.
  • Understand the importance of washing and rinsing vegetables twice.
  • Discover how to recycle broccoli stems for soups and stocks.

Ingredients

  • Broccoli florets
  • Water
  • Vinegar

Instructions

  1. Trim the untidy bit from the broccoli stem.
  2. Cut the broccoli florets into smaller pieces, keeping the flower-like shape.
  3. Place the florets in a container of water.
  4. Trim the broccoli stems and reserve them for soups or stocks.
  5. Add vinegar to the water with the broccoli florets.
  6. Let the broccoli rest in the vinegar water for a few minutes to remove any insects.
  7. Discard the vinegar water and wash the broccoli florets again in clean water.
  8. Cook the broccoli florets by steaming or blanching in boiling salted water.
  9. Use the reserved broccoli stems for making soups or stocks.
