fennel_tomato_ragu.txt - Fennel and Tomato Ragú

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare a vegetarian fennel and tomato ragu.
  • Understand the importance of blanching fennel for a better texture.
  • Explore different techniques for preparing vegetables for a dish.

Ingredients

  • 1 large eggplant (aubergine)
  • 1 fennel bulb
  • 1 large onion
  • 2 cloves garlic
  • 1 can peeled tomatoes
  • 1/2 cup homemade tomato sauce (optional)
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • 1 teaspoon black pepper
  • 3-4 tablespoons chopped parsley (optional)
  • 4 anchovy fillets (optional)

Instructions

  1. Fill a large saucepan with water and bring to a boil.
  2. Cut the eggplant into cubes and sprinkle with salt. Let sit for 15-20 minutes.
  3. Remove the green part of the tomatoes and make a small cross at the top with a knife.
  4. Plunge the tomatoes into the boiling water for 5-10 seconds, then immediately transfer to a bowl of ice water.
  5. Peel the tomatoes and remove the seeds.
  6. Trim the tough outer leaves and stalks of the fennel bulb.
  7. Cut the fennel bulb in half.
  8. Add a tablespoon of salt to the boiling water and blanch the fennel halves for 5-6 minutes.
  9. Remove the fennel from the boiling water and plunge into ice water to stop the cooking.
  10. Rinse the eggplant cubes under cold water to remove excess salt.
  11. Cut the peeled tomatoes into quarters.
  12. Thinly slice the onion.
  13. Peel and remove the germ from the garlic cloves.
  14. Heat a large saucepan over medium heat.
  15. Add a tablespoon of olive oil to the pan and heat.
  16. Add the thinly sliced onion to the pan and cook for 2 minutes.
  17. Add the blanched fennel halves to the pan and cook for 10 minutes, stirring occasionally.
  18. Add the peeled and quartered tomatoes to the pan.
  19. Season with salt and pepper.
  20. Add the eggplant cubes, garlic cloves, and homemade tomato sauce (optional) to the pan.
  21. Season with additional salt and pepper.
  22. Cover the pan and cook for 30 minutes, or until the vegetables are tender.
  23. If necessary, add a little extra water to the pan and close the lid to ensure the vegetables cook properly.
  24. Add the chopped parsley (optional) and anchovy fillets (optional) to the pan.
  25. Stir to combine and cook for 5 minutes.
  26. Remove from heat and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=XPXoqEEwkRQ

fig_raspberry_tart.txt - Fig and Raspberry Tart

Objectives

  • Demonstrate how basic cooking techniques can elevate simple ingredients.
  • Create a delicious and visually appealing tart using seasonal fruits.

Ingredients

  • Fresh raspberries

Instructions

  1. Roll out the shortcrust pastry and line a tart pan.
  2. Spread a thin layer of almond cream over the pastry.
  3. Arrange fresh figs in a circle, leaving some space for raspberries.
  4. Bake the tart at 180°C (350°F) for 40 minutes.
  5. Allow the tart to cool completely before decorating.
  6. Sprinkle cinnamon sugar over the cooled tart.
  7. Arrange fresh raspberries on top of the figs.
  8. Decorate with additional figs around the edges.

financier_cake.txt - Financier Cake

Objectives

  • Learn the history of the financier cake.
  • Master the technique of making hazelnut butter.
  • Create a delicious and easy financier cake with various toppings.

Ingredients

Dry Ingredients - 50g plain flour - 60g almond meal (ground almond) - 150g icing sugar

Wet Ingredients - 3 egg whites - 150g plain butter

Topping Options - Pears - Raspberries - Flaked almonds

Instructions

  1. Melt the butter in a saucepan over medium heat until it starts to foam and brown.
  2. Whisk constantly until the butter turns a light hazelnut color.
  3. Remove from heat and filter the butter through a sieve to remove any brown bits.
  4. Sift the flour, icing sugar, and almond meal into a bowl and mix well.
  5. Add the egg whites to the dry ingredients and mix until combined.
  6. Gradually add the hazelnut butter to the batter, mixing until fully incorporated.
  7. Cover the batter and refrigerate for 1 hour.
  8. Preheat oven to 200 degrees Celsius (392 degrees Fahrenheit).
  9. Grease a muffin pan with butter.
  10. Fill each cavity with approximately one tablespoon of batter.
  11. Top each financier with your choice of fruit or almonds.
  12. Bake for 5 minutes at 200 degrees Celsius, then reduce the heat to 180 degrees Celsius (356 degrees Fahrenheit) and bake for an additional 10-15 minutes.
  13. To check if the financiers are done, insert a knife into the center. It should come out clean but slightly moist.
  14. Sprinkle the financiers with icing sugar while still hot.
  15. Let the financiers cool for at least 15 minutes before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=tLv0qHCHHtQ

fish_canal.txt - French Style Fish Canal

Objectives

  • Learn a simple French culinary technique for making various dishes
  • Make fish canal, a French-style fish dumpling
  • Learn to make a flavorful cream sauce with cognac and scampi

Ingredients

Fish Canal - Any type of fish (cold or half-frozen) - 2 eggs - 1/4 cup butter - 1/4 cup cream - Salt - Pepper - Cayenne pepper (optional)

Sauce - Fish stock (jellified) - 1 tablespoon butter - Scampi (or lobster, shrimp) - 1 clove garlic - 1 carrot (chopped) - 1 celery stalk (chopped) - 1 leek (chopped) - Salt - Pepper - Tomato paste - 1-2 tablespoons cognac - Heavy cream

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Fish Canal:
  2. In a cold bowl of a food processor, blend half-frozen fish until it becomes a paste.
  3. Add eggs and blend until smooth.
  4. Season with salt, pepper, and cayenne pepper (optional).
  5. Slowly pour in cream and butter while blending until smooth.

  6. Cover the mixture with plastic wrap, pressing it onto the surface, and refrigerate overnight.

  7. Cook the Fish Canal:

  8. Bring a pot of water to a simmer. Add a clove of garlic, salt, and pepper.
  9. Using a deep spoon, scoop out some of the fish mixture and roll it into a canal shape.
  10. Gently place the canals in the simmering water.
  11. Cook for 15 minutes, turning the canals every 5 minutes with a spoon.

  12. Drain the canals on paper towels and set aside.

  13. Make the Sauce:

  14. Reduce the fish stock in a saucepan over medium heat.
  15. In a separate saute pan, melt butter over high heat and cook scampi until browned.
  16. Add garlic, carrot, celery, and leek to the pan and cook until softened.
  17. Season with salt and pepper.
  18. Stir in tomato paste and cook for 1-2 minutes.
  19. Add cognac and heat until it ignites.
  20. Pour in heavy cream and reduce heat to low.
  21. Simmer until the sauce thickens.

  22. Season with additional salt, pepper, and cayenne pepper to taste.

  23. Assemble and Broil:

  24. Preheat oven to 375 degrees Fahrenheit (190 degrees Celsius).
  25. Place the cooked fish canals in a heat-proof dish.
  26. Pour the sauce over the canals, ensuring they are half-submerged.

  27. Broil for 10 minutes, or until the sauce bubbles and the canals are golden brown.

  28. Serve:

  29. Serve immediately with a garnish of scampi flesh.
  30. Enjoy the light and flavorful fish canals with the rich, creamy sauce.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Or0dCoJNmqM

fish_fillet_sauce_van_blonde.txt - Fish Fillet with Sauce Van Blonde

Objectives

  • Learn to fillet a whole fish and create a classic French fish sauce.
  • Master the art of making a fish fumet from scratch.
  • Develop a deep understanding of sauce reduction techniques.

Ingredients

Fish

  • 1 flathead fish (or any round fish)
  • 20 grams of butter
  • 1 onion
  • 1 shallot
  • 1 carrot
  • Mushroom trimming
  • Thyme (optional)
  • Bouquet garni
  • Salt
  • Peppercorns
  • White wine

Sauce

  • 1 tablespoon of butter
  • 1/2 cup of cream
  • Fresh tomato
  • Parsley

Instructions

  1. Wash hands thoroughly.
  2. Prepare the fish by scaling, removing the gills and tail, and cleaning the fish.
  3. Fillet the fish using a sharp knife, following the bone.
  4. Carefully make an incision along the backbone, then slide the knife under the skin to separate the fillet.
  5. Remove the skin from the fillet.
  6. Prepare the fish fumet by melting butter in a pan.
  7. Add the onion, shallot, carrots, and mushroom trimming to the pan.
  8. Sweat the vegetables for 1-2 minutes over low heat.
  9. Add the fish bones, coating them with the vegetables.
  10. Pour a small amount of water and white wine over the bones, barely covering them.
  11. Add the bouquet garni, salt, and peppercorns.
  12. Bring the mixture to a boil, then reduce heat and simmer for 20-25 minutes.
  13. Strain the fish fumet through a sieve and let it cool completely.
  14. Cook the fish fillets in a deep pan by brushing the bottom with butter and adding salt, pepper, shallots, onion, and parsley.
  15. Arrange the fish fillets on top of the garnish, add a small amount of white wine to the pan, and cover the fillets with the cooled fish fumet.
  16. Cover the pan with parchment paper, turn the heat to medium, and bring to a simmer.
  17. Preheat the oven to 160 degrees Celsius (320 degrees Fahrenheit).
  18. Once the mixture simmers, transfer the pan to the oven and cook for 5-7 minutes, depending on the size of the fillets.
  19. Remove the pan from the oven and carefully filter the cooking juices into a separate pan.
  20. Bring the cooking juices to a boil and reduce them almost to a glaze.
  21. Add half the amount of cream called for in the recipe and reduce it by half.
  22. Once the sauce is smooth and creamy, taste and adjust seasoning.
  23. Optionally, add a fresh tomato to the sauce to create a sauce DubLi La.
  24. Turn off the heat and add a final piece of butter to the sauce for shine and flavor.
  25. Serve the fish fillets with the sauce Van Blonde, garnished with parsley.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=H6KFMovkFCU

fish_veloute_john_dory.txt - Fish Veloute with John Dory

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a classic French fish veloute sauce.
  • Understand the techniques of poaching fish and creating a roux.
  • Master the art of creating a delicate and flavorful sauce for fish.

Ingredients

English: - Fish stock - Butter - Fresh lemon - Flour - 2 egg yolks - John Dory fillets - White wine - Shallots - Leeks - Tomatoes

Chinese: - 鱼汤 - 黄油 - 鲜柠檬 - 面粉 - 2个蛋黄 - 多宝鱼片 - 白葡萄酒 - 葱头 - 韭葱 - 番茄

Instructions

  1. Prepare the ingredients:
    • Thinly slice two shallots.
    • Separate the egg yolks from the egg whites.
    • Slice 3/4 of a leek, mainly the white part.
  2. Make the roux:
    • Melt 25 grams of butter in a saucepan over low heat.
    • Add 25 grams of flour and cook for 1-2 minutes, stirring constantly, until the roux is white.
    • Remove from heat and set aside to cool.
  3. Prepare the fish:
    • Melt a small amount of butter in a pan over low heat.
    • Add the shallots and sweat until softened.
    • Arrange the John Dory fillets in the pan, ensuring they are evenly spaced.
    • Season with salt and pepper.
    • Add a splash of white wine.
    • Pour in fish stock until it just covers the fish.
    • Cover with a piece of parchment paper and a lid.
    • Poach the fish for 6-8 minutes.
  4. Prepare the garnish:
    • Julienne the leeks.
    • Melt some butter in a pan.
    • Add the leeks and a pinch of sugar.
    • Add a tablespoon of water.
    • Cover the pan and cook over low heat for 5-6 minutes.
  5. Strain the fish stock:
    • Gently remove the poached John Dory fillets from the pan.
    • Strain the fish stock into a clean saucepan.
  6. Make the veloute sauce:
    • Slowly whisk the hot fish stock into the cooled roux.
    • Add 1 1/2 cups of fish fumet.
    • Season with salt and pepper.
    • Bring to a boil, stirring constantly, until the sauce thickens.
    • Reduce heat to low and simmer for a few minutes to sterilize the sauce.
    • Remove from heat and whisk in 2 egg yolks that have been diluted with 1 tablespoon of crème fraiche.
    • Stir in the juice of half a lemon.
    • Whisk in 40 grams of butter.
  7. Assemble the dish:
    • Place a bed of leeks in butter on a plate.
    • Place a John Dory fillet on top.
    • Drizzle the fish with the veloute sauce.
    • Garnish with a slice of lemon, a few tomato slices, and a sprinkle of parsley.
  8. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=u34GpPRkmPk

flambe_crepes.txt - Flambé Crepes

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic Flambé Crepe dessert.
  • Understand the importance of using high-quality ingredients, particularly Grand Marnier and Cointreau.
  • Discover how to create a rich and flavorful syrup for bathing the crepes.

Ingredients

  • 1-2 Crepes (made with your preferred recipe)
  • 1/4 cup sugar
  • 2 tablespoons unsalted butter
  • 1/4 cup orange juice, freshly squeezed
  • 1/4 cup lemon juice, freshly squeezed
  • 1/4 cup Grand Marnier
  • 1/4 cup Cointreau
  • 1/4 orange, flesh only, no skin
  • 1/4 lemon zest, blanched (optional)

Instructions

  1. Heat a stainless steel frying pan over medium heat.
  2. Add the sugar and butter to the pan and melt, stirring occasionally.
  3. Add the orange juice, lemon juice, Grand Marnier, and Cointreau to the pan and stir gently.
  4. Bring the mixture to a simmer and cook until it thickens slightly, resembling a syrup.
  5. Carefully place the crepes into the syrup, ensuring they are fully submerged.
  6. Optionally, fold the crepes in half or thirds to create a more compact shape.
  7. Increase the heat to high and carefully add the remaining alcohol to the pan.
  8. Ignite the alcohol with a flame (be extremely cautious!).
  9. Allow the flames to extinguish naturally.
  10. Remove the crepes from the syrup and serve immediately, drizzled with the remaining syrup and garnished with orange flesh and lemon zest (optional).

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=FwE-r-y5hws

flambé_omelet.txt - Flambé Omelet

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a classic French-style omelet
  • Understand the flambé technique to add a touch of excitement
  • Master the art of flipping the omelet for a perfect presentation

Ingredients

  • 2-3 eggs
  • 1 tablespoon of butter
  • Pinch of salt
  • 1 teaspoon of sugar
  • Optional: Filling of your choice (e.g., cheese, ham, vegetables)

Instructions

  1. Crack 2-3 eggs into a bowl and whisk them together until well combined.
  2. Add a pinch of salt and 1 teaspoon of sugar to the egg mixture and whisk again.
  3. Heat a non-stick pan over medium heat.
  4. Add 1 tablespoon of butter to the pan and let it melt completely.
  5. Pour the egg mixture into the pan and tilt the pan to distribute the eggs evenly.
  6. As the eggs begin to set, gently push the edges of the omelet towards the center using a spatula.
  7. Continue tilting the pan to allow uncooked egg to flow to the edges.
  8. When the omelet is mostly set but still slightly wet on top, add any desired fillings.
  9. Fold one-third of the omelet over the center.
  10. Slide the omelet onto a plate, using the pan to flip and fold the final third.
  11. Flambé: Carefully pour a small amount of liquor (e.g., brandy, rum) over the omelet. Light the liquor with a match or lighter and let it burn off.
  12. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=pgOVRnBE92o

flaming_cook.txt - Flammekueche

Objectives

  • Learn to make a traditional Flammekueche, a Franco-German pizza-style dish.
  • Master the simple dough recipe without using yeast.
  • Discover the key to achieving a thin, crispy crust.
  • Understand the importance of thinly slicing ingredients for even cooking.
  • Enjoy a delicious and flavorful Flammekueche.

Ingredients

English | Chinese ------- | -------- 200 ml Water | 水 200 毫升 25 ml Oil | 油 25 毫升 Pinch of Salt | 盐 少许 250 g Flour | 面粉 250 克 1 Onion | 洋葱 1 个 Bacon | 培根 适量 Cottage cheese | 干酪 适量 Creme Fraiche | 淡奶油 适量 Nutmeg | 肉豆蔻 适量

Instructions

  1. Combine 200 ml of water, 25 ml of oil, and a pinch of salt in a bowl.
  2. Make sure the salt dissolves completely before adding the flour.
  3. Place 250 g of flour in a food processor fitted with a dough blade.
  4. Gradually add the liquid mixture to the flour while the processor runs on low speed.
  5. Once the dough comes together, remove it from the processor and place it on a plate.
  6. Thinly slice one onion using a food processor.
  7. Cut bacon into thin strips.
  8. Combine cottage cheese, creme fraiche, and a pinch of nutmeg in a bowl.
  9. Mix the ingredients together until well combined.
  10. Roll out the dough on a lightly floured surface until it is very thin, about a few millimeters thick.
  11. Place the dough on a baking sheet.
  12. Spread the cottage cheese mixture evenly over the dough.
  13. Sprinkle with sliced onions and bacon.
  14. Preheat oven to 200 degrees Celsius (400 degrees Fahrenheit).
  15. Bake for 8-10 minutes, or until the crust is golden brown and crispy.
  16. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=SJuoTgBRMzI

flatten_meat_bread_mayo.txt - Flattening Meat, Breading, & Homemade Mayonnaise

Objectives

  • Learn how to flatten meat for schnitzel.
  • Master three different breading techniques.
  • Create a perfect homemade mayonnaise.

Ingredients

For Mayonnaise - 1 egg yolk - Pinch of salt and white pepper - 1/2 teaspoon vinegar - 1 teaspoon mustard - 120-150 ml oil (sunflower oil recommended)

For Breading - Flour - Eggs - Breadcrumbs - Mustard (for mustard breading) - Clarified butter (for butter breading)

Instructions

  1. Flatten Meat:
  2. Place a piece of parchment paper on a sturdy chopping board.
  3. Place the meat on the parchment paper.
  4. Cover the meat with another piece of parchment paper.
  5. Use a heavy pan with a thick bottom to flatten the meat, applying firm pressure.
  6. Make Homemade Mayonnaise:
  7. Ensure all ingredients are at room temperature.
  8. Whisk together vinegar, salt, pepper, egg yolk, and mustard in a bowl.
  9. Gradually whisk in oil, starting with a small amount to emulsify the mixture.
  10. Continue whisking, adding oil in small amounts at first, then increasing the amount as the mayonnaise thickens.
  11. Whisk until the mayonnaise is thick and creamy.
  12. Classic Breading:
  13. Season the meat with salt and pepper.
  14. Dredge the meat in flour, tapping off any excess.
  15. Dip the meat in beaten eggs, allowing excess to drip off.
  16. Coat the meat in breadcrumbs, pressing gently to ensure they adhere.
  17. For a double-coated breading, repeat steps 3-4.
  18. Mustard Breading:
  19. Season the meat with salt and pepper.
  20. Brush the meat with mustard using a pastry brush.
  21. Press the meat into breadcrumbs.
  22. Butter Breading:
  23. Melt clarified butter.
  24. Brush the meat with melted butter.
  25. Press the meat into breadcrumbs.
  26. Shallow Fry:
  27. Heat 2 tablespoons of sunflower oil in a pan over medium heat.
  28. Gently place the breaded meat in the pan.
  29. Cook until golden brown and cooked through.
  30. Remove the meat from the pan and place on a plate lined with paper towels to absorb excess oil.

Tips:

  • Use a sturdy chopping board and a heavy pan for flattening meat.
  • Ensure all ingredients for mayonnaise are at room temperature.
  • Whisk in oil gradually to prevent the mayonnaise from splitting.
  • For a double-coated breading, repeat steps 3-4.
  • Use a pastry brush to apply mustard for mustard breading.
  • Use clarified butter for butter breading.
  • Cook the breaded meat over medium heat to prevent burning.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=fJSda6u7suQ

floating_island.txt - Floating Island

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French dessert called Floating Island.
  • Master the art of making French custard.
  • Discover how to cook meringues in water for a unique texture.

Ingredients

  • 4 eggs
  • 500 ml milk
  • 200 g caster sugar
  • 1 vanilla pod
  • 30 g water
  • 100 g white sugar
  • 1/4 cup water
  • Almonds (for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Make the custard:
  2. Heat half the milk in a saucepan over medium-high heat.
  3. Split the vanilla pod in half and scrape out the seeds.
  4. Add the vanilla pod and seeds to the milk and bring to a boil.
  5. Separate the egg yolks from the whites, reserving the whites for later.
  6. In a bowl, whisk together the egg yolks and 100 g of sugar until pale and creamy.
  7. Gradually whisk in a small amount of the hot milk, then add the remaining milk, ensuring it is not boiling hot.
  8. Return the mixture to the saucepan and cook over medium heat, stirring constantly, until the custard thickens and coats the back of a spoon.
  9. Remove from heat and let cool.
  10. Make the meringues:
  11. In a food processor or mixer, beat the egg whites with a pinch of salt until foamy.
  12. Gradually add 50 g of sugar and continue beating until stiff peaks form.
  13. Using an ice cream scoop, drop spoonfuls of meringue into a pot of simmering water.
  14. Cook for 1 minute on each side, then remove and place on a plate lined with kitchen paper to absorb excess water.
  15. Make the caramel sauce:
  16. Combine 100 g of white sugar and 1/4 cup of water in a saucepan over high heat.
  17. Bring to a boil and cook until the caramel turns a deep brown color.
  18. Immediately remove from heat and pour into a bowl of cold water to stop the cooking process.
  19. Assemble the dessert:
  20. Pour a small amount of custard into the bottom of a serving dish.
  21. Arrange the meringues on top of the custard.
  22. Drizzle with caramel sauce.
  23. Garnish with toasted almonds (optional).
  24. For the fine dining version:
  25. Pour custard into a cocktail glass.
  26. Add one meringue to the glass.
  27. Drizzle generously with caramel sauce.
  28. Sprinkle with toasted almonds.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=w-QgqIj1zVc

foie_gras_sauce.txt - Foie Gras Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French foie gras sauce.
  • Understand the importance of reducing the sauce for optimal flavor and texture.
  • Discover the secrets to creating a smooth and luxurious sauce.

Ingredients

  • 100g foie gras
  • 1 tablespoon of butter
  • 1/2 cup of white wine
  • 1/4 cup of chicken stock
  • 1/4 teaspoon of salt
  • 1/4 teaspoon of black pepper

Instructions

  1. Heat a small saucepan over medium heat.
  2. Add the foie gras and melt slowly, stirring occasionally.
  3. Add the butter and continue to stir until melted.
  4. Add the white wine and chicken stock, bring to a simmer and reduce by half.
  5. Season with salt and pepper to taste.
  6. Continue to simmer until the sauce has thickened to your desired consistency.
  7. Serve immediately over your favorite dish.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=x-s9Cd9KkEs

forest_bbq.txt - Forest BBQ

Objectives

  • Visit a friend who lives remotely in a forest near Melbourne.
  • Enjoy a barbecue with homemade burgers and calamari.
  • Learn about winemaking and explore a forest garden.

Ingredients

  • Calamari
  • Olive oil
  • Pepper
  • Vinegar
  • Wine
  • Homemade burgers
  • Parsley
  • Onions
  • Eggs
  • Breadcrumbs
  • Balsamic vinegar
  • Tomatoes
  • Cucumbers
  • Eggplant
  • Basil
  • Zucchini

Instructions

  1. Heat the barbecue to a high temperature.
  2. Season the calamari with pepper, olive oil, and vinegar.
  3. Place the calamari on the barbecue and cook for 5 minutes until browned.
  4. While the calamari is cooking, prepare the homemade burgers.
  5. Combine minced onions, parsley, eggs, and breadcrumbs in a bowl.
  6. Shape the mixture into patties and place them on the barbecue.
  7. Cook the burgers until they are cooked through.
  8. To assemble the burgers, place a burger patty on a bun, add desired toppings, and drizzle with balsamic vinegar.
  9. Enjoy the barbecue feast with calamari, burgers, and wine.
  10. Take a tour of the forest garden and learn about native Australian plants.
  11. Observe the chickens and collect fresh eggs.
  12. Sample the homemade wine and learn about the winemaking process.
  13. Enjoy the beautiful scenery and the fresh air.

forest_mushroom_rice.txt - Forest Mushroom Rice

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple and delicious mushroom rice using forest mushrooms.
  • Understand the importance of proper mushroom preparation and cleaning.
  • Master the technique of creating a paper lid for perfect rice cooking.

Ingredients

  • 1 cup of rice
  • 1/2 cup of parsley
  • 2 cloves of garlic
  • 1 sprig of fresh thyme
  • 1 onion
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 300g of fresh forest mushrooms
  • 1 tablespoon of olive oil
  • Salt to taste
  • 1 1/2 cups of water
  • Parchment paper

Instructions

  1. Clean the forest mushrooms using a brush and a little bit of water. Avoid soaking them as they absorb water and become mushy.
  2. Trim the ends of the mushrooms.
  3. Dice the onion vertically and then into small cubes.
  4. Chop the parsley leaves, separating them from the stems.
  5. Slice the mushrooms into thick pieces, ensuring they have a flat surface for cooking.
  6. Heat a tablespoon of olive oil in a pan over medium-high heat.
  7. Once the pan is hot, add the mushrooms and season with salt.
  8. Reduce the heat and add the garlic and parsley. Cook for 1-2 minutes to release the flavors.
  9. Set the mushroom mixture aside.
  10. In a separate saute pan, heat 3 tablespoons of olive oil over medium-high heat.
  11. Add the diced onion and cook for 2 minutes.
  12. Add the bay leaf and the pan-fried mushrooms.
  13. Pour in the rice and stir everything together.
  14. Reduce the heat and cook the rice until it becomes slightly translucent.
  15. Pour in 1 1/2 cups of water.
  16. Increase the heat slightly and bring the mixture to a light boil.
  17. Create a paper lid using parchment paper:
  18. Fold the parchment paper in half.
  19. Fold it in half again.
  20. Cut a hole in the center of the folded paper, about half the diameter of the pan.
  21. Unfold the paper to create a lid with a hole in the center.
  22. Place the paper lid over the rice mixture.
  23. Cover the pan with a regular lid and transfer it to a preheated oven at 190 degrees Celsius (375 degrees Fahrenheit) for 15-17 minutes.
  24. Remove the pan from the oven and let it rest for 5 minutes.
  25. Fluff the rice with a fork and serve.

Enjoy your delicious and simple forest mushroom rice!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=eYyIDTMmmsM

forest_mushroom_sauce_rabbit_steak.txt - Forest Mushroom Sauce with Rabbit Steak

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare and clean various types of mushrooms.
  • Master the art of creating a flavorful, creamy forest mushroom sauce.
  • Combine the sauce with a pan-fried rabbit steak for a delicious meal.

Ingredients

  • 1 rabbit steak
  • 1 shallot
  • 1/2 cup of heavy cream
  • 1/4 cup of reduced stock
  • 1 tablespoon of butter
  • 1/2 cup of button mushrooms
  • 1/2 cup of chanterelle mushrooms
  • 1/4 cup of shiitake mushrooms
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • Parsley for garnish

Instructions

  1. Clean and trim the mushrooms.
    • Button mushrooms: Trim the ends and rinse.
    • Chanterelle and shiitake mushrooms: Trim the ends, brush with a pastry brush, and rinse quickly.
  2. Heat a pan over medium heat.
  3. Melt butter in the pan and add shallots.
  4. Sweat the shallots until fragrant.
  5. Add button mushrooms, chanterelle mushrooms, and shiitake mushrooms to the pan.
  6. Cook the mushrooms until they release some of their moisture, but don't let them dry out completely.
  7. Add heavy cream to the pan and bring to a simmer.
  8. Reduce the cream for about 10 minutes until it thickens.
  9. Add reduced stock to the sauce and simmer until it reaches desired consistency.
  10. Season with salt and pepper to taste.
  11. Heat a pan over medium heat and add butter and oil.
  12. Sear the rabbit steak for 3-4 minutes per side, aiming for a medium-rare doneness.
  13. Remove the steak from the pan and rest on a plate covered with foil.
  14. Add the pan juices from the steak to the mushroom sauce.
  15. Reduce the sauce over low heat.
  16. Garnish the steak with parsley.
  17. Pour the sauce over the steak and serve immediately.

forty_cloves_garlic_chicken.txt - 40 Cloves Garlic Chicken

Objectives

  • Learn a bistro-style recipe for 40 cloves garlic chicken.
  • Cook chicken thighs with whole garlic cloves for a unique flavor.
  • Create a simple, flavorful sauce with white wine and cognac.

Ingredients

  • 1 kilo chicken thighs
  • 30 cloves garlic
  • 1 glass dry white Sauvignon Blanc
  • Salt and pepper
  • Butter
  • Oil
  • Cognac
  • Fresh parsley

Instructions

  1. Heat a pan with a mix of oil and butter over medium heat.
  2. Brown the chicken thighs, skin-side down, for 5-6 minutes.
  3. Flip the chicken and add the whole garlic cloves.
  4. Cook for 10-15 minutes, ensuring the garlic is submerged in the butter and oil.
  5. Increase heat to high and add cognac for a flambe.
  6. Once the flames die down, cook for another 10 minutes.
  7. Remove the chicken and deglaze the pan with white wine, scraping up any browned bits.
  8. Reduce the wine slightly.
  9. Return the chicken to the pan, resting it on top of the garlic cloves.
  10. Simmer for 10 minutes, or until the chicken is cooked through.
  11. Serve the chicken with some of the garlic and sauce, or create a creamy garlic sauce by adding 4 cloves of caramelized garlic and a tablespoon of cream to the sauce.
  12. Garnish with fresh parsley.

four_quarter_cake.txt - Four Quarter Cake

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple, versatile cake known as the "Four Quarter Cake"
  • Understand the importance of weighing ingredients for consistent results
  • Discover the secrets to a moist and fluffy cake texture

Ingredients

  • 3 eggs (separated into yolks and whites)
  • 160 grams sugar
  • 160 grams salted butter
  • 160 grams all-purpose flour
  • Grand Marnier or other flavoring (optional)

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 200 degrees Celsius (400 degrees Fahrenheit).
  2. Grease and flour a rectangular cake tin.
  3. Melt the butter over low heat. Set aside.
  4. Beat egg whites with a pinch of salt and a squeeze of lemon juice until stiff peaks form. Refrigerate.
  5. In a mixing bowl, beat egg yolks and sugar together until light and fluffy.
  6. Gradually add melted butter to the yolk mixture, mixing well after each addition.
  7. Fold in flour gradually, mixing until just combined.
  8. Gently fold in the whipped egg whites until just incorporated.
  9. Add desired flavoring (e.g., Grand Marnier, vanilla extract, orange zest).
  10. Pour batter into prepared cake tin.
  11. Bake for 15 minutes at 200 degrees Celsius.
  12. Reduce oven temperature to 180 degrees Celsius (350 degrees Fahrenheit) and bake for an additional 25 minutes.
  13. Allow cake to cool slightly before inverting onto a wire rack to cool completely.
  14. Slice and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=KFrQAHf1lc0

french_aperitif_dips.txt - French Aperitif Dips: Aioli & Tapenade

Objectives

  • Learn to make two classic French aperitif dips: aioli and tapenade.
  • Understand the importance of using fresh ingredients and proper techniques.
  • Explore the flavors and textures of these dips with toasted bread.

Ingredients

Aioli

  • 14 garlic cloves
  • 1 tablespoon vinegar
  • Olive oil (about 100 ml)
  • 1 tablespoon anchovies, filleted
  • Parsley, chopped
  • Basil, chopped

Tapenade

  • 1 cup black olives, pitted
  • 1 tablespoon capers
  • 1 clove garlic
  • 1 tablespoon anchovies, filleted
  • 1 tablespoon Dijon mustard
  • 1 tablespoon cognac
  • Olive oil
  • Black pepper

Instructions

Aioli

  1. Prepare ingredients: Chop garlic, parsley, and basil.
  2. Combine in mortar: Add garlic, vinegar, and a small amount of olive oil to a pestle and mortar.
  3. Grind ingredients: Grind the mixture together using a circular motion with the pestle.
  4. Add anchovies: Add anchovies and continue grinding until a smooth paste forms.
  5. Incorporate olive oil: Gradually drizzle in olive oil while grinding, incorporating it into the paste.
  6. Adjust consistency: Continue adding olive oil until the desired thickness is reached.
  7. Chill: Transfer to a container and refrigerate for at least 10-15 minutes to allow flavors to meld.

Tapenade

  1. Combine ingredients: In a food processor, combine olives, capers, garlic, anchovies, Dijon mustard, cognac, and a small amount of olive oil.
  2. Pulse ingredients: Pulse the mixture until a rough paste forms.
  3. Add remaining olive oil: Gradually add more olive oil while pulsing until the desired consistency is reached.
  4. Season: Adjust seasoning with salt, pepper, and additional olives if needed.
  5. Chill: Transfer to a container and refrigerate for at least 10-15 minutes to allow flavors to meld.

Serving

  1. Toast bread: Toast slices of baguette under the broiler.
  2. Spread dips: Spread aioli and tapenade onto the toasted bread.
  3. Enjoy: Serve with a glass of white wine.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Lx7G2xgarc4

french_apple_tart.txt - French Apple Tart

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French apple tart.
  • Master the technique of laying down the apple slices.
  • Discover the importance of using quality ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 5 apples
  • 1 lemon
  • Shortcrust pastry (made previously)
  • 2 eggs
  • 1 egg yolk
  • 300 ml cream
  • 50 grams sugar
  • Vanilla extract

Instructions

  1. Peel the apples and immediately apply lemon juice to prevent browning.
  2. Core the apples using a core remover.
  3. Lay out the shortcrust pastry on a floured surface, keeping it in a square shape.
  4. Roll the pastry around a rolling pin to transfer it to a tart pan.
  5. Butter the bottom of the tart pan and press the pastry into the sides.
  6. Trim any excess dough and prick the bottom of the pastry with a fork.
  7. In a bowl, whisk together two eggs, one egg yolk, cream, sugar, and a few drops of vanilla extract.
  8. Refrigerate the egg mixture for 10 minutes.
  9. Cut the apples into quarters.
  10. Arrange the apple quarters around the edges of the tart pan, overlapping slightly.
  11. Pour the egg mixture over the apples.
  12. Bake the tart in the oven at 350 degrees Fahrenheit for 35 minutes.
  13. Let the tart cool slightly before serving.
  14. Dust with icing sugar for presentation.

french_baguette_101.txt - French Baguette 101

Objectives

  • Learn the basics of French baguette making
  • Understand the key ingredients and equipment needed
  • Explore the importance of proper fermentation and cooking techniques

Ingredients

  • 250 grams all-purpose flour
  • 3 grams instant dry yeast
  • 5 grams sea salt
  • 175 grams water (temperature dependent)

Instructions

  1. Combine water and salt in a bowl and mix until salt is dissolved.
  2. Add flour to the bowl.
  3. Attach dough hook to KitchenAid mixer.
  4. Add water and salt mixture to flour.
  5. Mix on speed 2 for 2-3 minutes, until flour is fully incorporated.
  6. Cover the bowl with plastic wrap and let rest at room temperature for 45 minutes.
  7. Add yeast to the dough.
  8. Knead dough in KitchenAid mixer on speed 2 for 8 minutes.
  9. Transfer dough to a lightly floured bowl.
  10. Cover the bowl with plastic wrap and let rest at room temperature for 1 hour.
  11. Lightly flour a work surface.
  12. Turn dough out onto the surface.
  13. Fold the edges of the dough inward to form a ball.
  14. Place dough back in the bowl, cover with plastic wrap, and let rise for 2 hours at room temperature.
  15. Transfer dough to the refrigerator and let rise overnight.
  16. Lightly flour a work surface.
  17. Turn dough out onto the surface and gently press to remove excess air.
  18. Fold dough into a rectangle shape.
  19. Fold the sides inward to create a rounded shape.
  20. Place dough on parchment paper and let rest for 20-30 minutes.
  21. Preheat oven to 255 degrees Celsius (500 degrees Fahrenheit).
  22. Place a baking sheet in the oven and heat until the desired temperature is reached.
  23. Add water to the baking sheet to create steam.
  24. Lightly flour the dough and shape into a baguette.
  25. Score the baguette with a sharp knife.
  26. Place the baguette on the parchment paper and slide it onto the hot baking sheet.
  27. Bake for 20-25 minutes, or until golden brown.
  28. Let cool for 5-10 minutes before slicing and serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=GHbj3R5qSUE

french_baguette_sandwiches.txt - French Baguette Sandwiches

Objectives

  • Learn how to make three classic French baguette sandwiches
  • Understand the importance of fresh ingredients and proper bread selection
  • Explore the unique flavors and textures of French cuisine

Ingredients

  • French Baguette
  • Unsalted Butter
  • Dry Sausage (Saucisson)
  • Ham
  • Countryside Pate
  • Gherkins

Instructions

  1. Slice the French baguette in half, leaving it connected at the bottom.
  2. Spread a thin layer of unsalted butter on one half of the baguette using a wooden knife.
  3. For the ham sandwich:
    • Place a generous amount of ham on the buttered side of the baguette.
    • Close the sandwich and hold it together.
  4. For the dry sausage sandwich:
    • Spread a thin layer of unsalted butter on one half of the baguette.
    • Layer slices of dry sausage on the buttered side.
    • Close the sandwich and hold it together.
  5. For the pate sandwich:
    • Open the baguette slightly wider than the other sandwiches.
    • Place a few pieces of countryside pate on the baguette.
    • Add a few gherkins on top of the pate.
    • Close the sandwich and press gently to compact the ingredients.
  6. Enjoy your French baguette sandwiches with a glass of wine!

french_bean_soup.txt - French Bean Soup with Pancetta and Mushrooms

Objectives

  • Recreate a classic French bean soup inspired by chef Joël Robuchon.
  • Learn how to properly prepare and cook white beans for a creamy soup.
  • Understand the importance of layering flavors with pancetta and mushrooms.

Ingredients

  • 1 cup dried white beans (soaked for at least 2 hours)
  • 1 onion, chopped
  • 2 cloves garlic, crushed
  • 1/2 carrot, chopped
  • 1/2 cup pork belly, diced
  • 1 tablespoon duck fat (optional)
  • 4 cups chicken broth
  • 1/4 cup dried porcini mushrooms (soaked for 1-2 hours)
  • 1/4 cup pancetta, thinly sliced
  • 1/4 cup heavy cream
  • 1 tablespoon crushed garlic
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • Whipped cream (for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Blanch the soaked white beans by bringing them to a boil in a pot of water.
  2. Drain the beans and rinse them under cold water.
  3. Return the beans to the pot and add the chopped onion, garlic, carrot, diced pork belly, and duck fat (if using).
  4. Cover the ingredients with cold water, ensuring all are submerged.
  5. Bring the pot to a boil, then reduce heat to a simmer and cover.
  6. Cook the beans for 1-2 hours, or until tender, checking periodically. Do not add salt until 3/4 of the way through cooking.
  7. Once cooked, remove the garnish (onion, carrot, pork belly) and set aside.
  8. Drain the beans, reserving the cooking liquid.
  9. Puree the cooked beans in a blender until smooth.
  10. Transfer the pureed beans to a clean pot and add the reserved cooking liquid and chicken broth.
  11. Blend again to combine thoroughly.
  12. Pass the soup through a sieve to remove any remaining bean skins.
  13. Return the soup to the pot and add heavy cream.
  14. Heat the soup gently over medium heat until warmed through.
  15. In a separate pan, sauté the thinly sliced pancetta over low heat until crispy.
  16. Add the soaked and drained porcini mushrooms to the pancetta and cook until softened.
  17. Season the soup with crushed garlic, salt, and pepper to taste.
  18. Stir in the cooked pancetta and mushrooms.
  19. Whip heavy cream until stiff peaks form.
  20. Gently fold the whipped cream into the soup.
  21. Serve the soup warm, garnished with additional whipped cream.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=AXwXfCZzesU

french_canary_madera_sauce.txt - French Canary Madeira Sauce

Objectives

  • Explore the fundamentals of French pan sauces.
  • Learn how to create a delicious Madeira sauce from scratch.
  • Understand the key components of a classic French pan sauce.

Ingredients

  • 1 beef steak (approx. 200g)
  • 200 mL beef stock
  • 3 button mushrooms
  • 1 teaspoon shallots (finely diced)
  • 25 mL Madeira wine
  • Salt and pepper
  • 1 tablespoon olive oil
  • 1 tablespoon butter
  • 1/2 teaspoon fresh Madeira wine
  • Chopped parsley (optional)

Instructions

  1. Heat the beef stock in a small saucepan and bring to a boil for 1-2 minutes to sterilize it.
  2. Slice the mushrooms thinly, quartering or squaring them as desired.
  3. Heat a pan over medium-high heat. Add the olive oil and butter and pan-fry the mushrooms until they are lightly browned.
  4. Season the steak with salt and pepper.
  5. Heat a pan over medium-high heat. Add a tablespoon of sunflower oil and wait for it to shimmer before adding the steak.
  6. Sear the steak for 2-3 minutes on each side, ensuring a good caramelized crust forms.
  7. Remove the steak from the pan and set aside on a plate, covering with foil to keep warm.
  8. Reduce the heat to low and add the diced shallots to the pan. Cook until softened, about 1 minute.
  9. Deglaze the pan with the Madeira wine, scraping up any caramelized bits from the bottom. Reduce the wine until almost dry.
  10. Add the heated beef stock to the pan and bring to a boil. Reduce the sauce until it thickens and becomes syrupy.
  11. Add the pan-fried mushrooms to the sauce and stir to coat.
  12. Remove the pan from the heat.
  13. Add the butter to the sauce, swirling it in gently to melt and create a smooth, glossy texture.
  14. Stir in the 1/2 teaspoon of fresh Madeira wine.
  15. Arrange the steak on a plate, drizzle with the Madeira sauce, and garnish with mushrooms and parsley (optional).
  16. Serve immediately with fries or your favorite side dish.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6OTNDlRu2Sw

french_cheese_beignets.txt - French Cheese Beignets

Objectives

  • Learn to make simple French cheese beignets using a few ingredients.
  • Understand the importance of resting the dough before frying.
  • Discover a new way to use fresh cheese in a sweet treat.

Ingredients

  • 250g fresh cheese (fromage blanc, cottage cheese, ricotta, or quark)
  • 1 egg + 1 egg yolk
  • 1/2 cup sugar
  • 1 cup all-purpose flour, plus extra for dusting
  • Sunflower oil for frying

Instructions

  1. Drain the fresh cheese in a fine-mesh sieve to remove excess water.
  2. In a bowl, whisk together the drained cheese, sugar, and egg + yolk until smooth.
  3. Gradually whisk in the flour until a thick, non-runny batter forms.
  4. Cover the batter with plastic wrap and refrigerate for at least 1 hour to allow the flour to absorb moisture.
  5. Heat 1.2 liters of sunflower oil in a deep fryer or large saucepan to 170 degrees Celsius.
  6. Use two spoons to scoop out portions of the batter and drop them into the hot oil.
  7. Fry the beignets for 5-7 minutes, until golden brown and puffed.
  8. Remove the beignets from the oil and drain on paper towels.
  9. While still warm, roll the beignets in granulated sugar to coat.
  10. Serve immediately and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=N258kreF_gQ

french_cheese_rolls.txt - French Cheese Rolls

Objectives

  • Learn how to make French cheese rolls, a classic French snack.
  • Master the technique of creating a hollow puff pastry tube.
  • Understand the importance of proper puff pastry preparation to prevent over-puffing.

Ingredients

  • Puff pastry sheets
  • 1 egg (for egg wash)
  • Butter
  • Flour
  • Milk
  • 1/2 red onion
  • Cloves
  • 2 bay leaves
  • Salt
  • Black pepper (or white pepper)
  • Mushrooms
  • Cayenne pepper
  • Gruyère cheese
  • Ham

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 390°F (200°C).
  2. Unroll puff pastry sheets and measure the width of the baking tube.
  3. Cut a strip of puff pastry the same width as the tube.
  4. Roll the puff pastry around the tube, pressing it firmly into place.
  5. Use egg wash to seal the inside seam of the pastry tube.
  6. Brush the entire tube with egg wash and decorate with a fork or knife.
  7. Bake the tubes for 15-20 minutes, until they are 3/4 cooked.
  8. While the tubes bake, make a roux by melting butter and whisking in flour. Cook for 1-2 minutes.
  9. Remove the roux from heat and let it cool completely.
  10. Warm milk in a saucepan and add red onion, cloves, bay leaves, salt, pepper, mushrooms, and cayenne pepper. Simmer for 10-15 minutes.
  11. Strain the flavored milk through a fine-mesh sieve.
  12. Add the cooled roux to the warm milk and whisk until thickened.
  13. Cook the bechamel for a few minutes, then add Gruyère cheese and stir until melted.
  14. Add ham to the bechamel and stir gently.
  15. Let the bechamel cool slightly, then transfer it to a piping bag.
  16. Fill the baked pastry tubes with the bechamel mixture.
  17. Top the filled tubes with grated cheese.
  18. Bake the assembled cheese rolls for 10 minutes at 180°C until the cheese is melted.
  19. Serve warm.

Notes:

  • If the puff pastry puffs too much, prick it with a fork before baking.
  • Use a silicone mat to prevent sticking.
  • If the bechamel sauce becomes too thick, add a little more milk.
  • The cheese rolls can be made ahead of time and reheated before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=B-4fP5a6RBw

french_chicken_soup.txt - French Chicken Soup

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French chicken soup with a creamy texture and unique cumin flavor.
  • Discover the secret ingredient that makes this soup a hangover cure.
  • Understand the importance of simmering the soup for a long time to achieve a rich, flavorful broth.

Ingredients

  • 1 whole chicken, broken down into parts (carcass, drumsticks, thighs, wings, and breast)
  • 1 large onion, sliced
  • 2 leeks, sliced
  • 2 carrots, sliced
  • 1 shallot, sliced
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 2 sprigs of thyme
  • 2 cloves of garlic
  • 1 tablespoon of butter
  • 1 tablespoon of rock salt
  • 1 teaspoon of white pepper
  • 1 teaspoon of cumin seeds
  • 4 cups of water
  • 1 bunch of parsley (leaves and stalks)
  • 200ml of heavy cream
  • Carrots for decoration (optional)
  • Croutons (optional)
  • Chicken breast for garnish (optional)

Instructions

  1. Break down the whole chicken into parts. Keep the carcass, drumsticks, thighs, and wings for the soup. Set aside the chicken breast for garnish or a second meal.
  2. Slice the onion, leeks, carrots, and shallot.
  3. Heat a large pot over medium-high heat.
  4. Add the butter to the pot and wait until it melts.
  5. Add all the sliced vegetables to the pot and sweat for 3-4 minutes, until they release their natural juices.
  6. Reduce the heat to medium and add the chicken pieces (excluding the carcass) to the pot.
  7. Mix the chicken with the vegetables and cook for 2 minutes.
  8. Season with salt, white pepper, and cumin seeds.
  9. Add 4 cups of water to the pot, ensuring the water level is just above the chicken.
  10. Add the chicken carcass to the pot.
  11. Add the parsley (leaves and stalks) to the pot.
  12. Raise the heat slightly and bring the mixture to a boil.
  13. Reduce the heat to a simmer and skim off any impurities that rise to the surface.
  14. Simmer the soup for 1 hour, or until the meat falls off the bone.
  15. Remove the chicken carcass, skin, and large pieces of parsley from the soup.
  16. Transfer the remaining chicken pieces to a separate container and let them cool.
  17. Use a stick blender to blend the soup until smooth.
  18. Filter the soup to remove any remaining solids.
  19. Heat the heavy cream in a separate saucepan until it comes to a simmer.
  20. Shred the chicken meat, removing any bones or brown bits.
  21. Add the shredded chicken to the soup or serve it separately.
  22. Add a pinch of cumin seeds to the soup.
  23. Serve the soup hot, garnished with shredded chicken, croutons, and parsley.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Z55TzKKxpyE

french_chocolate_mousse.txt - French Chocolate Mousse

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French chocolate mousse
  • Create a smooth and silky ganache
  • Incorporate egg whites into a fluffy meringue
  • Assemble the mousse and chill for optimal texture

Ingredients

  • 4 egg whites
  • 200g good-quality dark chocolate (70% cocoa)
  • 100ml heavy whipping cream
  • 50ml full cream milk
  • 50g caster sugar

Instructions

  1. Melt the chocolate using the double boiler technique:
    • Fill a small saucepan with water and bring to a simmer.
    • Turn off the heat and place a heat-proof bowl on top of the saucepan.
    • Add the chocolate to the bowl and let it melt gently with the residual heat.
  2. Heat the cream and milk in a small saucepan over medium heat.
    • Bring to a simmer, then immediately turn off the heat.
    • Set aside to cool slightly.
  3. While the chocolate and milk mixture are cooling, prepare the meringue:
    • Add egg whites, a pinch of salt, and caster sugar to a food processor or blender.
    • Blend until stiff peaks form.
  4. Once the chocolate is melted and the milk mixture is slightly cooled, pour the cream mixture into the chocolate and whisk until smooth.
  5. Gradually incorporate a small amount of the egg whites into the chocolate mixture using a whisk, ensuring a consistent texture.
  6. Fold in the remaining egg whites using a rubber spatula, gently incorporating them into the chocolate mixture.
  7. Pour the mousse into glasses or ramekins and refrigerate for at least 2-4 hours, preferably overnight.
  8. Decorate with fresh fruit, mint, or chocolate shavings before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=8iLcEUXTLKo

french_cocktail_sauce.txt - French Cocktail Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn to make the authentic French cocktail sauce.
  • Discover the simple ingredients and techniques for preparing this classic sauce.
  • Explore two ways to present prawns with the French cocktail sauce.

Ingredients

  • Homemade mayonnaise (link provided in video)
  • Ketchup
  • Cognac
  • Tabasco
  • Worcestershire sauce
  • Cayenne pepper

Instructions

  1. Add homemade mayonnaise to a bowl.
  2. Add a small amount of ketchup, ensuring the mixture doesn't become too red.
  3. Add a few drops of cognac, Tabasco, and Worcestershire sauce.
  4. Add a sprinkle of cayenne pepper.
  5. Mix all ingredients together with a spatula.
  6. For the home-style presentation:
  7. Slice an avocado in half.
  8. Pour cocktail sauce into the avocado halves.
  9. Add prawns, lettuce, and a sprinkle of cayenne pepper.
  10. For the cocktail version:
  11. Pour cocktail sauce into a cocktail glass.
  12. Add a lemon wedge for color.
  13. Arrange 3-4 prawns in the glass.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=HglBMzKHFsI

french_cooking_academy_health_and_safety.txt - French Cooking Academy: Health and Safety

Objectives

  • Emphasize the importance of safety in the kitchen.
  • Highlight the need for a clean and organized workspace.
  • Explain proper food handling practices to prevent contamination.

Instructions

  1. Always prioritize safety for yourself and others in the kitchen.
  2. Wear a clean, cotton uniform, avoiding loose clothing or jewelry.
  3. Use a clean apron made of cotton, always having one on hand.
  4. Tie long hair up to prevent it from falling into food.
  5. Remove all jewelry before cooking.
  6. Wash your hands thoroughly with soap and water before starting to cook.
  7. Maintain a clean and clutter-free workspace.
  8. Use fresh ingredients and check expiration dates on all food items.
  9. Store prepared food for no longer than 24 hours in the refrigerator.
  10. When thawing frozen food, transfer it to the refrigerator for at least a day before use.
  11. Never refreeze thawed food.

french_cooking_academy_scallops_in_shells.txt - Scallops in Shells

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French dish, "coquilles Saint-Jacques," featuring scallops in shells
  • Prepare a flavorful velouté sauce with fish stock, cream, and mushrooms
  • Create a visually appealing garnish with puff pastry and clams

Ingredients

  • 4 scallops
  • 30g butter
  • 30g flour
  • 1/2 liter fish stock
  • Cream
  • Shallots
  • Parsley
  • Mushrooms
  • Clams
  • White wine
  • Puff pastry
  • Salt
  • Pepper

Instructions

  1. Prepare the roux:
    • Melt butter in a pan over medium heat.
    • Add flour and stir until a paste forms.
    • Cook for 3-4 minutes, then remove from heat and set aside to cool.
  2. Make the duxelles:
    • Melt butter in a pan.
    • Add shallots and cook for 1-2 minutes.
    • Add mushrooms, salt, and pepper.
    • Cook until the mushrooms are dry and fragrant.
    • Stir in parsley and set aside to cool.
  3. Make the velouté:
    • Bring fish stock to a boil.
    • Gradually whisk in the cooled roux, starting with a small amount.
    • Add cream and simmer over low heat for 20-30 minutes, reducing the sauce by a quarter.
  4. Prepare the clams:
    • Melt butter in a pan.
    • Add shallots and parsley.
    • Add clams and white wine.
    • Bring to a boil, cover, and steam for 5 minutes.
    • Reserve the clam juices.
  5. Make the puff pastry garnish:
    • Roll out puff pastry and cut into circles or half-moon shapes.
    • Bake in the oven until golden brown.
  6. Cook the fish:
    • Melt butter in a pan.
    • Add shallots and cod fillets.
    • Season with salt and pepper.
    • Add fish stock and white wine, ensuring the wine doesn't touch the fish.
    • Simmer over low heat for 5 minutes, covering with parchment paper to create a steam pocket.
    • Transfer the pan to the oven and bake for 5-6 minutes at 180 degrees Celsius.
  7. Assemble the dish:
    • Place the scallop shells on a baking sheet lined with foil.
    • Fill each shell with a bed of velouté sauce.
    • Top with flaked cod and a sprinkle of breadcrumbs.
    • Broil in the oven for 5 minutes.
  8. Pan-fry the scallops:
    • Heat a pan over medium heat.
    • Add scallops and cook for 2-3 minutes per side.
  9. Plate the dish:
    • Arrange the broiled scallop shells on a plate.
    • Top with pan-fried scallops.
    • Garnish with the puff pastry shapes and clams.
  10. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=AxNmWk8Dy1g

french_cooking_basics.txt - French Cooking Basics

  • Understand the importance of having a reference book for French culinary techniques.

french_cooking_stock.txt - French Cooking Stock

Objectives

  • Understand the importance of using a good stock in French cooking
  • Learn how to make a basic French stock using readily available ingredients
  • Discover the difference between a common white stock and a more refined "chic" stock

Ingredients

  • 1.5 kg chicken bones
  • 1 kg chicken carcass
  • 1 carrot, roughly chopped
  • 1 onion, roughly chopped
  • 1 celery stalk, roughly chopped
  • 1 leek, roughly chopped
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 4-5 peppercorns
  • 2-3 sprigs of thyme
  • 3-4 sprigs of parsley
  • 1 tbsp salt

Instructions

  1. Combine all ingredients in a large pot.
  2. Cover with cold water, ensuring all bones and vegetables are submerged.
  3. Bring the pot to a boil over high heat.
  4. Skim off any foam that rises to the surface.
  5. Reduce heat to a simmer and maintain for 3-4 hours, or until the stock has reduced by half.
  6. Strain the stock through a fine-mesh sieve lined with cheesecloth.
  7. Discard the solids and store the stock in the refrigerator for up to 5 days or freeze for longer storage.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QyEQGvGHkJc

french_cooking_utensils.txt - French Cooking Utensils

Objectives

  • Discuss essential kitchen utensils for French cooking
  • Provide tips for choosing quality and useful tools
  • Emphasize the importance of fit-for-purpose utensils

Instructions

  1. Invest in a good quality set of utensils, as they will last longer and be more effective.
  2. Start with basic utensils: a metal spatula, a rubber spatula, a balloon whisk, wooden spoons, ladles of various sizes, and a rolling pin.
  3. Consider a set of kitchen tools that includes a sieve, a scoop, and a few different pans.
  4. Choose a whisk with a sturdy rubber grip for comfort and control.
  5. Look for utensils that are heat-resistant and non-stick, especially for preparing bowls and dishes.
  6. Invest in a few preparation bowls of different sizes, such as small, medium, and large.
  7. Purchase a lemon reamer or juice extractor for easy citrus juice extraction.
  8. Select a peeler with a pointy bit for removing eyes from potatoes and an articulated blade for peeling various shapes.
  9. Invest in a baking sheet, baking tray, and silicone mat for various baking needs.
  10. When selecting utensils, prioritize usefulness and fit for purpose.
  11. Avoid buying large kits with many utensils you may not use, as they can take up valuable storage space.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Q72tCcB8Nqs

french_crepes.txt - French Crepes

Objectives

  • Learn how to make classic French crepe batter
  • Understand the importance of resting the batter
  • Prepare the batter for a variety of crepe fillings

Ingredients

  • 1/2 liter full cream milk
  • 40 grams butter
  • 40 grams white sugar
  • 2 grams salt
  • 225 grams plain flour
  • 3 medium eggs
  • Optional: Liqueurs, orange peels, lemon peels

Instructions

  1. Wash hands thoroughly.
  2. Gather ingredients in clean containers.
  3. In a large bowl, sift the flour.
  4. Add salt and sugar to the flour and whisk together.
  5. Create a well in the center of the flour mixture.
  6. Crack the eggs into the well and gently whisk them into the flour.
  7. Gradually add the milk, whisking continuously to avoid clumps.
  8. Continue whisking until the batter is smooth and free of lumps.
  9. Melt the butter in a small pan over medium heat.
  10. Once the butter is melted, remove from heat.
  11. Pour the melted butter into the batter and whisk gently to combine.
  12. Add any desired flavorings, such as rum, orange peel, or lemon peel.
  13. Cover the batter with a clean cloth and let it rest for at least one hour, or up to two hours.
  14. When ready to cook, heat a crepe pan over high heat.
  15. Pour a thin layer of batter onto the hot pan and cook until golden brown.
  16. Flip the crepe and cook the other side until golden brown.
  17. Serve with your favorite fillings.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=hph-o63wlEo

french_crouton.txt - French Crouton

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a simple, yet delicious, French crouton.
  • Understand the importance of using fresh bread and avoiding hard crusts.
  • Learn how to fry croutons to achieve a crispy exterior and soft interior.

Ingredients

  • 1 loaf of country bread
  • Sunflower oil (or grapeseed oil)
  • Paper towels

Instructions

  1. Slice a portion of the country bread, removing any hard crusts.
  2. Cut the bread into small, even squares.
  3. Heat a metal pan over high heat.
  4. Pour sunflower oil into the pan, ensuring it reaches a high temperature before adding croutons.
  5. Add the croutons to the hot oil and fry, shaking the pan occasionally to ensure even browning.
  6. Fry until croutons are golden brown on one side, then flip and repeat on the other side.
  7. Remove croutons from the pan and place them on paper towels to absorb excess oil.
  8. Serve croutons with salad or other desired dishes.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=If2dmMgBUao

french_custard.txt - French Custard (Crème brûlée without the caramel)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple and delicious French custard without caramel.
  • Understand the importance of warming the milk to infuse vanilla flavor.
  • Learn how to bake the custard in a bain-marie to achieve a smooth and creamy texture.

Ingredients

  • 500 ml milk
  • 3 whole eggs
  • 3 egg yolks
  • 80-100 grams sugar
  • 1 vanilla bean

Instructions

  1. Warm the milk over medium heat.
  2. Add the vanilla bean to the milk and stir gently.
  3. Preheat the oven to 150 degrees Celsius (300 degrees Fahrenheit).
  4. In a separate bowl, whisk together the sugar, eggs, and egg yolks until well combined.
  5. Slowly pour a small amount of the warm milk into the egg mixture, whisking constantly to temper the eggs.
  6. Pour the remaining milk into the egg mixture and whisk until smooth.
  7. Strain the custard through a fine mesh sieve to remove any vanilla seeds or clumps.
  8. Pour the custard into individual ramekins or a baking dish.
  9. Place the ramekins in a larger baking dish.
  10. Pour warm water into the larger baking dish until it reaches halfway up the sides of the ramekins.
  11. Carefully slide the baking dish into the oven.
  12. Bake for 30-40 minutes, or until the custard is set and a knife inserted into the center comes out clean.
  13. Allow the custard to cool completely before refrigerating.
  14. To achieve a caramelized top, you can broil the custard for a short time under a preheated broiler.
  15. Serve chilled.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=YZGkP22gHPE

french_delicacies.txt - French Delicacies

Objectives

  • Explore regional specialties in the OSI region of France
  • Showcase local cheese, sausage, and sweet treats
  • Highlight the unique flavor profiles of regional products

Ingredients

  • Saucisson sec (dry pork sausage)
  • Mûre (local cheese)
  • Biscuits with salted caramel
  • Biscuits with crunchy hazelnuts
  • Flocons de Neige (snowflakes)
  • Coupet (puff pastry with apple compote)

Instructions

  1. Start with the most basic regional specialty: saucisson sec (dry pork sausage).
  2. Cut the sausage very thin, as the texture is dry and requires thin slices for optimal enjoyment.
  3. Notice the hints of pepper and the salty, slightly cured flavor.
  4. Pair the sausage with a gherkin or cornichon for a contrasting flavor profile.
  5. Move on to the Mûre cheese, a specialty of the OSI region.
  6. Cut the cheese into thin slices, as it is a pressed cheese with a compact texture.
  7. Enjoy the cheese with a piece of baguette or on its own, appreciating its slightly salty and nutty notes.
  8. Sample the biscuits with salted caramel, noting the fresh butter flavor and pronounced caramel nuggets.
  9. Try the biscuits with crunchy hazelnuts, experiencing the airy texture and the strong hazelnut taste.
  10. Indulge in the Flocons de Neige (snowflakes), a meringue-like treat inspired by the snowy Pyrenees.
  11. Enjoy the light, fluffy texture and the delicate sweetness of the snowflakes.
  12. Finish with the Coupet, a puff pastry filled with apple compote.
  13. Appreciate the smooth, slightly crunchy texture and the sweet apple filling.
  14. Enjoy the variety of regional specialties and continue exploring the diverse culinary landscape of France.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=rnKhue-sJXk

french_dressing.txt - French Dressing

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a classic French vinaigrette
  • Understand the importance of proper proportions in dressing
  • Explore variations of French dressing with mustard and shallots

Ingredients

  • 1 liter of oil
  • 30 centiliters of vinegar
  • 40 grams of mustard (optional)
  • Salt
  • Pepper

Instructions

  1. Start with vinegar. Add 1 tablespoon of red wine vinegar to a bowl.
  2. Dissolve salt in the vinegar.
  3. Add 3 tablespoons of sunflower oil.
  4. Gently mix the ingredients together.
  5. For a mustard version:
    • Add 1 tablespoon of red wine vinegar to a bowl.
    • Add 1 teaspoon of mustard.
    • Dissolve salt in the vinegar and blend the mustard with the other ingredients.
    • Add 3 tablespoons of sunflower oil.
    • Mix thoroughly.
  6. For a shallot version:
    • Add 1 tablespoon of red wine vinegar to a bowl.
    • Dissolve salt in the vinegar.
    • Add 3 tablespoons of sunflower oil.
    • Mix thoroughly.
    • Add finely chopped shallots to the dressing.
    • Let the dressing infuse for at least 10-15 minutes before using.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=gwT6ULmtNlk

french_family_chicken.txt - French Family Chicken

Objectives

  • Explore the history of home cooking in the 1800s and 1900s
  • Learn how to prepare a classic French roast chicken with potatoes, onions, garlic, and tomatoes
  • Understand the importance of proper chicken trussing and roasting techniques

Ingredients

  • 1 whole chicken (approximately 1.4 kilos)
  • 6-8 potatoes, peeled, washed, and cut into quarters
  • 2 onions, halved and sliced
  • 8 garlic cloves, peeled
  • 1/2 cup Roma tomatoes, halved
  • 1/4 cup flat leaf parsley
  • 1 sprig of thyme
  • 1 bay leaf
  • Salt
  • Lemon pepper
  • Olive oil
  • Butter

Instructions

  1. Season the chicken inside and out with salt and pepper.
  2. Stuff the chicken cavity with parsley, thyme, bay leaf, and 2-3 garlic cloves.
  3. Truss the chicken with string, ensuring the legs are tightly bound and the wings are secured.
  4. Cut off the gland at the end of the chicken's tail.
  5. Preheat the oven to 200 degrees Celsius (400 degrees Fahrenheit).
  6. Place the chicken in a roasting pan on its side for 15 minutes.
  7. Turn the chicken to the other side and roast for another 15 minutes.
  8. After 30 minutes, turn the chicken upright and add the potatoes around it.
  9. Season the chicken and potatoes with salt and lemon pepper.
  10. Drizzle olive oil over the chicken and potatoes.
  11. Place a piece of butter on top of the chicken.
  12. Roast for 15 minutes, then add the remaining garlic cloves to the pan.
  13. Gently turn the chicken over and roast for another 15 minutes.
  14. Add the onions and tomatoes to the pan.
  15. Mix the onions and tomatoes in the juices and roast for 25-30 minutes until the chicken is golden brown and cooked through.
  16. Serve the chicken with the potatoes, onions, tomatoes, and garlic.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=qaV7PgvDPTs

french_fish_fumet.txt - French Fish Fumet

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a flavorful French fish fumet from scratch.
  • Understand the importance of using fresh ingredients and proper cooking techniques.
  • Discover how to use fish fumet in various culinary applications.

Ingredients

  • 1 mirepoix (carrots, celery, onion)
  • 1 bouquet garni
  • Rock salt
  • Coarsely ground pepper
  • White wine (10 cm)
  • Organic butter
  • Fish bones (cut into manageable chunks)
  • Water (enough to cover the fish bones)

Instructions

  1. Cut the fish bones into manageable chunks that can fit into the stockpot.
  2. Prepare the aromatic base:
  3. Cut the onion in half and slice thinly.
  4. Slice the shallots thinly, following the lines.
  5. Cut the carrots into quarters, keeping them thin (max 1 cm wide).
  6. Heat a stockpot over medium-low heat.
  7. Add the butter and let it melt without browning.
  8. Add the sliced vegetables and stir.
  9. Sweat the vegetables for 3-4 minutes, without browning, to remove excess water.
  10. Add the fish bones and stir.
  11. Cook the fish bones and vegetables for another 3-4 minutes, without browning.
  12. Add the white wine and stir.
  13. Add enough water to cover the fish bones.
  14. Add the bouquet garni and a pinch of salt.
  15. Cover the stockpot and cook over low heat for 20-25 minutes.
  16. Strain the fish fumet:
  17. Use a ladle to remove excess liquid.
  18. Discard the fish bones.
  19. Strain the remaining liquid through a fine-mesh sieve into a clean pan.
  20. Use the fish fumet immediately or store it in the refrigerator for up to 24 hours.
  21. Freeze any leftover fish fumet in batches for future use.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=yZ-_vR5kBVY

french_fish_soup.txt - French Fish Soup

Objectives

  • Learn to make a traditional French fish soup
  • Understand the importance of using bottom-feeder fish for optimal flavor
  • Master the art of making aioli, a classic French sauce

Ingredients

  • 3 different types of bottom-feeder fish (rock fish, red garnet, school whiting, rockling)
  • 1 onion
  • 2 garlic cloves
  • 1 shallot
  • 1 tablespoon tomato paste
  • 1 pinch paprika
  • 1 pinch saffron threads
  • 1 star anise
  • 1 bouquet garni
  • 1 bunch parsley
  • 1 fennel bulb
  • 1 celery stalk
  • 2 carrots
  • 1 leek
  • Olive oil
  • Salt and pepper
  • 1 liter homemade fish stock
  • Cayenne pepper
  • Lemon juice
  • 2 egg yolks
  • 1 cheddar cheese

Instructions

  1. Prepare all ingredients by cutting vegetables and aromatic herbs and filleting the fish.
  2. Make a fish stock from scratch or use a good quality store-bought stock.
  3. Heat olive oil in a pan over medium-high heat.
  4. Add the bouquet garni, star anise, paprika, salt, and pepper.
  5. Sweat the vegetable mix for 5 minutes.
  6. Add all the fish fillets to the pan.
  7. Pour in the fish stock and bring to a boil.
  8. Add crushed garlic, tomato paste, and saffron threads.
  9. Simmer for 30 minutes.
  10. While the soup is cooking, prepare the aioli.
    • Crush garlic cloves.
    • Combine garlic with egg yolks, salt, pepper, cayenne pepper, and lemon juice.
    • Gradually whisk in olive oil until the mixture thickens.
  11. Once the soup is cooked, remove the bouquet garni and hard bits.
  12. Blend the soup with a hand blender and pass it through a sieve.
  13. Return the soup to the pan.
  14. Add the filleted rockling to the soup and cook for 15 minutes.
  15. Toast bread slices in the oven until crispy.
  16. Grate cheddar cheese.
  17. To serve, ladle the soup into bowls.
  18. Spread aioli on the toasted bread.
  19. Top with grated cheese.
  20. Enjoy the soup with the bread and aioli.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=fp9Lqx2EUco

french_fries_pom_noisette.txt - French Fries, Pom Noisette, and Pom P

Objectives

  • Learn how to make three different types of French fries: Pom Alumet, Pom P, and Pom Noisette
  • Master the techniques for preparing potatoes for frying
  • Understand the importance of two-stage frying for crispy fries

Ingredients

  • Large potatoes
  • Cold water
  • Vegetable oil for frying
  • Salt flakes
  • Homemade smoked chili mayo infused with lemon
  • Heinz ketchup

Instructions

  1. Prepare Pom Noisette (Hazelnut Potatoes)
  2. Use a melon baller to carve out small, round potatoes.
  3. Reserve the carved potatoes in cold water.
  4. Remove any excess potato bits and change the water.
  5. Prepare Pom Alumet (French Fries)
  6. Cut large potatoes into square shapes.
  7. Cut the potatoes into thin strips, approximately 0.5 cm thick.
  8. Reserve the fries in cold water.
  9. Prepare Pom P (Chunky Fries)
  10. Cut large potatoes into square shapes.
  11. Cut the potatoes into thicker slices, approximately 1 cm thick.
  12. Reserve the fries in cold water.
  13. Dry the Potatoes
  14. Rinse the potatoes thoroughly in cold water.
  15. Drain the potatoes and pat them dry with paper towels or a clean kitchen towel.
  16. First Fry (Blanching)
  17. Heat vegetable oil in a fryer to 160°C.
  18. Carefully add the fries to the hot oil.
  19. Fry for 3-4 minutes for Pom Alumet, 6-7 minutes for larger quantities.
  20. Remove the fries from the oil and let them cool on a wire rack or paper towels.
  21. Blanch Pom Noisette
  22. Place the Pom Noisette in a saucepan with cold water.
  23. Bring the water to a boil.
  24. Immediately remove the potatoes from the boiling water and reserve them in a clean container.
  25. Second Fry (Final Cook)
  26. Heat vegetable oil in a fryer to 175-180°C.
  27. Add the Pom Noisette, Pom P, and Pom Alumet to the hot oil.
  28. Fry until the potatoes are golden brown and crispy.
  29. Remove the fries from the oil and drain on a wire rack or paper towels.
  30. Serve
  31. Arrange the fries on a serving platter.
  32. Season with salt flakes.
  33. Serve with homemade smoked chili mayo infused with lemon and Heinz ketchup.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=-V4g9b5KJBk

french_hot_chocolate.txt - French Hot Chocolate

Objectives

  • Learn to make a gourmet French hot chocolate from scratch.
  • Infuse the milk with cinnamon bark for enhanced flavor.
  • Create a rich and silky chocolate texture.

Ingredients

  • 1/2 liter full cream milk
  • Organic dark chocolate with 70% cocoa content
  • Fresh cinnamon bark
  • Pinch of sugar
  • Vanilla extract
  • 1 tbsp cocoa powder
  • Pinch of salt

Instructions

  1. Heat a medium-high heat pan and add 1/2 liter of milk.
  2. Add cinnamon bark and vanilla extract to the milk.
  3. Bring the milk to a boil, then reduce heat to low and simmer for 10 minutes.
  4. Discard the cinnamon bark.
  5. Add 1 tablespoon of cocoa powder to the milk and stir until combined.
  6. Filter the milk mixture through a sieve into a clean pan.
  7. Add a pinch of sugar and a pinch of salt to the filtered milk.
  8. Add all of the chocolate pieces to the milk and stir until melted and smooth.
  9. Optional: Leave the heat on to thicken the chocolate further, or turn off the heat and serve immediately.
  10. To serve, pour the hot chocolate into a bowl and enjoy with a piece of bread.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=HTfokMC4Ho4

french_kish_lorraine.txt - French Kish Lorraine

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a classic French Kish Lorraine
  • Understand the importance of proper dough preparation and resting time
  • Discover a simple and delicious recipe for a savory custard filling

Ingredients

  • 200g bacon
  • 200g cheese (cheddar recommended)
  • 250ml milk
  • 250ml cream
  • 2 eggs
  • 2 egg yolks
  • Salt
  • Nutmeg
  • Cayenne pepper
  • Kish dough (recipe not included in this video)

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 200°C (425°F).
  2. Pan-fry 200g of bacon until crispy.
  3. Roll out kish dough and place in a baking dish.
  4. Use a fork to poke holes in the bottom of the dough to allow heat to circulate evenly.
  5. Refrigerate the dough to keep it firm.
  6. In a bowl, whisk together 250ml milk and 250ml cream.
  7. Add 2 whole eggs and 2 egg yolks to the milk and cream mixture.
  8. Season with salt, a pinch of nutmeg, and a pinch of cayenne pepper.
  9. Arrange bacon and cheese evenly in the prepared kish dough.
  10. Pour the custard mixture over the bacon and cheese, using a sieve to remove any egg shells or bits of egg.
  11. Add extra bacon on top for extra flavor.
  12. Bake for 30-35 minutes.
  13. Allow the kish to cool and rest for 30-45 minutes before cutting and serving. The custard should be firm and not watery.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=3a70SGBIGaU

french_lemon_tart.txt - French Lemon Tart

Objectives

  • Learn how to blind bake a sweet short crust pastry
  • Understand the difference between blind baking and regular tart baking
  • Master the technique of making a French-style lemon cream

Ingredients

Pastry Dough: - 200g plain flour - 100g unsalted butter, cold and cubed - 60g caster sugar - 1 egg yolk - 2 tablespoons ice-cold water

Lemon Cream: - 100g caster sugar - 100ml lemon juice - 250ml double cream - 2 large eggs - 2 large egg yolks - 2 tablespoons corn flour - 50g unsalted butter, softened

Other: - 1 teaspoon vanilla extract (optional) - Ceramic beads or dried beans for blind baking - Clear syrup for decoration (optional) - Lemon slices for decoration (optional)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the pastry dough:
  2. Combine flour, butter, sugar, egg yolk, and water in a bowl.
  3. Mix until a dough forms, then wrap and refrigerate for at least 30 minutes.
  4. Blind bake the tart shell:
  5. Preheat oven to 200°C (400°F).
  6. Roll out the dough on a lightly floured surface and line a 9-inch tart pan with a removable bottom.
  7. Trim excess dough and crimp the edges.
  8. Line the tart shell with parchment paper and fill with ceramic beads or dried beans.
  9. Bake for 20 minutes.
  10. Remove the beads and parchment paper, and bake for an additional 5-10 minutes until golden brown.
  11. Make the lemon cream:
  12. In a saucepan, combine sugar and lemon juice.
  13. Bring to a boil over medium heat, stirring constantly.
  14. In a separate saucepan, heat the cream to a simmer.
  15. In a bowl, whisk together eggs, egg yolks, and corn flour until smooth.
  16. Slowly whisk in the hot lemon syrup, followed by the hot cream.
  17. Return the mixture to the saucepan and cook over medium heat, stirring constantly, until thickened.
  18. Remove from heat and stir in the softened butter until smooth.
  19. Strain the cream through a fine-mesh sieve to remove any lumps.
  20. Let cool to room temperature.
  21. Assemble the tart:
  22. Pour the lemon cream into the cooled tart shell.
  23. Refrigerate for at least 2 hours or overnight.
  24. Decorate and serve:
  25. Before serving, brush the top of the tart with clear syrup (optional).
  26. Garnish with lemon slices (optional).
  27. Enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=0JAfUi4oZFU

french_marinade.txt - French Marinade (Marino Not Iku)

Objectives

  • Learn about the two main types of French marinades: "Marino Not Iku" and "Instant Marinade."
  • Understand how to make a traditional "Marino Not Iku" marinade using raw vegetables and wine.
  • Discover the benefits of marinating meat overnight for enhanced flavor.

Ingredients

  • Bouquet garni (fresh herbs, optional - can be substituted with dry bay leaf and thyme)
  • 1 onion, halved
  • 1 shallot, halved
  • 1 carrot, halved
  • 1 celery stalk, halved
  • 1 bottle of red wine (Burgundy Pinot Noir recommended)
  • 1 dash of cognac
  • Peanut oil (or other cooking oil)

Instructions

  1. Place half of the bouquet garni, onion, shallot, carrot, and celery at the bottom of a dish.
  2. Layer the meat pieces on top of the vegetables.
  3. Add the remaining bouquet garni, onion, shallot, carrot, and celery on top of the meat.
  4. Pour the bottle of red wine over the meat and vegetables.
  5. Add a dash of cognac.
  6. Cover the ingredients with peanut oil.
  7. Cover the dish tightly with plastic wrap and refrigerate for at least 12 hours, ideally overnight.
