lamb_ragout.txt - Lamb Ragout

Objectives

  • Learn to make a traditional French lamb ragout
  • Understand the importance of low and slow cooking for tender meat
  • Master the technique of thickening a sauce with flour

Ingredients

  • 1 shoulder of lamb, cut into pieces
  • 1 leek, white part only, sliced
  • 1 onion, sliced
  • 1 tablespoon butter
  • 1 tablespoon flour
  • 1 cup white wine
  • 1 cup water
  • 1 bouquet garni
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • 1/2 cup button mushrooms, sliced
  • 1/2 cup heavy cream
  • 2 egg yolks
  • 1 teaspoon lemon juice

Instructions

  1. Heat a large pan over medium-high heat. Add butter and brown the lamb pieces on all sides.
  2. Remove the lamb from the pan and set aside.
  3. Reduce heat to low and add butter to the pan. Add sliced leeks and onions and sweat for 5 minutes, stirring occasionally.
  4. Return the lamb to the pan and stir to combine.
  5. Add flour to the pan and stir to coat the lamb and vegetables.
  6. Add white wine, water, bouquet garni, salt, and pepper to the pan.
  7. Bring to a boil, then reduce heat to low and simmer for 30 minutes, covered.
  8. Add sliced mushrooms to the pan and stir to combine. Cover and cook for 10 minutes.
  9. Turn off the heat and remove the pan from the stove.
  10. In a separate bowl, whisk together heavy cream, egg yolks, and lemon juice.
  11. Gradually whisk in a small amount of the hot lamb ragout into the cream mixture until it is tempered.
  12. Pour the tempered cream mixture into the pan and stir to combine.
  13. Cook the sauce over low heat, stirring constantly, until it thickens to a coating consistency. Do not boil.
  14. Remove the bouquet garni from the pan.
  15. Serve the lamb ragout hot, with crusty bread for dipping.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=0Cv8Yw3pbBU

lamb_saute_chasser.txt - Lamb Saute Chasser

Objectives

  • Learn to use a splayed saute pan for cooking.
  • Master the art of searing meat for maximum flavor.
  • Create a delicious French lamb dish with a rich sauce.

Ingredients

  • Diced Lamb
  • Brown Stock
  • Mushrooms
  • Tarragon
  • Bay Leaf
  • Shallots
  • Tomato Paste
  • White Wine
  • Oil
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Flour
  • Butter
  • Parsley (optional)
  • Cognac (optional)

Instructions

  1. Heat the saute pan over high heat.
  2. Add a teaspoon of oil to the pan.
  3. Sear the diced lamb in batches, ensuring a nice brown crust forms on each piece.
  4. Remove the seared lamb and set aside.
  5. Add a teaspoon of oil to the pan and sauté thinly sliced shallots for 20-30 seconds.
  6. Deglaze the pan with a few tablespoons of white wine, reducing the heat to medium.
  7. Make a slurry by whisking together a teaspoon of flour and a teaspoon of butter.
  8. Add the slurry to the wine reduction, stirring until thickened.
  9. Return the seared lamb to the pan.
  10. Add a teaspoon of tomato paste and cook for a minute to remove the acidity.
  11. Pour in enough brown stock to cover the lamb, adding more wine or water if needed.
  12. Season with salt, pepper, and a bay leaf.
  13. Add a few sprigs of thyme.
  14. Cover the pan with a slightly ajar lid and simmer until the lamb is cooked through, about 15-30 minutes depending on the size of the lamb pieces.
  15. While the lamb is simmering, sauté mushrooms until golden brown.
  16. Add the sauteed mushrooms to the lamb mixture.
  17. Add a crushed garlic clove (optional).
  18. Continue cooking for 5-10 minutes, or until the sauce is thickened and the lamb is tender.
  19. Stir in a tablespoon of chopped tarragon and a pinch of parsley.
  20. Add a dash of cognac (optional).
  21. Taste and adjust seasoning as needed.
  22. Serve immediately.

lazy_sunday_beef_bourguignon.txt - Lazy Sunday Beef Bourguignon

Objectives

  • Learn to make a traditional French Beef Bourguignon.
  • Master the art of slow cooking for tender, flavorful meat.
  • Create a hearty, comforting dish perfect for a lazy Sunday.

Ingredients

  • 1 kg chuck steak, cubed (about 50g per piece)
  • 100g smoked bacon, diced
  • 1 onion, diced
  • 1 carrot, diced
  • 1 pickling onion, peeled
  • 1 bunch parsley
  • 2 cloves garlic
  • 30g plain flour
  • 1 bottle Pinot Noir (or similar Burgundy-style wine)
  • 500ml beef stock
  • 1 tablespoon olive oil
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • 4-5 potatoes, peeled and boiled
  • 1 small onion, sliced
  • 2 tablespoons butter
  • 1 tablespoon sugar
  • 200g mushrooms, sliced
  • Garlic and herb butter (optional)

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 240°C (450°F).
  2. Dice bacon, onion, carrot, and chuck steak into manageable cubes.
  3. Finely chop parsley and garlic together in a food processor.
  4. In a small pan, bring stock to a boil and reduce slightly.
  5. In another pan, bring wine to a boil and reduce slightly. Optionally, flambe the wine to remove excess alcohol.
  6. Heat olive oil in a large casserole dish over medium-high heat.
  7. Brown chuck steak pieces on all sides, ensuring a nice crust forms.
  8. Remove meat from pan and set aside.
  9. Add diced onion and carrot to the pan and cook until softened, about 5 minutes.
  10. Return meat to the pan and sprinkle 30g of flour over the meat and vegetables.
  11. Place the pan in the preheated oven for 4-5 minutes to toast the flour.
  12. Remove pan from oven and stir the flour into the juices to create a roux.
  13. Add the reduced stock and wine to the pan, ensuring the liquid level is just above the meat.
  14. Add 2 cloves of garlic, salt, and pepper to taste.
  15. Cover the pan and reduce oven temperature to 200°C (420°F).
  16. Cook for 2-2.5 hours, checking occasionally to ensure the liquid doesn't evaporate too much.
  17. While the stew cooks, prepare the garnish.
  18. Boil potatoes in salted water until tender.
  19. Caramelize onions by sautéing sliced onions in butter and sugar until golden brown.
  20. Pan-fry bacon until crispy and set aside on paper towels.
  21. Pan-fry mushrooms until golden brown and set aside.
  22. Melt butter in a pan and stir in the parsley and garlic mixture to create a garlic and herb butter (optional).
  23. After 2-2.5 hours, remove the stew from the oven.
  24. Carefully remove the meat from the stew and set aside.
  25. Strain the sauce through a fine-mesh sieve into a clean dish.
  26. To serve, arrange meat, gravy, mushrooms, bacon, and caramelized onions on a plate.
  27. Top with mashed potatoes and a drizzle of garlic and herb butter (optional).
  28. Garnish with parsley.

Enjoy your Lazy Sunday Beef Bourguignon!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=72pXASYZXoQ

leek_onion_kish.txt - Leek and Onion Kish

Objectives

  • Learn to make a traditional French quiche
  • Master the technique of sweating vegetables
  • Prepare a delicious and versatile leek and onion quiche

Ingredients

  • Short crust pastry (homemade, rested for 2 hours)
  • 2 onions
  • 1 leek
  • 250 ml full milk
  • 4 eggs (2 whole, 2 yolks)
  • 250 ml double cream
  • Salt
  • Nutmeg
  • Cayenne pepper
  • Butter
  • Bacon (optional)
  • Swiss cheese (optional)

Instructions

  1. Clean and wash all vegetables.
  2. Slice the leek very thinly.
  3. Dice the onions into small cubes.
  4. Sweat the leek and onions in butter over low heat for 10 minutes.
  5. Ensure the vegetables are cooked through but still retain some crunch.
  6. Transfer the cooked leek and onion mixture to a clean container.
  7. Roll out the pastry and line a quiche mold.
  8. Trim any excess pastry and prick the base with a fork.
  9. Prepare the quiche filling:
  10. Whisk together 4 eggs (2 whole, 2 yolks), 250 ml double cream, 250 ml milk, salt, nutmeg, and cayenne pepper.
  11. Garnish the quiche mold with your chosen ingredients:
  12. For the leek and onion quiche, use the cooked leek and onion mixture.
  13. For the Kish Lauren, use bacon and Swiss cheese.
  14. Pour the quiche filling evenly over the garnish, ensuring all vegetables are covered.
  15. Preheat oven to 180°C.
  16. Bake the quiche for 25 minutes at 180°C.
  17. Let the quiche rest for 15 minutes outside the oven before removing from the mold.
  18. Serve and enjoy!

leek_potato_soup.txt - Leek and Potato Soup

Objectives

  • Learn how to elevate a simple leek and potato soup to a restaurant-quality dish
  • Understand the importance of using high-quality ingredients
  • Learn how to create a smooth and creamy texture in a soup

Ingredients

  • 1 tablespoon olive oil
  • 1 onion, sliced
  • 1 leek, sliced
  • 2-3 potatoes, peeled and diced
  • 1 teaspoon cumin
  • A few saffron threads
  • 4 cups white chicken stock
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • 1/2 cup white wine
  • 2-3 tablespoons cream
  • A squeeze of lemon juice

Instructions

  1. Heat a tablespoon of olive oil in a large saucepan over medium heat.
  2. Add the sliced onion and cook for 3 minutes, or until softened.
  3. Add the sliced leek, diced potatoes, cumin, and saffron threads to the pan.
  4. Pour in 4 cups of white chicken stock.
  5. Season with salt and pepper to taste.
  6. Bring the soup to a simmer and cook for 20 minutes, or until the potatoes are tender.
  7. Reduce the heat to low and partially cover the pan.
  8. After 20 minutes, turn off the heat and allow the soup to cool slightly.
  9. Using a stick blender or a regular blender, blend the soup until smooth.
  10. Add the white wine and cream to the soup and mix well.
  11. Transfer the soup to another saucepan and heat over medium heat.
  12. Add a squeeze of lemon juice and adjust seasoning as needed.
  13. Serve hot, garnished with a drizzle of olive oil.

leek_preparation.txt - Leek Preparation

Objectives

  • Learn the proper French method for preparing leeks.
  • Understand the different uses of leeks in French cuisine.
  • Discover the nutritional benefits of leeks.

Ingredients

  • 1 leek

Instructions

  1. Remove any damaged or wilted leaves from the leek.
  2. Cut off the root end of the leek.
  3. Remove any extra leaves from the top of the leek.
  4. Make a small incision along the length of the leek, cutting through the outer skin.
  5. Peel off the outer layer of skin.
  6. Repeat steps 4 and 5 until all of the outer skin is removed.
  7. Use a paring knife to make an incision along the length of the leek on both sides.
  8. Rinse the leek thoroughly under running water, removing any dirt or debris.
  9. Cut off the green base of the leek and set it aside for later use.
  10. Finely chop the remaining leek for use in soups or stews.
  11. To make leek julienne, cut a small piece of the leek in half lengthwise.
  12. Cut the leek into very thin strips, about 1/8 inch thick.
  13. To prepare leeks for a vinaigrette, bundle several leeks together with kitchen string.
  14. Cook the leeks in salted boiling water until tender.
  15. Cool the leeks and serve with a vinaigrette.

leeks_in_two_ways.txt - Leeks in Two Ways

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare and cook leeks for two different French recipes.
  • Create a classic vinaigrette-dressed leek dish.
  • Make a creamy leek veloute with cider and cream.

Ingredients

Vinaigrette: - Leeks - Vinaigrette

Veloute: - Leeks - 1 Onion - 1 Lemon - 1 tbsp Butter - 1 tbsp Flour - Salt - White Pepper - Nutmeg - Cream - Cider

Instructions

  1. Trim the leeks, discarding the dark green portion and the root end.
  2. Cut the leeks into approximately equal lengths.
  3. Tie the leeks together with string to form a bundle.
  4. Boil the leeks in salted water until tender.
  5. While the leeks are cooking, prepare the veloute.
  6. Melt butter in a saucepan over low heat.
  7. Add sliced onion and cook until softened and slightly browned.
  8. Stir in flour to make a roux and cook for 1-2 minutes, stirring constantly.
  9. Slowly whisk in cider and bring to a simmer.
  10. Gradually add cream until desired consistency is reached.
  11. Season with salt, white pepper, and nutmeg to taste.
  12. Remove the leeks from the boiling water and let them rest until cool.
  13. Arrange the leeks in a serving dish.
  14. For the vinaigrette, pour the dressing over the leeks.
  15. For the veloute, pour the sauce over the leeks.
  16. Serve and enjoy!

lentil_salad.txt - Lentil Salad

Objectives

  • Create a simple and quick lentil salad inspired by Leon cuisine.
  • Transform a basic lentil salad into a visually appealing and appetizing starter.
  • Showcase a Parisian-style presentation for a simple lentil salad.

Ingredients

  • Brown lentils (pre-cooked or canned)
  • Bacon (thinly sliced and pan-fried)
  • Croutons (small, pan-fried)
  • Shallot (thinly sliced)
  • Mustard vinaigrette (recipe in a separate video)
  • Poached egg
  • Fresh parsley
  • Fresh vinegar
  • Freshly ground black pepper

Instructions

  1. Place cooked lentils in a bowl.
  2. Add thinly sliced shallots, reserving some for garnish.
  3. Add pan-fried bacon, reserving some for garnish.
  4. Pour mustard vinaigrette over the lentils, shallots, and bacon.
  5. Toss gently to coat all ingredients, being careful not to break the lentils.
  6. Let the salad sit for 5 minutes to allow the flavors to meld.
  7. Arrange the lentil mixture on a plate.
  8. Garnish with remaining shallots, bacon, and croutons.
  9. Top with a poached egg.
  10. Drizzle with fresh vinegar.
  11. Garnish with fresh parsley.
  12. Season with freshly ground black pepper.
  13. Serve immediately.

lentils_alla_dijonaise.txt - Lentils Alla Dijonaise

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple and delicious lentil dish with Dijon mustard and smoked pork belly.
  • Understand the importance of proper cooking time for lentils.
  • Discover how to use leftovers to create a lentil puree for another meal.

Ingredients

  • 300 grams green lentils
  • 900 grams water
  • 1 sliced carrot
  • 1 sliced onion
  • 1 clove garlic
  • 2 small bay leaves
  • 2 tablespoons Dijon mustard
  • 2 slices pork belly (good quality)
  • Salt
  • Butter

Instructions

  1. Rinse the lentils under cold water and place them in a stock pot.
  2. Add three times the volume of water to the lentils.
  3. Turn the heat to high and bring the water to a boil.
  4. Remove any impurities that float to the top.
  5. Add the sliced carrot, onion, garlic, bay leaves, and pork belly to the pot.
  6. Bring the mixture to a boil, then reduce the heat to low and simmer for 40 minutes with the lid on.
  7. Remove the garnish (carrot, onion, garlic, and bay leaves) and pork belly from the pot.
  8. Mix the Dijon mustard with some of the lentil cooking liquid to create a creamy mixture.
  9. Gently incorporate the mustard mixture into the lentils.
  10. Pan-fry the pork belly (optional).
  11. Serve the lentils on a plate with the pork belly, a knob of butter, and a little bit of the cooking liquid.
  12. Garnish with pepper and a touch of grainy mustard (optional).

Leftover Recipe

  • Use a stick blender to puree the leftover lentils for a delicious soup.
  • Alternatively, drain the lentils and use them in a vegetable meal or make a lentil mash.
  • Heat the lentil mash in a saucepan to remove excess moisture and use it as a side for chicken or red meat.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=TfflVyts3Xw

lentils_pork_belly.txt - Sauces all on T

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple, classic French dish called "Sauces all on T"
  • Prepare lentils with pork belly and aromatics
  • Enjoy a delicious combination of lentils and pork sausages

Ingredients

  • 1/2 onion
  • 2 carrots
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 1 clove
  • 1 teaspoon of salt
  • 1 teaspoon of thyme
  • 1 tablespoon of oil
  • 3 lentils (French style green lentils)
  • pork belly
  • pork sausages
  • butter

Instructions

  1. Cut the onion in half and reserve one half.
  2. Prick the clove with a fork to create a "hedgehog" shape.
  3. Slice the carrots into 1-centimeter thick pieces.
  4. Optionally, use a lemon zester to create decorative trenches in the carrots.
  5. Remove the rinds from the pork belly and dice it roughly.
  6. Rinse the lentils in cold water.
  7. Place the lentils in a bowl and set aside.
  8. Place the lentils, carrots, onion, thyme, bay leaf, and clove in a pot.
  9. Add enough water to cover the lentils.
  10. Bring the water to a boil.
  11. Remove any scum from the surface of the boiling water.
  12. Reduce heat to a simmer and cook for 20 minutes, partially covered.
  13. Check the lentils for impurities and add salt.
  14. Heat oil in a pan over low to medium heat.
  15. Add the sausages to the pan and cook gently.
  16. Once the lentils and sausages are cooked, serve the lentils with the sausages on top.
  17. Add a knob of butter to the lentils for a rich flavor.
  18. Enjoy!

macaroni_and_cheese_gratinee.txt - Macaroni and Cheese Gratin

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a French-style macaroni and cheese gratin.
  • Understand the importance of infusing cream and milk with garlic and spices.
  • Discover a simple and flavorful way to prepare a classic dish.

Ingredients

  • Macaroni pasta
  • Olive oil
  • Salt
  • Water
  • Full cream/heavy cream
  • Milk
  • Garlic
  • Nutmeg
  • Black pepper
  • Butter
  • Tomato slices
  • Grated cheese

Instructions

  1. Bring a pot of salted water to a boil.
  2. Add olive oil to the boiling water.
  3. Add macaroni pasta to the boiling water and cook until al dente.
  4. While the pasta is cooking, heat a pan over medium heat.
  5. Add full cream/heavy cream, milk, salt, pepper, garlic, and nutmeg to the pan.
  6. Bring the cream mixture to a boil, then reduce heat and simmer until the garlic flavors infuse.
  7. Drain the cooked macaroni and transfer to a large bowl.
  8. Add the cream mixture to the macaroni and mix well.
  9. Allow the macaroni to sit for a few minutes to absorb the cream mixture.
  10. Spread butter on the bottom and sides of a baking dish.
  11. Sprinkle the dish with garlic.
  12. Preheat oven to 180 degrees Celsius (356 degrees Fahrenheit).
  13. Transfer the macaroni mixture to the prepared baking dish.
  14. Season with salt and pepper.
  15. Sprinkle generously with grated cheese.
  16. Arrange tomato slices on top of the cheese.
  17. Bake for 25-30 minutes until the cheese is melted and bubbly.
  18. Let the gratin cool slightly before serving.
  19. Enjoy!

mackerel_escabeche.txt - Mackerel Escabeche

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare mackerel for escabeche.
  • Master the art of creating a flavorful marinade for mackerel.
  • Understand the importance of marinating the fish for 24 hours.

Ingredients

  • 50 ml olive oil
  • 4 cloves garlic, crushed
  • 1 teaspoon coriander seeds, crushed
  • 1/2 teaspoon black peppercorns
  • 1 onion, thinly sliced
  • 1 shallot, thinly sliced
  • 2 carrots, thinly sliced
  • 1/2 cup sherry vinegar
  • 1/2 cup apple cider vinegar
  • 1/2 liter white wine
  • Salt to taste
  • Juice of 1 lemon
  • 1 mackerel, trimmed and cleaned
  • Additional olive oil for sizzling

Instructions

  1. Thinly slice the onions, shallots, carrots, and garlic. Crush the coriander seeds.
  2. Heat 50 ml of olive oil in a pan over low heat.
  3. Add the garlic, crushed coriander seeds, and black peppercorns to the oil and infuse the flavors for a few minutes.
  4. Add the onions, shallots, and carrots to the pan and cook for 2 minutes, or until softened.
  5. Add the sherry vinegar and apple cider vinegar to the pan and bring to a boil.
  6. Add the white wine to the pan and bring to a boil again.
  7. Season with salt and add the lemon juice.
  8. Simmer the marinade for 5 minutes, then turn off the heat and set aside.
  9. Trim the mackerel, removing the skin from the belly and the tail.
  10. Season the mackerel with salt and pepper.
  11. Heat a small amount of olive oil in a pan over medium heat.
  12. Sizzle the mackerel on one side for 30 seconds, then transfer to a container.
  13. Repeat the sizzling process for the remaining mackerel.
  14. Pour the remaining olive oil over the mackerel in the container.
  15. Pour the warm marinade over the mackerel.
  16. Add the lemon slices to the container.
  17. Cover the container with parchment paper and refrigerate for 24 hours.
  18. Serve chilled.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=klR9WRF5EX0

madeleine_recipe.txt - French Madeleine

Objectives

  • Learn how to make authentic French Madeleines.
  • Discover the history and origin of the Madeleine.
  • Understand the key ingredients and techniques for perfect Madeleines.

Ingredients

  • Whole eggs
  • Honey
  • Baking powder
  • Plain flour
  • Butter
  • Lemon
  • Sugar

Instructions

  1. Crack eggs into a bowl and add sugar.
  2. Beat the egg mixture for 3-4 minutes until light and foamy.
  3. Add honey and continue beating for another 3-4 minutes.
  4. Melt butter in a pan and add a squeeze of lemon juice and a pinch of salt.
  5. Let the butter cool while sifting flour into a bowl.
  6. Add baking powder to the sifted flour.
  7. Slowly incorporate the cooled butter into the egg mixture, whisking until a smooth paste forms.
  8. Cover the batter and let it rest at room temperature for at least 2 hours.
  9. Preheat oven to 220°C (428°F).
  10. Grease a Madeleine pan with melted butter.
  11. Fill each mold in the pan three-quarters full with batter.
  12. Bake for the first 3 minutes at 220°C (428°F) for a "thermal shock."
  13. Reduce heat to 200°C (396°F) and bake for an additional 6-7 minutes.
  14. Remove Madeleines from the oven and allow to cool slightly before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=AxbVJGiZsnQ

make_butter.txt - Making Butter

Objectives

  • Learn how butter is made from cream
  • Understand the importance of using pure cream
  • Make your own butter using a stand mixer

Ingredients

300 ml pure cream

Instructions

  1. Pour 300 ml of pure cream into the bowl of a stand mixer.
  2. Beat the cream on high speed until it forms stiff peaks.
  3. Continue beating until the cream separates into a thick, yellow butter and a watery buttermilk.
  4. Remove the butter from the buttermilk using a wooden spoon.
  5. Rinse the butter under cold water to remove any excess buttermilk.
  6. Shape the butter as desired and enjoy.

maltese_sauce.txt - Maltese Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn how to transform a mother sauce into a daughter sauce
  • Understand the concept of mother sauces and their derivatives
  • Create a unique and flavorful Maltese sauce using blood orange and hollandaise

Ingredients

  • 1 blood orange (for juice and zest)
  • 1 tablespoon clarified butter
  • 2 egg yolks
  • 1 tablespoon water
  • 1 tablespoon white wine vinegar
  • Salt to taste
  • 1/2 cup water (for hollandaise dilution)

Instructions

  1. Peel the blood orange and cut the zest into thin julienne strips.
  2. Blanch the zest in boiling water for 3-4 minutes, twice, to remove bitterness.
  3. While the zest is blanching, juice the blood orange and strain the juice through a fine mesh sieve to remove pulp and seeds.
  4. Reduce the blood orange juice by half in a saucepan over medium heat to concentrate the flavor.
  5. Once the juice is reduced, strain a small amount over the blanched zest to infuse it with flavor.
  6. Set up a makeshift double boiler with a small pan in a large bowl to ensure even heat distribution.
  7. Bring water to a simmer in the double boiler.
  8. In the pan, whisk together 1 tablespoon of water and 1 tablespoon of white wine vinegar.
  9. Add the egg yolks and whisk continuously until the mixture becomes thick and foamy, forming a sabayon. This may take a few minutes.
  10. Remove the pan from the heat and gradually whisk in the clarified butter, 1-2 tablespoons at a time, ensuring the butter is not too hot.
  11. Once the hollandaise is thick and emulsified, add a squeeze of lemon juice and a pinch of salt.
  12. Taste the hollandaise and adjust seasoning as needed.
  13. To transform the hollandaise into a Maltese sauce, add the reduced blood orange juice and the zest to the hollandaise.
  14. Whisk to combine and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=WhjBH0FF_CE

marinated_aubergine.txt - Marinated Aubergine

Objectives

  • Learn how to grill aubergine for a French-style appetizer
  • Understand the importance of marinating aubergine overnight
  • Discover a versatile recipe that can be adapted with other vegetables

Ingredients

  • Aubergine
  • Olive oil
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Lemon juice
  • Cherry or balsamic vinegar
  • Brown sugar
  • Sultanas or raisins
  • Cloves
  • Roasted nuts (cashew nuts)
  • Bay leaves
  • Chili flakes

Instructions

  1. Cut the aubergine in half lengthwise and brush with olive oil, salt, and pepper.
  2. Heat a cast iron griddle pan over high heat.
  3. Place the aubergine cut-side down on the hot griddle pan and cook for 5-6 minutes.
  4. Flip the aubergine and cook for another 5 minutes on the other side.
  5. Remove the aubergine from the heat and set aside.
  6. In a bowl, combine lemon juice, cherry or balsamic vinegar, brown sugar, sultanas or raisins, olive oil, cloves, and roasted nuts.
  7. Mix the ingredients until the sugar dissolves.
  8. Cut the cooked aubergine into bite-sized pieces using scissors.
  9. Add the aubergine pieces to the marinade.
  10. Add bay leaves and chili flakes to the marinade (optional).
  11. Mix the aubergine and marinade together gently.
  12. Refrigerate the marinated aubergine for at least a few hours or overnight.
  13. Serve chilled with a drizzle of marinade.

marinated_zucchini_salad.txt - Marinated Zucchini Salad

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple and refreshing summer salad using zucchini.
  • Discover a unique marinade that keeps zucchini crunchy and flavorful.
  • Explore different ways to customize this salad with additional ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 1 zucchini
  • 1 lemon
  • 1 teaspoon coriander seeds
  • 30g sugar
  • 1 tablespoon water
  • 1 tablespoon vinegar
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • Olive oil (optional)
  • Pine nuts (optional)
  • Mint (optional)

Instructions

  1. Bring a pot of salted water to a boil.
  2. Zest the lemon and squeeze out the juice.
  3. Slightly crush the coriander seeds.
  4. Slice the zucchini thinly using a mandoline or a knife.
  5. Blanch the zucchini slices in boiling water for 1-2 minutes.
  6. Drain the zucchini and pat dry with a tea towel.
  7. Arrange the zucchini slices in a serving dish.
  8. Sprinkle the zucchini with coriander seeds, lemon zest, salt, and pepper.
  9. Drizzle with lemon juice.
  10. Refrigerate for at least 2 hours.
  11. To make the gastric, heat sugar and water in a saucepan over medium heat.
  12. Once the sugar starts to caramelize, add vinegar.
  13. Immediately pour the hot gastric over the zucchini.
  14. Refrigerate for at least 2 hours.
  15. Serve chilled with additional ingredients like olive oil, pine nuts, and mint (optional).

mini_food_processor_dips.txt - Mini Food Processor Dips

Objectives

  • Showcase the versatility of a mini food processor
  • Explore various dip recipes from a provided booklet
  • Evaluate the effectiveness of the food processor for each recipe

Ingredients

Mayonnaise - 1 egg - Salt - Pepper - Mustard - Oil

Cocktail Sauce - Mayonnaise (from previous step) - Ketchup - English Sauce - Cognac - Cream Fresh

Ham Dip - 2 slices of ham, cut into small pieces - Grain Mustard - Cream Fresh

Asparagus Dip - 3 tablespoons of fromage frais (cream cheese) - 2 tablespoons of orange juice - 1 teaspoon of apple cider vinegar - Salt - Pepper

Tuna Rillettes - 200g can of tuna in brine - 1 teaspoon of olive oil - 1 teaspoon of mustard - 1 tablespoon of chives - 2 tablespoons of cream fresh - Salt - Pepper

Fennel and Goat Cheese Dip - 150g fresh fennel - 100g fresh goat cheese - 1 teaspoon of lemon juice - Parsley - Mint - 1 tablespoon of walnut oil - Salt - Pepper

Instructions

  1. Make the Mayonnaise:
  2. Add an egg, salt, pepper, and mustard to the mini food processor.
  3. Slowly drizzle in oil while pulsing until the mayonnaise is thick and creamy.
  4. Transform into Cocktail Sauce:
  5. Add the mayonnaise, ketchup, English sauce, cognac, and cream fresh to the food processor.
  6. Pulse until well combined.
  7. Make the Ham Dip:
  8. Add the diced ham, grain mustard, and cream fresh to the food processor.
  9. Pulse until the ham is finely chopped and the dip is smooth.
  10. Make the Asparagus Dip:
  11. Add the fromage frais, orange juice, apple cider vinegar, salt, and pepper to the food processor.
  12. Pulse until smooth.
  13. Make the Tuna Rillettes:
  14. Add the tuna, olive oil, mustard, chives, cream fresh, salt, and pepper to the food processor.
  15. Pulse until the tuna is finely chopped and the rillettes are well combined.
  16. Make the Fennel and Goat Cheese Dip:
  17. Pulse the fennel in the food processor until finely chopped.
  18. Add the goat cheese, lemon juice, parsley, mint, walnut oil, salt, and pepper.
  19. Pulse until well combined.

mirepoix_technique.txt - Mirepoix Technique

Objectives

  • Understand the importance of the mirepoix technique in French cooking.
  • Learn the classic mirepoix recipe and its variations.
  • Explore different applications of mirepoix in various dishes.

Ingredients

  • 1 large carrot, peeled and diced
  • 1 large onion, peeled and diced
  • 1 celery stalk, diced

Instructions

  1. Peel and dice the carrot, onion, and celery into roughly the same size pieces.
  2. Combine the diced vegetables in a bowl.
  3. This classic mirepoix can be used as a base for many French sauces and soups.
  4. The ratio of vegetables can be adjusted to taste, but the classic ratio is 2:1:1 (carrot:onion:celery).
  5. Mirepoix can be cooked in butter or oil over medium heat until softened, about 10-15 minutes.
  6. The softened mirepoix can then be used as a base for sauces, soups, stews, or other dishes.
  7. Variations on the classic mirepoix include adding other vegetables such as leeks, garlic, or mushrooms.
  8. The mirepoix technique is a fundamental building block of French cuisine and can be used in countless dishes.

mobile_cookware_review.txt - Mobile Cookware Review: Copper vs. Stainless Steel

Objectives

  • Share the speaker's experience with Mobile cookware after two years of use.
  • Compare the performance of the copper and stainless steel series.
  • Discuss the limitations and specific uses of the stainless steel cookware.

Instructions

  1. Choose between the copper or stainless steel series based on your budget and cooking needs.
  2. Understand that the stainless steel cookware is designed for professional use and requires a specific approach.
  3. Limit heat to 75% of your burner's maximum power when using the stainless steel series.
  4. Use each pan for its intended purpose (e.g., saucepan for sauces, frying pan for searing, stockpot for braising).
  5. Be patient with the slower cooking times associated with the stainless steel series.
  6. Avoid using the stainless steel cookware for tasks it's not designed for (e.g., high-heat searing, cooking acidic foods).
  7. If you experience sticking or burning, adjust your cooking method and heat level.
  8. Remember that the stainless steel cookware requires a learning curve and may not be suitable for every home cook.

mu_clad.txt - Mu Clad

Objectives

  • Learn to make a French bistro dish called Mu Clad.
  • Understand the importance of preparing mussels properly.
  • Master the technique of making a velouté sauce.

Ingredients

  • 2 liters mussels
  • 2 tablespoons butter
  • 50 grams shallots
  • 1 parsley stalk
  • 1 garlic clove
  • 1 sprig thyme
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 1 cup dry white wine (Sauvignon Blanc)
  • 10 grams flour
  • 1/2 teaspoon saffron threads
  • 1-2 tablespoons cream
  • 1 egg yolk
  • 1 tablespoon cream
  • Parsley for garnish

Instructions

  1. Heat a large pot over medium-high heat.
  2. Add butter and melt.
  3. Add half of the shallots, parsley stalk, garlic clove, thyme, and bay leaf.
  4. Cook for 1 minute, or until softened.
  5. Add the white wine and bring to a boil.
  6. Add mussels, reduce heat to medium, and cover.
  7. Steam for 4 minutes, shaking the pot occasionally to ensure even cooking.
  8. Remove mussels from the pot and place in a sieve to cool.
  9. Strain the cooking juices through a fine-mesh sieve into a bowl.
  10. Measure the juices, reserving 1 cup (300 ml) for the sauce.
  11. In a saucepan over medium heat, melt butter.
  12. Add remaining shallots and cook for 1-2 minutes.
  13. Add flour and cook for 1-2 minutes, stirring constantly, to create a roux.
  14. Stir in saffron threads and cook for 1 minute.
  15. Strain the roux through a fine-mesh sieve into a clean saucepan.
  16. Bring to a simmer and cook for 5 minutes, whisking constantly.
  17. Add cream and continue cooking for 10 minutes, or until the sauce has reached the desired thickness.
  18. In a small bowl, whisk together egg yolk and cream.
  19. Reduce heat to low and gradually whisk the egg yolk mixture into the sauce.
  20. Cook for 1 minute, or until the sauce is thickened.
  21. Arrange the mussels on a baking dish, discarding the top shells.
  22. Pour the sauce over the mussels.
  23. Broil for 3 minutes, or until the sauce is glazed.
  24. Garnish with parsley and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=y8N3vYlcs2w

muscle_mushroom_bake.txt - Grattin de Moules

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French muscle and mushroom bake.
  • Master the art of marinating muscles for a flavorful base.
  • Create a delicious mushroom garnish using a traditional French technique.

Ingredients

  • Butter
  • Shallot
  • Parsley
  • Muscles (cleaned)
  • Shellfish stock
  • White wine (Pinot Blanc)
  • Lemon juice
  • Salt
  • Button mushrooms (finely chopped)
  • Fresh parsley
  • Cream
  • Flour
  • Breadcrumbs (optional)

Instructions

  1. Marinate the muscles:
  2. Melt butter in a large pan over high heat.
  3. Add shallots and parsley, stir until fragrant.
  4. Add muscles, stir to coat.
  5. Pour in shellfish stock and white wine.
  6. Cover and cook for a few minutes until muscles open.
  7. Remove muscles from shells and set aside.
  8. Prepare the mushroom garnish:
  9. Melt butter in a pan over low heat.
  10. Add shallots and sweat for a few minutes.
  11. Add white wine and reduce until almost dry.
  12. Add finely chopped mushrooms, salt, and lemon juice.
  13. Cook until all moisture evaporates.
  14. Stir in fresh parsley.
  15. Make the velouté:
  16. Melt butter in a pan.
  17. Add shallots and sweat for a minute.
  18. Add white wine and reduce by a third.
  19. Add 200 ml of muscle cooking juices and 200 ml of shellfish stock.
  20. Reduce by a third.
  21. Add cream and reduce again.
  22. Thicken with a roux (flour and butter) or cornstarch.
  23. Assemble the bake:
  24. Combine the velouté, mushrooms, and muscles.
  25. Transfer to a baking dish.
  26. Top with breadcrumbs (optional).
  27. Broil until golden brown.
  28. Serve and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=G1hj8OB-P8M

mushroom_cheese_tartlets.txt - Mushroom and Cheese Tartlets

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French appetizer, mushroom and cheese tartlets.
  • Understand the importance of preparing a bechamel sauce.
  • Create a delicious and simple finger food for parties.

Ingredients

English | Chinese ------- | -------- Butter | 黄油 Flour | 面粉 Small bay leaf | 小月桂叶 Shallot | 葱 One clove | 一瓣 Milk | 牛奶 Cheese | 奶酪 Mushrooms | 蘑菇 Salt | 盐 Pepper | 胡椒

Instructions

  1. Prepare the ingredients:
  2. Trim the mushrooms, discarding the dried bits and keeping the base for flavoring the milk.
  3. Thinly slice the mushroom caps.
  4. Grate the cheese.
  5. Make the roux:
  6. Melt the butter in a pan over low heat.
  7. Add the flour and whisk until combined.
  8. Cook for 3 minutes, until lightly colored.
  9. Prepare the flavored milk:
  10. Pour the milk into a pan.
  11. Add the shallot, clove, bay leaf, mushroom base, salt, and pepper.
  12. Heat gently until almost boiling.
  13. Combine the roux and milk:
  14. Turn off the heat for the milk.
  15. Pour the warm milk into the cold roux through a sieve.
  16. Whisk to combine.
  17. Cook the bechamel:
  18. Stir the bechamel over low heat for 5 minutes until thickened.
  19. Pan-fry the mushrooms:
  20. Heat a tablespoon of butter in a pan over medium heat.
  21. Add the mushrooms, salt, and pepper.
  22. Fry until softened.
  23. Assemble the tartlets:
  24. Warm the bechamel over low heat.
  25. Stir in the grated cheese until melted.
  26. Add the cooked mushrooms to the bechamel.
  27. Fill the tartlets:
  28. Spoon the mushroom and cheese mixture into the prepared tartlet shells.
  29. Sprinkle with breadcrumbs.
  30. Drizzle with melted butter.
  31. Bake the tartlets:
  32. Bake in a preheated oven at 170 degrees Celsius for a few minutes, until warmed through and the breadcrumbs are slightly browned.
  33. Serve:
  34. Arrange the tartlets on a serving platter.
  35. Garnish with parsley and mushrooms, if desired.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=uvsadISlCL0

mushroom_cream.txt - Crème de Champignon

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a classic French mushroom cream soup.
  • Understand the different types of soups in French cuisine.
  • Master the technique of making a clear bechamel sauce.

Ingredients

English | Chinese ------- | -------- 40 grams butter | 黄油 (huáng yóu) 40 grams flour | 面粉 (miàn fěn) 800 ml milk | 牛奶 (niú nǎi) 50 grams butter | 黄油 (huáng yóu) 1 shallot, finely chopped | 细碎切好的小洋葱 (xì suì qiē hǎo de xiǎo yáng cōng) 500 grams mushrooms | 蘑菇 (mó gu) 1-2 pinches of salt | 盐 (yán) 1-2 pinches of black pepper | 黑胡椒粉 (hēi hú jiāo fěn) 1 bay leaf | 月桂叶 (yuè guì yè) 1/2 onion with cloves | 带丁香的半个洋葱 (dài dīng xiāng de bàn ge yáng cōng) 1/2 teaspoon nutmeg | 肉豆蔻 (ròu dòu kòu) 200 ml crème fraîche | 淡奶油 (dàn nǎi yóu) 1 tablespoon parsley, chopped | 切碎的欧芹 (qiē suì de ōu qín)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the ingredients: finely chop the shallot, roughly chop the mushrooms, and weigh out the butter and flour.
  2. Make the roux: melt the butter in a saucepan over medium heat. Add the flour and whisk until combined. Cook for 2 minutes, then remove from heat and set aside to cool.
  3. Sweat the shallot: melt the butter in a large pan over medium heat. Add the shallot and cook until softened, about 2 minutes.
  4. Cook the mushrooms: add the mushrooms to the pan and cook for 1-2 minutes, stirring occasionally. Season with salt and pepper.
  5. Infuse the milk: add the milk, bay leaf, onion, nutmeg, salt, and pepper to a saucepan. Bring to a boil, then remove from heat and let steep for 5 minutes.
  6. Reduce the mushrooms: reduce the heat to medium-low and cook the mushrooms until they have released their liquid and are starting to brown, about 10 minutes.
  7. Make the bechamel: remove the bay leaf and onion from the milk. Add a small amount of the hot milk to the roux, whisking constantly to create a smooth paste. Pour the roux mixture into the remaining hot milk and whisk until smooth. Bring to a simmer, stirring constantly, until thickened.
  8. Strain the bechamel: strain the bechamel through a fine-mesh sieve to remove any lumps.
  9. Blend the mushrooms: transfer the cooked mushrooms to a blender and blend until smooth.
  10. Combine the bechamel and mushroom puree: add the mushroom puree to the bechamel and whisk until combined.
  11. Heat the soup: add the crème fraîche and milk to the soup and heat gently, stirring constantly, until warmed through.
  12. Serve: ladle the soup into bowls and garnish with chopped parsley.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=rvxVCKlL2Gs

mushroom_royale.txt - Mushroom Royale

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a classic French side dish, the Mushroom Royale.
  • Understand the importance of using cold purees and custards for a successful Royale.
  • Master the technique of poaching the Royale in a water bath.

Ingredients

  • 200 milliliters (7 oz) heavy cream
  • 2 eggs (or 1 egg and 2 egg yolks)
  • 1/4 teaspoon salt
  • 1/8 teaspoon black pepper
  • 1/8 teaspoon grated nutmeg
  • Cauliflower puree
  • Broccolini puree
  • Mushroom duxelle
  • Tomato puree (reduced)
  • Unsalted butter, softened
  • Parchment paper
  • Ramekins (or other heatproof molds)
  • Roasting pan

Instructions

  1. Prepare the purees. Boil each vegetable in salted water until tender. Pass through a food processor with a bit of butter and let cool completely.
  2. Prepare the custards. In a bowl, whisk together the cream, eggs (or egg and yolks), salt, pepper, and nutmeg.
  3. Assemble the Royale.
    • For each ramekin, cut a circle of parchment paper to fit the bottom.
    • Brush the inside of the ramekin with softened butter.
    • Place the parchment paper circle in the bottom of the ramekin.
  4. Combine the custard and puree. In a separate bowl, whisk together the custard and puree in a 1:1 ratio. Adjust the ratio as needed to achieve a desired consistency.
  5. Fill the ramekins. Pour the custard-puree mixture into the prepared ramekins, leaving a small margin at the top.
  6. Preheat the oven to 150 degrees Celsius (300 degrees Fahrenheit).
  7. Prepare the water bath. Fill a roasting pan with water and bring to a boil. Place a sheet of parchment paper in the bottom of the pan to prevent water from splashing into the ramekins.
  8. Poach the Royale. Carefully place the ramekins in the roasting pan. The water level should come about 3/4 of the way up the sides of the ramekins.
  9. Bake. Bake for 25-30 minutes, or until the Royale is set.
  10. Cool. Allow the Royale to cool completely before unmolding.
  11. Unmold. To unmold, run a thin knife around the edges of the Royale. Gently invert the ramekin onto a plate.
  12. Serve. Serve the Royale cold, garnished as desired.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=71tVL8CKh_4

mussel_chorizo_cream.txt - Mussels with Chorizo and Cream

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French recipe, Mussels with Chorizo and Cream.
  • Prepare a delicious and impressive meal in under 15 minutes.
  • Understand the importance of using fresh ingredients and proper cooking techniques.

Ingredients

  • Fresh Mussels
  • Parsley
  • Tomatoes
  • Cream
  • Shallots
  • Butter
  • Garlic
  • Thyme
  • White Wine
  • Chorizo
  • Olive Oil

Instructions

  1. Prepare all ingredients: chop parsley, tomatoes, shallots, garlic, and thyme.
  2. Heat a stainless steel pan over medium heat.
  3. Add a tablespoon or two of olive oil and melt butter.
  4. Once butter is melted, add shallots and cook for 1 minute.
  5. Add garlic, thyme, and chorizo to the pan. Cook for 1-2 minutes, ensuring chorizo is softened but not overcooked.
  6. Deglaze the pan with half a glass of white wine. Reduce the wine for a few minutes until almost dry.
  7. Add a tablespoon or two of diced tomatoes. Cook for 2-4 minutes until heated through.
  8. Add 300 ml of cream and reduce heat to low. Let the base infuse for a few minutes.
  9. Add the mussels to the pan, ensuring they are coated in the sauce.
  10. Cover the pan and cook for 5-6 minutes, or until mussels open.
  11. Remove the pan from heat and check the mussels. They should be slightly soft and bouncy, not rubbery.
  12. Transfer the mussels to a bowl and set aside.
  13. Strain the sauce through a fine mesh sieve to remove any sand or debris.
  14. Arrange the mussels in a serving dish.
  15. Pour the strained sauce over the mussels.
  16. Add chorizo pieces and garnish with chopped parsley.
  17. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=x0mBdyjRug8

mussel_soup_saffron.txt - Mussel Soup with Saffron

Objectives

  • Learn to cook mussels Marina style.
  • Create a classic French mussel soup with saffron.
  • Master the technique of sweating vegetables.
  • Understand the importance of filtering soup for a smooth texture.
  • Learn to use saffron effectively for color and flavor.

Ingredients

  • 1 kilo mussels
  • 1 shallot, finely chopped
  • Parsley
  • Butter
  • Wine (150 ml)
  • Carrots
  • Leeks
  • Fennel
  • Onion
  • Fish stock (500 ml)
  • Cream (100 ml)
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Star anise
  • Pastis (optional)
  • Threads of saffron
  • Olive oil (1 tablespoon)
  • Flour (20 grams)
  • Garlic
  • Croutons
  • Tomato

Instructions

  1. Prepare the mussels Marina style:
  2. Melt butter in a pan over medium heat.
  3. Add chopped shallots and cook for 1-2 minutes.
  4. Add parsley, wine, and increase heat to high.
  5. Add mussels and cook for 6 minutes with the lid on, shaking occasionally.
  6. Remove mussels from the pan and reserve in a bowl.
  7. Strain the mussel juice and set aside.
  8. Start the soup base:
  9. Melt butter in a pot over medium heat.
  10. Add onions and cook for 2 minutes.
  11. Add leeks, carrots, fennel, and thyme.
  12. Sweat the vegetables for 4-5 minutes until softened.
  13. Add olive oil if needed.
  14. Stir in flour to thicken the soup.
  15. Add the mussel juice and fish stock.
  16. Add a tomato for flavor.
  17. Bring to a boil, then reduce heat and simmer for 15 minutes.
  18. Filter the soup:
  19. Strain the soup through a sieve, pressing down on the vegetables to extract all the juices.
  20. Transfer the filtered soup to a clean pot.
  21. Finish the soup:
  22. Bring the filtered soup to a light boil.
  23. Add cream, pastis (optional), and saffron.
  24. Reduce the soup for 10 minutes.
  25. Adjust saffron as needed to achieve desired color.
  26. Taste and season with salt and pepper.
  27. Serve the soup:
  28. Serve the soup hot with reserved mussels, croutons, and a touch of parsley.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=mfC2ATn_8gU

navaran_opom.txt - Navaran Opom

Objectives

  • Learn to cook a traditional French lamb stew called Navaran Opom.
  • Master the slow-cooking technique for tender, flavorful meat.
  • Create a rich, aromatic sauce using tomatoes, garlic, onion, and carrots.

Ingredients

  • 1 kg lamb shoulder (with bone)
  • 800 g lamb shoulder (boneless)
  • 100 g carrots (about 1 carrot)
  • 100 g onions
  • 2 garlic cloves
  • 20 g tomato paste
  • 30 g flour
  • Parsley (for garnish)
  • Water (for cooking)
  • 6 boiling potatoes
  • 20 g butter
  • 1 tablespoon sugar
  • Water (for caramelized onions)
  • Peanut oil (for searing)

Instructions

  1. Wash, prepare, and cut all vegetables. Dice carrots and onions into small cubes (Mira size).
  2. Preheat oven to 220°C (400°F).
  3. Heat a cast iron pan over medium-high heat. Add about 5 tablespoons of peanut oil.
  4. Sear the lamb pieces in batches, ensuring they are not crowded in the pan. Brown each side for a few minutes.
  5. Remove the seared lamb and set aside.
  6. Remove excess fat from the pan, leaving the caramelized juices.
  7. Add carrots, onions, and a knob of butter to the pan. Sweat the vegetables for 2-3 minutes.
  8. Return the lamb to the pan. Sprinkle half of the flour over the meat, creating a light coating.
  9. Place the pan in the preheated oven for 5 minutes.
  10. Remove the pan from the oven. Stir in tomato paste and blend it into the meat and vegetables.
  11. Add water to cover the meat.
  12. Bring the mixture to a boil over high heat.
  13. Add garlic cloves, a piece of bouguignon, salt, and cracked pepper.
  14. Cover the pan and place it in the oven at 200°C (400°F) for 35 minutes.
  15. While the lamb cooks, blanch the potatoes by boiling them in cold water until they are cooked through.
  16. Remove the pan from the oven. Transfer the lamb pieces to a separate pan, leaving the sauce behind.
  17. Strain the sauce through a sieve, discarding the carrots and onions.
  18. Return the strained sauce to the pan, add the potatoes and lamb, and simmer over medium-low heat for 20 minutes.
  19. Caramelize the onions in a separate pan by sautéing them in butter, sugar, and a little water.
  20. Serve the Navaran Opom with a sprinkle of caramelized onions and parsley.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=SABeSRbAG9M

normandy_pork_chops.txt - Pork Chops with Apple Cider Sauce

Objectives

  • Make a delicious Normandy-style pork chop dish with minimal ingredients
  • Learn to create a flavorful sauce from pan juices and cider
  • Understand the importance of searing and caramelizing the pork chops

Ingredients

  • Pork chops or cutlets
  • Butter
  • Oil
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Dry cider
  • Heavy cream
  • Golden Delicious apples
  • Calvados (optional)

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 350 degrees F (175 degrees C).
  2. Season pork chops with salt.
  3. Heat butter and oil in a skillet over medium heat.
  4. Sear pork chops for 4 minutes per side, ensuring they are well-browned and juices are released into the pan.
  5. Remove pork chops from skillet and place on a baking sheet. Cover with foil and keep warm in the oven.
  6. While pork chops are cooking, slice apples thinly and sauté in butter with salt and pepper.
  7. Deglaze the pan with cider, scraping up the browned bits from the bottom.
  8. Reduce cider for 1-2 minutes, then add heavy cream.
  9. Bring the sauce to a boil and simmer until it thickens and coats the back of a spoon.
  10. Season sauce with salt and pepper.
  11. Add Calvados to the sauce (optional).
  12. Return pork chops to the pan and coat with the sauce.
  13. Cook for 1-2 minutes per side.
  14. Serve pork chops with apple slices and sauce.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6885ZmOdgNA

nuns_fart.txt - Nuns' Fart

Objectives

  • Create a choux paste-based dessert with a unique texture
  • Deep fry the choux paste to achieve a fluffy, donut-like consistency
  • Decorate the dessert with powdered sugar and a cauldron-shaped presentation

Ingredients

  • 1 cup milk
  • 1/2 teaspoon salt
  • 1/2 cup sugar
  • 1/2 cup butter
  • 1 cup flour
  • 4-6 eggs
  • Vegetable oil for deep frying
  • Powdered sugar for dusting

Instructions

  1. In a saucepan over medium heat, combine milk, salt, sugar, and butter.
  2. Bring the mixture to a boil, stirring constantly.
  3. Once boiling, immediately remove from heat and add all the flour at once.
  4. Stir vigorously until a dough ball forms.
  5. Transfer the dough to a bowl and let it cool for 10 minutes.
  6. In a food processor, combine the cooled dough and 3 eggs.
  7. Pulse until the dough is smooth and slightly sticky.
  8. Add additional eggs, one at a time, until the dough reaches a desired consistency where it holds its shape but is not watery.
  9. Heat vegetable oil in a deep fryer or large pot to 338 degrees Fahrenheit (170 degrees Celsius).
  10. Using two spoons, drop spoonfuls of the dough into the hot oil.
  11. Fry until golden brown and puffed up.
  12. Remove the fried dough and drain on paper towels.
  13. Toss the fried dough in powdered sugar.
  14. Arrange the sugared dough in a cauldron shape for presentation.
  15. Enjoy with your favorite fillings, such as jam, salted caramel, or chestnut cream.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=jrn7p8KdaJM

old_fashioned_macarons.txt - Old-Fashioned Macarons

Objectives

  • Learn to make old-fashioned macarons using only three ingredients
  • Understand the importance of using fresh egg whites for best results
  • Discover the versatility of old-fashioned macarons for different fillings and uses

Ingredients

  • 100g blanched almond meal
  • 100g granulated sugar
  • 60g egg whites

Instructions

  1. Combine blanched almond meal and granulated sugar in a bowl.
  2. Mix the almond meal and sugar together using a spoon until well blended.
  3. Slowly incorporate egg whites into the almond mixture, pressing hard to create a paste.
  4. Transfer the macaron paste to a piping bag fitted with a straight tip (about 1.5 cm in diameter).
  5. Pipe the macaron mixture onto a silicone baking mat, creating small mounds.
  6. Brush the tops of the macarons with plain water.
  7. Bake in an oven preheated to 180 degrees Celsius (355 degrees Fahrenheit) for 10-15 minutes.
  8. Allow the macarons to cool completely before filling and serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vKacPWYvR1g

olive_oil_almond_cake.txt - Olive Oil and Almond Cake

Objectives

  • Learn to bake a simple, modern cake with a French twist.
  • Utilize olive oil and almond meal for a unique flavor profile.
  • Discover the ease of baking this "emergency cake" for unexpected guests.

Ingredients

  • 200 grams almond meal
  • 200 grams granulated sugar
  • 30 grams all-purpose flour
  • 100 grams olive oil
  • 5 whole eggs

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 160 degrees Celsius.
  2. Grease and line a 24-centimeter (9.5-inch) round cake tin with parchment paper.
  3. In a bowl, crack the eggs and add the sugar.
  4. Using a whisk or stand mixer, beat the eggs and sugar together on medium speed until the sugar dissolves and the mixture lightens in color (about 30 seconds).
  5. Add the almond meal, flour, and olive oil to the egg mixture.
  6. Mix until all ingredients are well combined and the batter has a ribbon consistency.
  7. Pour the batter into the prepared cake tin.
  8. Bake for 40-45 minutes, or until a toothpick inserted into the center comes out clean.
  9. Let the cake cool in the tin for a few minutes before inverting it onto a wire rack to cool completely.
  10. Enjoy your delicious olive oil and almond cake!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Ulm_OeiAMm0

onion_tart.txt - Onion Tart

Objectives

  • Learn to make a traditional French onion tart, a forgotten recipe from the past.
  • Understand the importance of blanching onions to remove sharpness.
  • Master the technique of making a smooth, flavorful soubise puree.

Ingredients

  • 1 tablespoon of butter
  • 1 tablespoon of flour
  • 1 cup of milk
  • 1/2 teaspoon of nutmeg
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • 1 large onion, thinly sliced
  • 1 tablespoon of butter
  • 1/2 teaspoon of salt
  • 1/4 teaspoon of black pepper
  • 1/4 teaspoon of sugar
  • 1 tablespoon of cream
  • 1 shortcrust pastry, blind-baked

Instructions

  1. Blanch the onions: Fill a pan with cold water, add the sliced onions, and bring to a boil.
  2. Make the bechamel sauce: Melt butter in a saucepan over low heat. Whisk in flour and cook for 3 minutes. Gradually whisk in cold milk, then bring to a simmer. Add salt, pepper, nutmeg, and a bay leaf.
  3. Cook the onions: Drain the blanched onions and rinse with cold water. Melt butter in a pan and add the onions. Cook over low heat for 40 minutes, covered.
  4. Combine the onions and bechamel: Add the cooked onions to the bechamel sauce. Stir to combine, then blend with an immersion blender until smooth.
  5. Adjust seasoning and consistency: Add cream, salt, pepper, and nutmeg to taste. Cook for 15 minutes.
  6. Fill the tart shell: Pour the soubise puree into the blind-baked tart shell, ensuring it's filled to the brim.
  7. Bake: Sprinkle breadcrumbs on top and bake for 15 minutes at 220 degrees Celsius (428 degrees Fahrenheit).
  8. Cool and serve: Allow the tart to cool before slicing and serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=N-hOMbnp138

Objectives

  • Make a refreshing orange and grapefruit juice
  • Use a juicer to extract the juice from oranges and grapefruits
  • Boost your energy levels with a healthy, vitamin-rich drink

Ingredients

  • Oranges
  • Grapefruit

Instructions

  1. Take your oranges and place them into the juicer.
  2. Press the oranges down into the juicer to extract the juice.
  3. Add grapefruit to the juicer.
  4. Press the grapefruit down into the juicer to extract the juice.
  5. Enjoy your freshly squeezed orange and grapefruit juice!

oven_baked_fish_with_white_wine_sauce.txt - Oven Baked Fish with White Wine Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn a simple and delicious French recipe for oven-baked fish.
  • Discover a quick and easy way to prepare a classic Parisian Bistro dish.
  • Explore the versatility of this recipe using different types of white fish.

Ingredients

  • 1 white fish fillet (any type)
  • 1 tablespoon olive oil
  • 1/4 cup chopped shallots
  • 1 tablespoon chopped parsley
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • 1/4 cup breadcrumbs
  • 2 tablespoons butter, cubed
  • 1/4 cup white wine (optional)

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 220°C (428°F) with fan forced.
  2. Score the fish fillet on the underside, creating a crisscross pattern.
  3. Brush the bottom of a baking dish with olive oil.
  4. Place the scored fish fillet in the baking dish, skin side down.
  5. Sprinkle with chopped shallots, parsley, salt, and pepper.
  6. Top with breadcrumbs and butter cubes.
  7. Optionally, pour white wine over the fish.
  8. Bake in the preheated oven for 20 minutes.
  9. The butter will melt, the breadcrumbs will become golden brown, and the fish will be cooked through.
  10. Serve the fish with the reduced wine sauce, enjoying the delicious flavors of the classic French dish.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=yFc-6RPcdoE

palmi_heart_of_france.txt - Palmi (Heart of France)

Objectives

  • Learn to make a traditional French biscuit called Palmi or Heart of France
  • Understand the folding technique for puff pastry
  • Create a beautiful, layered biscuit with a crispy texture

Ingredients

  • 1 sheet of pre-made puff pastry (pure butter)
  • Granulated sugar

Instructions

  1. Unroll the puff pastry sheet and sprinkle a generous amount of sugar on top.
  2. Use a rolling pin to press the sugar into the pastry, ensuring it's evenly distributed.
  3. Repeat the process on the other side of the pastry, ensuring both sides have plenty of sugar.
  4. Fold one side of the pastry over, then fold the other side over to create a long rectangular shape.
  5. Sprinkle more sugar on top and use the rolling pin to press it into the pastry.
  6. Fold the pastry in half again, creating a long, narrow shape.
  7. Repeat the process of adding sugar and flattening with the rolling pin.
  8. Cut the pastry into strips approximately 2 centimeters (just over an inch) wide.
  9. Place the strips on a baking sheet lined with parchment paper, standing them on their sides with a small space between each strip.
  10. Bake in a preheated oven at 240°C (464°F) for 10 minutes.
  11. Watch the biscuits closely during baking, rotating them if they start to brown too quickly.
  12. Remove from the oven when golden brown and allow to cool slightly before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=i6b0Re_oqMc

pan_fried_egg.txt - Pan Fried Egg

Objectives

  • Learn the proper technique for cooking a pan-fried egg according to French culinary standards
  • Understand the importance of low heat and careful seasoning
  • Achieve a perfectly cooked egg with no coloration on the edges or underside

Ingredients

  • 1 egg
  • 1 tablespoon of butter
  • Salt and pepper to taste

Instructions

  1. Melt butter in a non-stick pan over very low heat.
  2. Crack the egg into a bowl and whisk until the white and yolk are well combined.
  3. Once the butter is melted and starts to foam, pour the egg into the pan.
  4. Season the egg with salt and pepper around the edges of the pan, never directly on the yolk.
  5. Cook the egg gently, ensuring the heat is low enough to prevent any browning or discoloration on the edges or underside.
  6. Continue cooking until the white is set and the yolk is still runny.
  7. Slide the cooked egg onto a plate using a spatula, maintaining its shape and avoiding any breakage.
  8. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=zS4U-OdJQQ4

paprika_chicken.txt - Paprika Chicken (Poulet au Paprika)

Objectives

  • Learn a simple family-style recipe from Augustus Coffee.
  • Practice basic cooking techniques like sauteing and making a simple sauce.
  • Create a flavorful paprika chicken dish with a creamy tomato sauce.

Ingredients

  • 4 pieces of chicken (cut into portions)
  • 2 tablespoons of sunflower oil
  • 1 tablespoon of butter
  • 1 diced onion
  • 1 peeled and diced tomato
  • 100 ml of white wine
  • 2 tablespoons of paprika powder
  • 2-3 tablespoons of cream (adjust to taste)
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • Flour for coating the chicken

Instructions

  1. Prepare the chicken: Cut the chicken into portions (wings, breasts, thighs) and coat each piece in flour.
  2. Prepare the mise-en-place: Dice the onion, peel and dice the tomato, and measure out the wine, butter, and paprika powder.
  3. Heat the pan: Heat 2 tablespoons of sunflower oil and 1 tablespoon of butter in a cast iron pan over medium heat.
  4. Sear the chicken: Add the chicken pieces to the pan, skin-side down, and sear until golden brown (about 5 minutes).
  5. Add the onions: Remove the chicken breasts from the pan to create space and add the diced onions. Cook for a few minutes, stirring occasionally, until softened.
  6. Add the wine: Return the chicken breasts to the pan and add the wine. Reduce the wine by half (about 5 minutes).
  7. Add the paprika: Once the wine has reduced, add the paprika powder and stir to coat the chicken and onions.
  8. Add the tomatoes: Add the diced tomatoes to the pan and cook for 5 minutes, stirring occasionally, until the tomatoes have softened and reduced.
  9. Add the cream: Add the cream to the pan and stir gently to combine. Let the cream melt before turning the chicken over to coat it in the sauce.
  10. Adjust the sauce: Taste the sauce and adjust the seasoning with salt, pepper, paprika powder, and/or a splash of wine as needed.
  11. Serve: Serve the paprika chicken immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=94TvgNnx-p4

paprika_rice.txt - Paprika Rice

Objectives

  • Learn to make a paprika rice using a pilaf technique.
  • Understand the origins of the pilaf technique and paprika powder.
  • Discover a foolproof method for cooking rice.

Ingredients

  • 200 grams of rice
  • 300 ml of water
  • 1 tablespoon of paprika powder
  • 1 onion, finely diced
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 1 teaspoon of salt
  • Olive oil
  • Butter
  • Bouquet garni

Instructions

  1. Preheat the oven to 200 degrees Celsius (400 degrees Fahrenheit).
  2. Pour water into a small pan and add a teaspoon of salt. Bring to a boil.
  3. Heat olive oil in a separate pan over medium heat.
  4. Once the oil is hot, add the diced onion and cook for 2-4 minutes until slightly browned.
  5. Add 1 tablespoon of paprika powder to the pan and stir quickly to avoid burning.
  6. Add the rice to the pan and let it absorb the oil for about 1 minute.
  7. Pour the boiling water into the pan with the rice, onion, and paprika.
  8. Add the bay leaf and bouquet garni to the pan.
  9. Bring the mixture to a boil, then turn off the heat.
  10. Cover the pan with a lid and place it in the preheated oven for 10 minutes.
  11. After 10 minutes, remove the pan from the oven (use a flour-covered oven mitt to avoid burns).
  12. Remove the bouquet garni from the pan.
  13. Check the rice. If all the water is absorbed and the rice is cooked, add a knob of butter to the pan and stir to make the rice shiny.
  14. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=TGc5IlcD9gs

parchment_circle.txt - Parchment Paper Circle

Objectives

  • Learn how to transform a square of parchment paper into a perfect circle
  • Understand why this technique is useful in French cooking
  • Learn how to adjust the size of the circle to fit different pans

Ingredients

  • Square of parchment paper
  • Scissors
  • Pan

Instructions

  1. Fold the parchment paper in half from right to left or left to right.
  2. Fold the paper in half again from bottom to top.
  3. Fold the paper in half a third time, creating a triangle shape.
  4. Place the pan on top of the folded parchment paper.
  5. Align the tip of the parchment paper with the center of the pan.
  6. Make a cut along the inside edge of the pan.
  7. Remove the pan and unfold the parchment paper.
  8. You now have a perfect circle of parchment paper.
  9. Adjust the size of the circle by adjusting the position of the parchment paper on the pan before cutting.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=jLRLiKMbVto

parisian_custard_pie.txt - Parisian Custard Pie

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a classic Parisian custard pie.
  • Understand the importance of letting the custard cool before baking.
  • Discover a simple dessert recipe that pays tribute to Paul Bocuse.

Ingredients

  • 5 egg yolks (100 grams)
  • 100 grams castor sugar
  • 50 grams cornstarch
  • 1 vanilla bean
  • 500 ml milk
  • 100 ml heavy whipping cream
  • Butter
  • Parchment paper

Instructions

  1. Separate the egg yolks and keep the whites for later use.
  2. Preheat oven to 300 degrees Fahrenheit (148 degrees Celsius).
  3. Grease a baking dish with butter and line the bottom with parchment paper.
  4. In a bowl, whisk together the egg yolks and sugar until the mixture turns white.
  5. Add the cornstarch to the egg yolk mixture and whisk until fully incorporated.
  6. Split the vanilla bean lengthwise and scrape out the seeds.
  7. Heat the milk and cream in a saucepan over medium heat.
  8. Add the vanilla seeds and bean to the saucepan.
  9. Bring the milk mixture to a boil, stirring occasionally.
  10. Remove the saucepan from the heat and strain the milk mixture through a sieve to remove the vanilla bean.
  11. Slowly pour the hot milk mixture into the egg yolk mixture, whisking constantly.
  12. Pour the custard mixture back into the saucepan.
  13. Cook the custard over medium heat, whisking continuously, for 4-5 minutes until it thickens and boils.
  14. Pour the custard into a clean container and cover with plastic wrap, ensuring the wrap is touching the surface of the custard.
  15. Allow the custard to cool to room temperature.
  16. Once the custard has cooled, whisk it until smooth.
  17. Pour the custard into the prepared baking dish.
  18. Bake in the preheated oven for 30-45 minutes, or until the custard is set and the top is golden brown.
  19. Allow the custard pie to cool slightly before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=llq-l50KpFE

pastry_cream.txt - Crème Pâtissière

Objectives

  • Learn to make delicious pastry cream (crème pâtissière)
  • Understand the importance of boiling the cream for 3 minutes
  • Learn how to add your own flavoring and consistency to pastry cream

Ingredients

  • 3 egg yolks
  • 1 vanilla pod
  • 1/2 cup sugar
  • 1/4 cup flour
  • 1 cup milk
  • 1 tablespoon butter
  • 1 tablespoon orange juice
  • 1 teaspoon rum

Instructions

  1. Heat a medium saucepan over medium-high heat.
  2. Add the milk, vanilla pod, and seeds to the pan.
  3. Bring the milk mixture to a boil.
  4. While the milk is heating, whisk together the egg yolks, sugar, and flour until light and frothy.
  5. Slowly whisk the boiling milk into the egg yolk mixture.
  6. Return the mixture to the saucepan and cook over medium heat, stirring constantly, until the cream thickens and boils.
  7. Cook for 3 minutes, stirring constantly, to remove the flour taste.
  8. Remove the cream from the heat and transfer to a clean bowl.
  9. Cover the cream with plastic wrap, pressing the wrap directly onto the surface of the cream to prevent a skin from forming.
  10. Refrigerate the cream until it is almost cold.
  11. Once the cream is cold, you can add your own flavoring and consistency.
  12. For a classic orange and rum pastry cream, add a tablespoon of orange juice and a teaspoon of rum to the cream.
  13. Mix well and use as desired.

pink_praline.txt - Pink Praline

Objectives

  • Learn the history of the praline and the pink praline.
  • Make pink pralines using a copper pan.
  • Understand the importance of temperature control when making pralines.

Ingredients

50 grams almonds 100 grams sugar 50 ml water Red food coloring (few drops)

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 190 degrees Celsius.
  2. Place almonds on a baking sheet lined with parchment paper and toast for 10 minutes.
  3. Combine sugar and water in a copper pan.
  4. Bring the mixture to a boil over high heat.
  5. Add a few drops of red food coloring.
  6. Use a thermometer to monitor the temperature of the syrup.
  7. When the syrup reaches 124 degrees Celsius, remove from heat.
  8. Add the toasted almonds to the syrup and stir to coat.
  9. Continue stirring until the syrup cools and solidifies slightly.
  10. Transfer the almonds to a baking sheet lined with parchment paper.
  11. Repeat steps 3-10 for a second coating of sugar. Use 50 grams of the pink sugar from the first coating and 50 grams of fresh sugar.
  12. For a third coating, pour the syrup over the almonds in a bowl and stir to coat.
  13. (Optional) Bake the pralines at 70 degrees Celsius for 30 minutes to remove any excess whiteness.
  14. Allow the pralines to cool completely before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=9aZ80YkS81o

pizza_saladier.txt - Pizza Saladier

Objectives

  • Learn to make a traditional Pizza Saladier from Nice, France
  • Prepare a flavorful and authentic Pisa base with sardines and herbs
  • Create caramelized onions with thyme and bay leaves for a sweet and savory topping

Ingredients

  • Dough
    • 250 g flour
    • 5 g dry yeast
    • 250 ml lukewarm water
    • 50 g milk
    • 1-2 pinches salt
    • 5 tablespoons olive oil
  • Pisa
    • 2 cloves garlic, crushed
    • Fennel seeds, crushed
    • 1 tin of sardines in olive oil, mashed
    • 5-6 anchovies
    • Olive oil, to create a paste consistency
  • Caramelized Onions
    • 1 kg onions, thinly sliced
    • Olive oil
    • Salt
    • Fresh thyme sprigs
    • 1-2 bay leaves
  • Topping
    • Black olives
    • Anchovies (optional)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Dough:
  2. In a bowl, dissolve yeast in lukewarm water.
  3. In a large container, combine flour and salt. Create a well in the center.
  4. Gradually add the yeast mixture, milk, and olive oil to the flour, incorporating everything into a dough.
  5. Knead the dough until it forms a smooth ball and doesn't stick to your fingers.
  6. Cover the dough with a cloth and let it rest for 1 hour.
  7. Make the Pisa:
  8. Crush the garlic and fennel seeds.
  9. Mash the sardines and olive oil together.
  10. Add the crushed garlic, fennel seeds, and anchovies to the sardines mixture.
  11. Gradually add olive oil, mixing until you create a semi-liquid paste.
  12. Caramelize the Onions:
  13. Heat olive oil in a pan over medium heat.
  14. Add thinly sliced onions and cook until they caramelize, about 10-25 minutes.
  15. Season with salt and add thyme sprigs and bay leaves.
  16. Stir occasionally, avoiding over-stirring to prevent onion disintegration.
  17. Assemble the Pizza Saladier:
  18. Preheat oven to 200°C (400°F).
  19. Dust a baking tray with flour.
  20. Roll out the dough and place it on the prepared tray.
  21. Spread the Pisa paste evenly over the dough.
  22. Top with a generous layer of caramelized onions.
  23. Arrange black olives and additional anchovies (optional) on top.
  24. Bake the Pizza Saladier:
  25. Bake for 20 minutes or until the crust is golden brown and crispy.
  26. Let cool slightly before slicing and serving.
  27. Serve:
  28. Cut the Pizza Saladier into small bites.
  29. Enjoy as an appetizer with a glass of white wine.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=5vzda3N36Fk

poached_eggs.txt - Poached Eggs

Objectives

  • Learn how to make perfect poached eggs without any special equipment.
  • Understand the importance of water temperature and vinegar in poaching eggs.
  • Learn how to properly cook and cool poached eggs for optimal results.

Ingredients

  • Eggs
  • Water
  • Vinegar

Instructions

  1. Fill a stockpot with water, ensuring the water level is 6-7 centimeters high.
  2. Bring the water to a rolling boil.
  3. Add a few drops of vinegar to the boiling water.
  4. Carefully crack an egg into a small bowl.
  5. Aim for a boiling bubble in the water and gently drop the egg into the water.
  6. Immediately reduce the heat to a simmer, ensuring only small bubbles appear at the bottom of the pan.
  7. Allow the egg to cook for approximately 2-2.5 minutes, depending on the size of the egg.
  8. Check the egg after 2 minutes. If the white is still not fully set, cook for another 30 seconds.
  9. When the egg is cooked to your liking, gently remove it from the water using a slotted spoon.
  10. Immediately transfer the egg to a bowl of ice water to stop the cooking process.
  11. Once the egg is cool, remove it from the ice water and pat it dry.

poached_pear.txt - Poached Pear

Objectives

  • Learn how to poach pears in a classic French style.
  • Discover the secrets to achieving a perfect poached pear texture and flavor.
  • Master the art of preparing a delicious chocolate sauce to complement the poached pears.

Ingredients

  • 500-600 g sugar
  • Lemon zest
  • Half a fresh vanilla pod
  • 1 liter water
  • 1 pear
  • Lemon juice
  • Ice
  • 200 g chocolate (58% to 70% cacao)
  • Butter
  • Cream

Instructions

  1. Trim the end of the pear with a scissor.
  2. Remove the core using a knife and a melon baller or apple corer.
  3. Peel the pear with a peeler.
  4. Brush the pear evenly with lemon juice to prevent discoloration.
  5. Plunge the pear into ice water with lemon juice to maintain its color.
  6. In a saucepan, combine sugar, lemon zest, vanilla pod pieces, and water.
  7. Bring the mixture to a boil, then add the pear and ensure it's fully submerged in the syrup.
  8. Place a circle of parchment paper on top of the pears to prevent discoloration.
  9. Cover the saucepan with a lid and simmer for 15-20 minutes, or until the pears are cooked through.
  10. Remove the parchment paper and let the pears cool in the syrup.
  11. Prepare the chocolate sauce by melting chocolate and butter in a bain-marie.
  12. Gradually add warm cream to the melted chocolate, stirring until smooth and silky.
  13. To serve, arrange the poached pear on a plate, drizzle with chocolate sauce, and add a scoop of ice cream.
  14. Garnish with almonds, if desired.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=3j36xLDuTeQ

poach_trout.txt - Poached Trout with Court Bouillon

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a traditional French court bouillon for poaching fish
  • Understand the importance of slow simmering for a clear broth
  • Learn how to properly poach a trout using the court bouillon

Ingredients

Court Bouillon - 1.5 liters of water - 1.5 liters of white wine - 1 onion, sliced - 2 carrots, sliced - 1 bouquet garni - Parsley - Bay leaves - Thyme - Juniper berries - 1 tablespoon of peppercorns - 12 grams of salt

Trout - 1 trout, cleaned

Instructions

  1. Wash your hands thoroughly.
  2. Wash, peel, and slice the carrots and onions.
  3. Make a bouquet garni using parsley, bay leaves, thyme, and juniper berries.
  4. In a large pot, combine water, white wine, sliced onions, carrots, bouquet garni, peppercorns, and salt.
  5. Bring the mixture to a boil over high heat.
  6. Skim off any foam that forms on the surface.
  7. Reduce heat to a simmer and cook for 15 minutes.
  8. Turn off the heat and transfer the court bouillon to a separate container to cool down.
  9. Once the court bouillon is completely cold, place the cleaned trout in the pot.
  10. Bring the court bouillon to a simmer over medium heat.
  11. Cover the trout with parchment paper to prevent it from drying out.
  12. Poach the trout for 8-10 minutes, depending on its size.
  13. Carefully remove the trout from the court bouillon using a spatula.
  14. Place the trout on a plate lined with a clean white cloth to absorb excess liquid.
  15. Garnish the trout with parsley and lemon slices.
  16. Use a knife to make small incisions in the skin of the trout.
  17. Use a fork to gently roll the skin off the fish, being careful not to damage the flesh.
  18. Serve the poached trout with a beurre blanc or hollandaise sauce.
