sauce_americaine.txt - Sauce Américaine

Objectives

  • Learn the origin story of Sauce Américaine.
  • Master the technique of making a classic French seafood sauce.
  • Discover how to use a mortar and pestle to extract flavor from crab shells.

Ingredients

  • 1 kilo fish bones
  • 1 bouquet garni (carrots, onions, shallots)
  • 100 ml white wine
  • 3 cups water
  • 1 tablespoon butter
  • Blue swimmer crabs (or any type of crab)
  • Olive oil
  • Salt and pepper
  • Cayenne pepper
  • Cognac
  • 400 grams chopped tomatoes
  • Parsley (or tarragon)
  • Butter and flour (for béchamel)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the fish stock:
  2. Heat a pan over medium heat and melt butter.
  3. Add carrots, onions, and shallots and sweat for a few minutes.
  4. Add fish bones and stir to ensure they are submerged in the butter and vegetables.
  5. Pour in white wine and cook for 1 minute.
  6. Add 3 cups of water and bring to a boil.
  7. Reduce heat to a simmer and add the bouquet garni.
  8. Simmer for 30-40 minutes, skimming off any impurities.
  9. Strain the stock through a fine-mesh sieve into a clean pan.
  10. Clean and prepare the crabs:
  11. Remove the top shell of the crabs by gently pressing and pulling.
  12. Remove the gills from each crab.
  13. Cut the crabs into pieces using a sharp knife.
  14. Cook the crabs:
  15. Heat a large casserole pan over medium-high heat and add olive oil.
  16. Once the oil is hot, add the crabs and season with salt and pepper.
  17. Cook for 2-3 minutes, then flip the crabs to ensure even browning.
  18. Reduce heat to low.
  19. Sweat the vegetables:
  20. Add carrots, onions, and shallots to the pan and sweat for a few minutes without browning.
  21. Flambé:
  22. Increase heat to high.
  23. Pour in 50 ml of cognac and ignite it.
  24. Once the flames subside, stir to combine.
  25. Add the white wine and reduce:
  26. Pour in the white wine and reduce for 3-4 minutes.
  27. Add the fish stock and tomatoes:
  28. Pour in the fish stock and bring to a boil.
  29. Reduce heat to low and add the bouquet garni and a pinch of cayenne pepper.
  30. Add the chopped tomatoes and simmer for 20 minutes.
  31. Crush the crab shells:
  32. Using a mortar and pestle, crush the crab shells to extract flavor.
  33. Alternatively, use a rolling pin directly in the pan.
  34. Return the crushed shells to the sauce and simmer for an additional 15 minutes.
  35. Strain the sauce:
  36. Strain the sauce through a fine-mesh sieve into a clean pan.
  37. Thicken the sauce:
  38. In a separate pan, melt butter and whisk in an equal amount of flour to create a béchamel.
  39. Add the béchamel to the sauce and bring to a boil, whisking constantly until desired consistency is reached.
  40. Season and serve:
  41. Stir in chopped parsley (or tarragon) for added flavor.
  42. Serve the sauce hot alongside pan-fried crab.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=5Ie7mRVaXV4

sauce_bordelaise.txt - Sauce Bordelaise

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French sauce Bordelaise.
  • Master the techniques of reducing wine and stock for a rich, concentrated sauce.
  • Understand how to incorporate bone marrow for a luxurious flavor and texture.

Ingredients

  • Bone Marrow
  • Shallots
  • Thyme
  • Bay Leaf
  • Veal Stock (Demi-Glace)
  • Bordeaux Red Wine
  • Unsalted Butter
  • Flour
  • Salt
  • Black Pepper
  • Parsley

Instructions

  1. Prepare the bone marrow by soaking it in water for at least one hour.
  2. Melt butter in a 10-inch saute pan over medium-low heat.
  3. Add diced shallots and sweat them for 2 minutes without browning.
  4. Add the wine and raise the heat to a boil.
  5. Carefully flambe the wine to burn off the alcohol.
  6. Add thyme and bay leaves, reduce heat to medium-high, and reduce the wine until it forms a glaze (almost completely dry).
  7. Reduce the veal stock in a separate pan until it reaches a thick, sauce-like consistency.
  8. If necessary, thicken the stock with a beurre manié (equal parts butter and flour) or a thickening agent like cornstarch or arrowroot.
  9. Once the wine is reduced, add the reduced stock and continue to simmer until the sauce thickens.
  10. Poach the bone marrow in simmering water for 6-8 minutes.
  11. Strain the sauce through a sieve into a clean saucepan.
  12. Season the sauce with salt and pepper to taste.
  13. Finish the sauce by gently swirling in pieces of butter until it becomes glossy.
  14. Plunge the poached bone marrow into ice water, then drain and cut into small cubes.
  15. Add the bone marrow to the sauce and gently stir to incorporate.
  16. Garnish with fresh parsley before serving.
  17. Enjoy your classic Sauce Bordelaise with any red meat dish.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=aOWWy-f4gE8

sauce_espanol.txt - Sauce Espagnole

Objectives

  • Learn the history and origin of Sauce Espagnole.
  • Master the techniques for creating a classic Sauce Espagnole from brown stock.
  • Understand how to use the sauce as a foundation for other culinary creations.

Ingredients

  • 3 cups brown stock (from previous video)
  • 1/2 cup diced bacon
  • 1/4 cup butter
  • 1/4 cup flour
  • 1/2 cup diced carrots
  • 1/2 cup diced onions
  • 1/4 cup diced mushrooms
  • 1 tablespoon tomato paste
  • 2 cloves garlic
  • 1 bouquet garni (parsley stalks, thyme, bay leaves)
  • 1/2 cup chopped tomatoes (skinned)
  • 1 tablespoon cold butter

Instructions

  1. Prepare the mise en place:
  2. Dice bacon, carrots, onions, and mushrooms.
  3. Remove the germ from the garlic clove.
  4. Weigh butter and flour.
  5. Create a bouquet garni with parsley stalks, thyme, and bay leaves.
  6. Skin the tomatoes by blanching them in boiling water for 20 seconds, then shocking them in ice water.
  7. Heat the brown stock in a saucepan over medium heat, skimming off any scum that rises to the surface.
  8. In a large cast-iron pan, melt the butter over medium heat.
  9. Add the diced bacon to the pan and cook until lightly browned.
  10. Add the diced carrots and onions to the pan and cook until they have a slight color.
  11. Add the flour to the pan and stir to combine with the bacon, carrots, and onions.
  12. Cook the mixture on low heat, stirring constantly, until the roux develops a light brown color.
  13. Add the tomato paste to the pan and cook for a few minutes to remove the acidity.
  14. Pour the boiling brown stock into the pan with the roux mixture.
  15. Add the diced tomatoes, bouquet garni, and garlic cloves to the pan.
  16. Bring the sauce to a simmer and cook for 1.5 to 2 hours, stirring occasionally.
  17. Strain the sauce through a fine-mesh sieve into a clean saucepan.
  18. Return the strained sauce to the saucepan and bring to a simmer.
  19. Slowly whisk in the cold butter until it is fully incorporated.
  20. Adjust the seasoning with salt and pepper to taste.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=FMLp3x7Arnk

sauce_gribiche.txt - Sauce Gribiche

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a classic French sauce called Sauce Gribiche.
  • Understand the importance of using boiled eggs as the base.
  • Discover a delicious way to serve cold meats.

Ingredients

  • 2 boiled eggs
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • 1 tablespoon pepper
  • 1 tablespoon Dijon mustard
  • 1 tablespoon white wine vinegar
  • 1 cup oil
  • 1 tablespoon fresh parsley
  • 1 tablespoon fresh tarragon
  • 3 small gherkins
  • 1 tablespoon capers

Instructions

  1. Hard boil the eggs.
  2. Separate the egg yolks from the whites.
  3. Use a sieve or fork to finely crush the egg yolks into a powder.
  4. Chop the egg whites into small cubes.
  5. In a bowl, combine the powdered egg yolks, salt, pepper, mustard, and white wine vinegar.
  6. Gradually whisk in the oil until the sauce thickens and becomes emulsified.
  7. Finely chop the parsley and tarragon.
  8. Slice the gherkins and roughly chop the capers.
  9. Add the chopped herbs, sliced gherkins, and chopped capers to the sauce.
  10. Gently fold in the chopped egg whites.
  11. Refrigerate the sauce for at least 30 minutes before serving.
  12. Serve the sauce with cold meats.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=xjXnNw9SG38

sauce_groblas.txt - Sauce Groblas

Objectives

  • Learn to make a versatile butter sauce called Sauce Groblas.
  • Understand the importance of using fresh ingredients and proper heat control.
  • Learn how to make brown butter and use it as a base for a delicious sauce.

Ingredients

  • 1 tablespoon of oil
  • Croutons (soft part of white bread)
  • Capers
  • Parsley
  • 150 gr of butter
  • Juice of half a lemon
  • Salt

Instructions

  1. Prepare the croutons by toasting them in a pan with oil over medium heat until golden brown.
  2. Once the croutons are done, drain them on paper towels to remove excess oil.
  3. Make the brown butter by melting butter in a pan over medium heat.
  4. As the butter melts, it will start to foam and make a crackling noise. This is the milk solids separating.
  5. Continue cooking the butter until the noise subsides and the butter turns a light brown color.
  6. Remove the pan from the heat and add the lemon juice, salt, capers, and half pieces of lemon.
  7. Return the pan to very low heat and allow the ingredients to infuse for a minute.
  8. Taste the sauce and adjust the salt as needed.
  9. Right before serving, add the parsley and croutons to the sauce.
  10. Pour the sauce over your fish and enjoy!

sauce_leon.txt - Sauce Leon

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a classic French sauce using a homemade demiglace
  • Understand the importance of using quality ingredients, especially vinegar
  • Explore the application of culinary basics in creating a flavorful sauce

Ingredients

  • 1 chopped onion
  • Equal amount of white wine vinegar
  • Equal amount of white wine
  • Demiglace (homemade)
  • Cream (optional)
  • Parsley (optional)
  • Butter
  • Salt
  • Black pepper

Instructions

  1. Melt butter in a saucepan over medium heat.
  2. Add chopped onions and cook slowly until they have a light blonde coloration.
  3. Add equal amounts of white wine and white wine vinegar.
  4. Bring the mixture to a boil, then reduce the heat and simmer until the liquid has reduced by half.
  5. Add the homemade demiglace and continue to reduce until the sauce is slightly syrupy and coats the back of a spoon.
  6. Optionally, add a small amount of cream and reduce for a few more minutes.
  7. Remove from heat and filter the sauce.
  8. Season with salt, black pepper, and a pinch of parsley (optional).
  9. Serve over chicken, pork chops, or other meats.

sauce_mutard.txt - Sauce Mutard (Home Style)

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a simplified version of the classic French mustard sauce
  • Understand the concept of "cuisine de menage" and its importance in French cooking
  • Discover an easy alternative to the traditional hollandaise-based sauce mutard

Ingredients

  • 1 tablespoon butter
  • 1 tablespoon flour
  • 1 cup milk
  • 1 shallot
  • 1 clove garlic
  • 1 sprig thyme
  • 1 bay leaf
  • Salt and pepper
  • 1 tablespoon heavy cream
  • 1 teaspoon vinegar
  • 1 teaspoon mustard
  • Optional: Dijon mustard

Instructions

  1. Melt butter in a saucepan over medium heat.
  2. Whisk in flour and cook for 2 minutes, stirring constantly, to create a paste (roux).
  3. Remove from heat and set aside to cool completely.
  4. In a separate saucepan, combine milk, shallot, garlic, thyme, bay leaf, salt, and pepper.
  5. Bring to a simmer over medium heat.
  6. Remove from heat and set aside.
  7. Once the roux is cool, whisk in half of the flavored milk, straining it through a sieve.
  8. Stir until smooth, then add the remaining milk, straining again.
  9. Return to medium-low heat and cook, stirring constantly, until the sauce thickens.
  10. Reduce heat to low and whisk in heavy cream, vinegar, and mustard.
  11. Continue stirring until well combined.
  12. Taste and adjust seasoning as needed.
  13. Add a dash of Dijon mustard for a stronger mustard flavor (optional).
  14. Serve warm over chicken, fish, vegetables, or toasted sandwiches.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=WdSzne_T9Uo

sauce_piquant.txt - Sauce Piquant

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a sauce piquant, a classic French sauce.
  • Understand the components of a sauce and how to create a sauce base.
  • Explore alternative methods for making a sauce base without homemade stock.

Ingredients

  • 1 tablespoon oil
  • 1 piece of pork belly
  • 20 grams butter
  • 1 mirepoix (carrots, celery, onions)
  • 1 tablespoon toasted flour
  • 1 tablespoon tomato paste
  • 2 cups veal stock (or substitute with bone broth)
  • 100 ml dry white wine
  • 150 ml shallots
  • 150 ml white wine vinegar
  • 1 tablespoon fresh tarragon
  • 1 tablespoon fresh chervil
  • 1 tablespoon fresh parsley
  • 2 teaspoons gherkins

Instructions

  1. Brown the pork belly in a pan over medium heat until caramelized.
  2. Remove the pork belly and discard excess grease.
  3. Add butter to the pan and sauté the mirepoix for 1-2 minutes.
  4. Add the toasted flour and tomato paste, cooking for 1 minute to remove acidity.
  5. Pour in the veal stock and bring to a boil.
  6. Reduce heat and simmer for 15 minutes, adding 100 ml of white wine.
  7. In a separate pan, combine the shallots, white wine, and vinegar.
  8. Bring to a boil and reduce by half.
  9. Combine the reduced shallots, wine, and vinegar with the sauce base.
  10. Simmer for 10 minutes, then taste and adjust seasoning.
  11. Turn off the heat and stir in the fresh herbs and gherkins.
  12. Taste and adjust seasoning as needed.
  13. Serve over grilled pork or other meats.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=G-Al_qn7xZg

sauce_viers.txt - Sauce Viers

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple, versatile warm dressing called Sauce Viers.
  • Understand the importance of fresh, seasonal ingredients.
  • Discover how to adjust the flavor profile to your taste.

Ingredients

  • 1-2 large tomatoes, peeled and diced
  • 1 shallot, thinly diced
  • 2 cloves garlic, crushed
  • 1 tablespoon olive oil
  • 1/2 teaspoon coriander seeds, crushed
  • 1 tablespoon balsamic vinegar
  • 2 tablespoons fresh herbs (basil, tarragon, chives, parsley)
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • Pinch of sugar (optional)

Instructions

  1. Peel and seed the tomatoes, then chop them into small cubes.
  2. Thinly dice the shallot and crush the garlic cloves.
  3. In a small bowl, combine the olive oil, crushed coriander seeds, garlic, and shallots.
  4. Warm the oil mixture over low to medium heat in a saucepan.
  5. Add the diced tomatoes to the saucepan.
  6. Cook the mixture over low heat for 5-6 minutes, stirring occasionally, until the tomatoes soften slightly.
  7. Remove the saucepan from the heat and stir in the balsamic vinegar.
  8. Add the herbs, salt, pepper, and a pinch of sugar to taste.
  9. Let the sauce rest for 2-3 minutes to allow the flavors to meld.
  10. Taste the sauce and adjust the seasoning as needed.
  11. Serve the sauce warm over grilled fish, vegetables, or other dishes.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ObG0o2OTrec

savory_palmy.txt - Savory Palmy

Objectives

  • Create a simple, impressive snack for guests
  • Utilize pre-made puff pastry for quick and easy preparation
  • Impress friends with a French-inspired snack

Ingredients

  • 1 pre-made puff pastry sheet (rectangle shape)
  • Red pesto
  • Green pesto
  • Optional: Freshly grated Parmesan cheese

Instructions

  1. Spread one half of the puff pastry sheet with red pesto, leaving a small edge free.
  2. Spread the other half of the puff pastry sheet with green pesto, leaving a small edge free.
  3. Sprinkle a small amount of freshly grated Parmesan cheese on top, if desired.
  4. Roll the pastry sheet up from the pesto-spread side, folding the edges inwards.
  5. Repeat with the other half of the pastry sheet.
  6. Place the rolled pastry in the freezer for 10 minutes to firm up.
  7. Once firm, slice the pastry into 1-centimeter wide strips.
  8. Arrange the slices on a baking sheet, leaving some space between each piece.
  9. Bake in the oven at 350°F (175°C) for 15-18 minutes, or until golden brown.
  10. Cover the palmy with a piece of foil loosely placed on top to prevent burning.
  11. Remove from oven and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=j89W_6PHdeE

savory_puffs.txt - Savory Puffs

Objectives

  • Learn how to make savory puffs using a choux pastry.
  • Explore various flavor combinations for savory puffs.
  • Master the deep-frying technique for achieving crispy, airy puffs.

Ingredients

Choux Pastry

  • Water
  • Butter
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Grated nutmeg (optional)
  • Flour
  • Eggs

Flavor Options

  • Ham
  • Duck confit with mushrooms and parsley
  • Blue cheese

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Choux Pastry:
  2. In a saucepan, combine water, butter, salt, pepper, and nutmeg (optional).
  3. Heat over medium heat until the butter melts and the water boils.
  4. Remove from heat and add the flour all at once, stirring vigorously until a smooth dough forms (called a "panada").
  5. Return the pan to medium heat and cook for 2-3 minutes, stirring constantly, to dry out the panada.
  6. Transfer the panada to a bowl and let it cool slightly.
  7. Gradually incorporate the eggs one at a time, beating well after each addition, until a smooth, thick paste forms.
  8. Prepare the Flavor Fillings:
  9. Divide the choux pastry into three portions.
  10. Mix one portion with diced ham.
  11. Mix another portion with duck confit, chopped mushrooms, and parsley.
  12. Mix the final portion with crumbled blue cheese.
  13. Deep-Fry the Puffs:
  14. Heat oil in a deep fryer or large saucepan to 165°C (330°F).
  15. Using two teaspoons, scoop out small portions of the flavored choux pastry and carefully drop them into the hot oil.
  16. Fry for about 5 minutes, or until golden brown and puffed up.
  17. Remove the puffs from the oil and drain on paper towels.
  18. Serve:
  19. Serve the savory puffs warm and enjoy!

scallops_creme_de_shallot.txt - Scallops with Shallot Cream Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French shallot cream sauce (crème de shallots).
  • Understand the importance of reducing the sauce for a rich flavor.
  • Create a simple yet elegant dish by pairing scallops with shallot cream sauce.

Ingredients

  • Thinly sliced shallots
  • Tarragon
  • Unsalted butter
  • Dry white wine
  • Heavy whipping cream
  • Scallops
  • Cayenne pepper
  • Orange zest (optional)

Instructions

  1. Wash and dry scallops thoroughly to remove any impurities.
  2. Heat a pan over medium heat.
  3. Add shallots, tarragon, and white wine to the pan.
  4. Simmer until the wine is almost completely reduced.
  5. Add heavy cream and reduce for 5 minutes, allowing the flavors to infuse.
  6. Reduce heat to low and whisk in cold butter, bit by bit, until the sauce is smooth and creamy.
  7. Season the sauce with salt to taste.
  8. Strain the sauce through a sieve to remove any solids.
  9. Heat a pan with butter over medium heat.
  10. Sear scallops for 1-2 minutes per side until golden brown.
  11. Remove scallops from heat and let rest for 1 minute.
  12. Add a touch of cayenne pepper to the sauce for a hint of heat and color.
  13. To assemble the dish, place a dollop of sauce on a plate.
  14. Arrange seared scallops on top of the sauce.
  15. Garnish with orange zest (optional) and a sprig of tarragon.
  16. Serve immediately.

seafood_alar_moriken.txt - Seafood À la Morikène

Objectives

  • Learn a fast, delicious recipe for Seafood À la Morikène, a Brittany specialty.
  • Understand how to use a crayfish bisque to create a shortcut version of the classic American sauce.
  • Master the art of cooking seafood, including crabs, mussels, and fish, to perfection.

Ingredients

  • 2 tablespoons of olive oil
  • Blue swimming crabs (optional)
  • 1/2 cup dry white wine
  • 1 tablespoon of tomato paste
  • 1 clove of garlic
  • Fresh tomatoes or chopped peeled tomatoes
  • 1/2 liter of crayfish bisque
  • 1/2 cup of water
  • Salt and pepper
  • 2 tablespoons of heavy cream
  • 1 pinch of Espelette pepper (or cayenne pepper)
  • A touch of orange zest
  • Mussels
  • Fish (e.g., white fish)

Instructions

  1. Heat 2 tablespoons of olive oil in a large pan over high heat.
  2. Add the blue swimming crabs to the pan and cook until they turn red, about 5 minutes.
  3. Remove the crabs from the pan and set aside.
  4. Add the white wine to the pan and bring to a boil.
  5. Reduce the heat and simmer until the wine is almost completely evaporated.
  6. Add the tomato paste and cook for 30 seconds, stirring constantly.
  7. Add the garlic, fresh tomatoes, and the reserved crabs.
  8. Pour in the crayfish bisque and add enough water to create a sauce-like consistency.
  9. Bring the mixture to a simmer and cook for 10 minutes, or until the crabs are cooked through.
  10. Strain the sauce through a fine-mesh sieve, discarding the solids.
  11. Return the strained sauce to the pan and add the heavy cream, Espelette pepper, and orange zest.
  12. Bring the sauce to a simmer and cook until the cream is heated through.
  13. Add the mussels to the sauce and cover the pan with a lid.
  14. Cook for 6 minutes, or until the mussels open.
  15. Remove the mussels from the pan and set aside.
  16. Add the fish to the sauce and cook for a few minutes, or until it is cooked through.
  17. Return the mussels to the pan and warm through.
  18. Serve the seafood immediately.

Objectives

  • Experience the unique taste of sea urchins
  • Learn about the different types of sea urchins

Ingredients

  4. Enjoy the sea urchin roe directly, or add it to other dishes.
  5. Shuck the royal oysters, and enjoy them fresh.
  6. Savor the unique flavors of the sea urchins and oysters.

shallot_prep.txt - How to Prepare Shallots

Objectives

  • Learn how to properly peel and prepare shallots for cooking
  • Understand the different ways to cut shallots for various uses
  • Discover the key differences between shallots and onions in French cooking

Instructions

  1. Trim the ends of the shallot using a paring knife, but avoid removing too much.
  2. Make a small incision at the top and bottom of the shallot.
  3. Carefully peel the skin off the shallot, being careful not to damage the flesh.
  4. Wash the peeled shallot under running water.
  5. For thin slices, cut the shallot lengthwise, following the natural stripes.
  6. For chopped shallots, slice the shallot lengthwise, leaving a small portion uncut at the bottom.
  7. Make crosswise cuts across the sliced shallot to create small, diced pieces.
  8. Discard the uncut end and use the finely chopped shallots in sauces or other preparations.

shallow_poached_fish.txt - Shallow Poached Fish with White Wine Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn the simple and effective French technique of shallow poaching fish.
  • Master the creation of a classic white wine sauce.
  • Discover the versatility of this technique for different types of fish.

Ingredients

  • Fish fillet
  • 1-2 tablespoons shallot
  • 1 tablespoon butter
  • 100 ml white wine (or white vermouth)
  • Salt and pepper
  • 2-3 tablespoons cream
  • Fresh parsley
  • Optional: Fish stock, mushrooms, tomato, onions, saffron

Instructions

  1. Season the fish fillet with salt and pepper on one side.
  2. Place the fish fillet in a saute pan.
  3. Add 1-2 tablespoons of chopped shallots to the pan.
  4. Add a small piece of butter and a few sprigs of parsley to the pan (optional).
  5. Pour 100 ml of white wine into the pan.
  6. Cover the pan with a lid (a paper lid is recommended).
  7. Bring the liquid to a simmer over medium heat.
  8. Reduce the heat to low and let the fish cook gently for 7-10 minutes, depending on the thickness of the fillet.
  9. While the fish cooks, prepare the sauce:
  10. Bring the poaching liquid to a boil over high heat.
  11. Reduce the liquid for 1-2 minutes until it becomes syrupy.
  12. Add 2-3 tablespoons of cream to the sauce.
  13. Reduce the sauce for 1 minute.
  14. Season the sauce with salt, pepper, and fresh parsley.
  15. Carefully remove the cooked fish from the pan and place it on a plate.
  16. Add a small amount of the sauce to the plate to prevent the fish from drying out.
  17. Place the lid back on the fish while you finish the sauce.
  18. Return the fish to the sauce and heat gently to allow the fish to absorb the flavors.
  19. Serve the fish with the creamy sauce, garnished with parsley, lemon zest, and paprika (optional).

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=u3ypQ78brsM

sharpening_japanese_knife.txt - Sharpening Japanese Knives

Objectives

  • Understand the unique sharpening requirements of Japanese knives
  • Recognize the limitations of traditional sharpening methods for Japanese knives
  • Learn about the specialized tools and techniques required for sharpening Japanese knives

Instructions

  1. Avoid using traditional sharpening methods: Japanese knives cannot be sharpened using hand sharpeners, electric sharpeners, or steel.
  2. Invest in a sharpening stone: You'll need a sharpening stone, a stone holder, and potentially multiple stones with different grits.
  3. Master the art of stone sharpening: Sharpening Japanese knives on a stone requires proper technique, including using running water, a cloth, and specific hand movements.
  4. Consider professional sharpening: Sharpening Japanese knives on a stone is a specialized skill. If you're not comfortable with the process, consider contacting a professional for sharpening services.

shortcrust_pastry_by_hand.txt - Shortcrust Pastry by Hand

Objectives

  • Learn how to make shortcrust pastry using your hands.
  • Understand the importance of incorporating butter and flour correctly.
  • Discover a simple technique for making a versatile pastry for various dishes.

Ingredients

  • Flour
  • Pinch of salt
  • Egg yolk
  • Water
  • Butter

Instructions

  1. Pour flour onto a surface and create a volcano shape.
  2. Add a pinch of salt, egg yolk, and water into the center of the volcano.
  3. Mix the wet ingredients together thoroughly.
  4. Cut butter into small pieces and add them to the center.
  5. Sprinkle a small amount of flour on top of the butter.
  6. Use your hands to press the butter into the flour mixture, squeezing it out and creating a crumbly texture.
  7. Gradually add more flour, continuing to press and squeeze the mixture.
  8. Repeat steps 5-7 until the dough starts to come together and pulls away from your fingers.
  9. Use a plastic scrapper to gather any excess flour on the sides.
  10. Form the dough into a disc and wrap it in plastic wrap.
  11. Refrigerate the dough for at least 2 hours before using.
  12. Remove the dough from the refrigerator 30 minutes to 1 hour before rolling it out.
  13. Roll out the dough to your desired thickness and use it for your chosen recipe.

short_crust_pastry.txt - Short Crust Pastry

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a classic French short crust pastry
  • Understand the importance of using high-quality ingredients
  • Master the use of a food processor for pastry making

Ingredients

  • 125g butter (organic)
  • 1 egg (yolk only)
  • 50ml water
  • 2g salt
  • 12.5g caster sugar
  • 250g flour

Instructions

  1. In a food processor, combine the flour and butter. Pulse until the mixture resembles coarse crumbs.
  2. In a separate bowl, combine the egg yolk, water, salt, and sugar.
  3. Gradually add the wet ingredients to the dry ingredients in the food processor. Pulse until the dough just comes together.
  4. Turn the dough out onto a lightly floured surface. Form it into a ball and wrap tightly in plastic wrap.
  5. Refrigerate the dough for at least 2 hours.

sicilian_inspired_ratatouille.txt - Sicilian Inspired Ratatouille

Objectives

  • Create a flavorful, slow-cooked vegetable dish inspired by Sicilian cuisine.
  • Achieve a jammy consistency with tomatoes and aubergine.
  • Explore a unique combination of sweet and sour flavors.

Ingredients

  • 1 onion, diced
  • 1 celery stalk, diced
  • 1 clove garlic, crushed
  • 1 zucchini, diced
  • 1 aubergine, diced
  • 1/2 cup black olives, pitted
  • 1/4 cup sultanas
  • 1/4 cup pine nuts
  • 1 tablespoon capers
  • 1 teaspoon sugar
  • 1 tablespoon vinegar
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • Olive oil

Instructions

  1. Heat olive oil in a large pot over medium heat.
  2. Sear the aubergine for about 5 minutes, until lightly browned.
  3. Remove the aubergine from the pot and set aside.
  4. Add diced onions and celery to the pot and cook over low heat until softened.
  5. Remove the onions and celery and set aside.
  6. Add the zucchini to the pot and cook for 2-3 minutes, seasoning with salt.
  7. Remove the zucchini and set aside.
  8. Return the aubergine, onions, celery, and garlic to the pot.
  9. Add black olives, sultanas, pine nuts, capers, sugar, and vinegar.
  10. Add a small amount of water (about 50 ml).
  11. Cook over very low heat for 40 minutes, or until the mixture reaches a jammy consistency.
  12. After 40 minutes, add the sultanas and half of the zucchini.
  13. Continue cooking for another 15 minutes.
  14. The dish is done when there is no liquid remaining in the pot and the vegetables are tender.
  15. Optionally, toast pine nuts in a pan and use for decoration.
  16. Serve warm or cold.

silk_weaver_brain.txt - Silk Weaver's Brain

Objectives

  • Learn the history of "Silk Weaver's Brain" cheese dip
  • Prepare a fresh, flavorful cheese dip using traditional French ingredients
  • Understand the importance of letting the flavors infuse before serving

Ingredients

  • Crème fraîche
  • Fromage blanc (cottage cheese)
  • Fresh goat cheese
  • Shallot (1/2)
  • Garlic clove (1)
  • Fresh onion
  • Chives
  • Parsley
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Red wine vinegar (optional)
  • Walnut oil

Instructions

  1. Press the fromage blanc through a sieve to drain excess water. Refrigerate for 10-20 minutes.
  2. Chop shallots, garlic, onion, chives, and parsley.
  3. Combine the drained fromage blanc, goat cheese, and crème fraîche in a bowl.
  4. Mix well, incorporating all ingredients.
  5. Season with salt, pepper, and red wine vinegar (optional).
  6. Slowly incorporate walnut oil, mixing gently to create a light, creamy consistency.
  7. Add the chopped herbs and mix thoroughly.
  8. Transfer the mixture to a container and refrigerate for 30 minutes to an hour, allowing the flavors to infuse.
  9. Serve with toasted bread, enjoying the fresh, flavorful dip.

skillet_cheese_souffle.txt - Skillet Cheese Souffle

Objectives

  • Modernize the classic cheese souffle
  • Create a simpler, easier-to-make souffle
  • Serve souffle in a more convenient, shareable format

Ingredients

Base (Mouret) - 100g cold milk - Salt - Pepper - Nutmeg (grated) - 50g butter - 50g flour - 20g cheese (grated) - 1 egg yolk

Cream Mixture - 200g heavy cream - Salt - Pepper - 30g cheese (grated) - 1 drop of lemon juice

Egg Whites - 100g egg whites - Pinch of salt

Instructions

  1. Combine cold milk, salt, pepper, and nutmeg in a bowl. Set aside.
  2. Melt butter in a saucepan over low heat.
  3. Add flour and whisk until combined.
  4. Cook for 2 minutes over low heat.
  5. Gradually whisk in the cold milk mixture, starting with a small amount.
  6. Continue whisking until the mixture thickens into a paste.
  7. Add the remaining milk and whisk until smooth.
  8. Increase heat to medium and whisk constantly until the mixture thickens.
  9. Reduce heat to low and simmer for 2 minutes.
  10. Remove from heat and add grated cheese. Stir until melted.
  11. Whisk in one egg yolk.
  12. Transfer the mouret to a container and allow to cool.
  13. In a separate bowl, whisk egg whites with a pinch of salt until stiff peaks form.
  14. Warm heavy cream in a skillet over medium heat.
  15. Add salt, pepper, and grated cheese.
  16. Simmer until cheese is melted and cream thickens slightly.
  17. Remove from heat.
  18. Gently fold a small amount of the egg whites into the mouret to loosen the consistency.
  19. Fold in the remaining egg whites until just combined, avoiding overmixing.
  20. Pour the cream mixture into the bottom of the skillet.
  21. Carefully pour the souffle mixture over the cream.
  22. Bake in a preheated oven at 375°F (190°C) for 12-14 minutes.
  23. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=fqHyxJDj39Q

snails_in_garlic_butter.txt - Snails in Garlic Butter

Objectives

  • Learn how to find and prepare snails for home cooking
  • Master the French recipe for snails in garlic butter
  • Discover the proper way to eat and enjoy snails

Ingredients

  • Snails in brine (2 dozen)
  • Empty snail shells
  • 4 garlic cloves
  • 20 g shallots
  • Thyme (a few branches)
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 20 g parsley (flat leaf or curly)
  • 100 g soft butter
  • 1 liter of water
  • Vegetable stock (1/2 cube)
  • Salt
  • Pepper

Instructions

  1. Prepare the garlic butter:
  2. Combine garlic, shallots, thyme, parsley, and butter in a food processor.
  3. Blend until finely ground.
  4. Add salt and pepper to taste.
  5. Prepare the snails:
  6. Drain the snails from the brine and rinse them in clean water.
  7. Bring 1 liter of water, vegetable stock, thyme, and bay leaf to a boil.
  8. Reduce heat to a simmer and add the snails.
  9. Simmer for 2-3 minutes.
  10. Remove the snails from the water and let them rest at room temperature.
  11. Refrigerate the snails to accelerate the cooling process.
  12. Assemble the snails:
  13. Preheat the oven to 220°C (428°F).
  14. Place a layer of rock salt in a baking dish for stability.
  15. Place a small amount of garlic butter at the bottom of each empty snail shell.
  16. Place a snail in each shell, pushing it in gently.
  17. Top each snail with a generous amount of garlic butter.
  18. Bake for 10 minutes.
  19. Serve and enjoy:
  20. Use a snail fork or toothpick to extract the snail meat from the shell.
  21. Enjoy the snail meat and the flavorful garlic butter.
  22. Once the snails have cooled, you can drink the remaining butter from the shells.

soubise_sauce.txt - Soubise Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn the history and origin of the Soubise sauce
  • Master the technique of making a classic béchamel sauce
  • Create a smooth and flavorful Soubise sauce by glazing onions and incorporating them into a béchamel base

Ingredients

  • 1 onion, minced
  • 1/2 liter milk
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 3 cloves
  • 50 grams butter
  • 50 grams flour
  • 20 grams sugar
  • 2 tablespoons cream
  • Salt

Instructions

  1. Blanch the minced onion in boiling water for 2-3 minutes.
  2. Drain the onion and rinse under cold water.
  3. Warm the milk in a pan on low heat with a pinch of salt, a bay leaf, and half an onion with three cloves.
  4. Melt butter in a clean pan on low heat.
  5. Add flour to the melted butter and mix well to create a roux.
  6. Cook the roux for 1-2 minutes on very low heat and then set aside to cool.
  7. While the milk is heating, glaze the onion in a pan with butter and sugar over low heat for 15 minutes until soft and translucent.
  8. Strain the warm milk through a sieve to remove the onion and cloves.
  9. Whisk the cooled roux into the warm milk, ensuring all lumps are dissolved.
  10. Heat the milk mixture on medium-low heat, stirring constantly, until it thickens.
  11. Strain the glazed onions through a sieve to remove excess fat.
  12. Add the strained glazed onions to the thickened béchamel sauce and whisk to combine.
  13. Pass the sauce through a sieve or use a stick blender to create a smooth purée.
  14. Stir in 2 tablespoons of cream and reduce the sauce over low heat for 2-3 minutes.
  15. Serve the Soubise sauce over your choice of protein, such as pan-fried chicken or white meat.

souffle_crepes_caramelized_apple.txt - Souffle Crepes with Caramelized Apples

Objectives

  • Make a sweet souffle mixture with pastry cream and egg whites.
  • Cook the souffle mixture inside a crepe for a unique dessert.
  • Caramelize apples to add flavor and visual appeal.

Ingredients

  • 2-3 eggs
  • 20-40 grams of butter
  • 1 tablespoon of white sugar or icing sugar
  • Apples
  • Calvados
  • Pastry Cream (recipe in video description)

Instructions

  1. Caramelize the apples:
  2. Heat butter in a pan over medium to high heat.
  3. Add sugar and stir to combine.
  4. Increase heat and flambe the sugar.
  5. Reduce heat to low and cook for 1-2 minutes.
  6. Set aside.
  7. Prepare the egg whites:
  8. Beat egg whites with a pinch of salt and sugar until stiff peaks form.
  9. Assemble the souffle mixture:
  10. Warm the pastry cream slightly.
  11. Add egg yolks and a splash of Calvados to the pastry cream and whisk until smooth.
  12. Fold in some of the caramelized apples.
  13. Gently fold in the egg whites until just combined.
  14. Fill the crepes:
  15. Warm the crepes in the microwave.
  16. Place a crepe on a baking sheet lined with parchment paper.
  17. Fill the crepe with the souffle mixture.
  18. Bake the souffle crepes:
  19. Preheat oven to 200 degrees Celsius.
  20. Bake for 6-7 minutes, or until the souffle has puffed up.
  21. Sprinkle with icing sugar 2 minutes before the end of baking time.
  22. Serve:
  23. Remove from the oven and let cool slightly.
  24. Garnish with additional caramelized apples if desired.
  25. Enjoy!

souffle_grand_marnier.txt - Souffle Grand Marnier

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a classic Souffle Grand Marnier
  • Understand the key elements of a souffle, including the pastry cream and meringue
  • Discover techniques for ensuring a souffle rises properly

Ingredients

Pastry Cream - 500ml milk - 1/2 vanilla bean (seeds scraped) - 2 egg yolks - 75g sugar - 25g flour - 1 tablespoon grand marnier (or other liquor) - 1 egg yolk (for the pastry cream) - Zest of 1 orange (optional)

Meringue - 130g egg whites (about 4 egg whites) - 75g sugar - Pinch of salt

Other - Grand Marnier (for soaking biscuits) - 1 tablespoon butter - Sugar (for coating ramekins) - Biscuits (from last week's video)

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 200 degrees Celsius (400 degrees Fahrenheit) with no fan.
  2. Make the pastry cream:
  3. Combine milk, vanilla bean, and seeds in a saucepan over medium-low heat.
  4. In a separate bowl, whisk together 2 egg yolks and sugar until light and frothy.
  5. Gradually whisk in the flour until fully incorporated.
  6. Slowly pour half of the warm milk into the egg yolk mixture, whisking constantly.
  7. Pour the mixture back into the saucepan with the remaining milk.
  8. Cook over medium-low heat, whisking constantly, until the cream thickens (about 1 minute 40 seconds).
  9. Continue cooking for 2-3 minutes after it boils, stirring constantly.
  10. Remove from heat and transfer to a clean container.
  11. Cover with plastic wrap, ensuring it touches the surface of the cream.
  12. Set aside at room temperature.
  13. Prepare the ramekins:
  14. Melt butter in a small pan.
  15. Use a pastry brush to coat the inside of each ramekin with butter, creating lines to help the souffle rise evenly.
  16. Fill each ramekin with sugar, then invert and tap to remove excess.
  17. Prepare the biscuits:
  18. Cut the biscuits into small pieces.
  19. Soak the biscuits in grand marnier, ensuring they are fully immersed.
  20. Make the meringue:
  21. In a clean bowl, whisk together egg whites, a small amount of sugar, and a pinch of salt until foamy.
  22. Gradually add the remaining sugar in three parts, waiting for the foam to form before adding more.
  23. Continue whisking until the egg whites are stiff and glossy.
  24. Combine the pastry cream and meringue:
  25. Gently fold a quarter of the meringue into the warm pastry cream.
  26. Fold in the remaining meringue in two or three additions, being careful not to deflate the meringue.
  27. Assemble the souffle:
  28. Place a few pieces of soaked biscuits in the bottom of each ramekin.
  29. Spoon the souffle mixture into the ramekins, filling them to the brim.
  30. Use a spatula to smooth out the surface of the souffle.
  31. To prevent sticking, run your thumb around the edge of each ramekin, creating a seal.
  32. Bake the souffles:
  33. Place the ramekins in the preheated oven.
  34. Bake for 10-12 minutes.
  35. Serve immediately:
  36. Souffles will deflate quickly, so serve immediately after baking.

Optional: - For extra support, wrap each ramekin in parchment paper before baking.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=FyqMA4yy6dI

souffle_omelette_de_la_mer_polar.txt - Souffle Omelette de la Mer Polar

Objectives

  • Learn the history of the Souffle Omelette de la Mer Polar
  • Make a classic Souffle Omelette de la Mer Polar
  • Discover the secret of the Souffle Omelette de la Mer Polar

Ingredients

  • 2 eggs
  • 20 grams of salted butter

Instructions

  1. Crack two eggs into a copper bowl.
  2. Whisk the eggs using an electric mixer until foamy and thick.
  3. Preheat a thick pan over high heat.
  4. Add the salted butter to the pan and melt.
  5. Pour the foamy egg mixture into the pan.
  6. Cook the omelette for about a minute, allowing the bottom to set.
  7. Tilt the pan and move it around the heat to cook the edges evenly.
  8. Reduce the heat to low and continue cooking until the edges are set and the center is slightly uncooked.
  9. Slide the omelette onto a plate.
  10. Fold the omelette in thirds.
  11. Serve immediately with a garnish of your choice, such as mushrooms or blue cheese.

steak_tartare.txt - Steak Tartare à la Paul Bocuse

Objectives

  • Learn to make a traditional French Steak Tartare.
  • Discover the benefits of grinding your own meat for improved flavor and quality.
  • Master the technique of mixing ingredients for a delicious and fragrant tartar.

Ingredients

  • 1 beef fillet (cut into cubes)
  • 1 egg yolk
  • 1 tablespoon Dijon mustard
  • 1/4 cup olive oil
  • 1 tablespoon chopped shallots
  • 1 tablespoon chopped capers
  • 1 tablespoon chopped gherkins
  • 1 tablespoon chopped parsley
  • 1 tablespoon chopped chives
  • 1 teaspoon Worcestershire sauce
  • 1/2 teaspoon Tabasco sauce
  • Salt and freshly ground black pepper to taste

Instructions

  1. Grind the beef fillet using a meat grinder or by hand.
  2. Place the ground beef in a bowl and refrigerate until cold.
  3. In a separate bowl, whisk together the egg yolk and Dijon mustard.
  4. Slowly drizzle in the olive oil, whisking continuously until the mixture emulsifies and thickens.
  5. Add the shallots, capers, gherkins, parsley, chives, Worcestershire sauce, and Tabasco sauce to the egg yolk mixture.
  6. Season with salt and pepper to taste.
  7. Combine the cold ground beef with the dressing, mixing gently.
  8. Serve immediately or refrigerate for later.
  9. To plate, use a food ring to mold the tartar into a neat shape.
  10. Garnish with chopped herbs, a few drops of Tabasco sauce, and salt and pepper.

stewed_pears_or_apples.txt - Poires au sirop vanillé

Objectives

  • Learn how to stew pears or apples in a simple, French-inspired recipe
  • Understand the importance of lemon juice to prevent browning
  • Master the technique for creating a perfect vanilla syrup

Ingredients

  • 2 lemons
  • 1 glass of water
  • pears or apples
  • 1/2 liter of water
  • 200 grams of sugar
  • vanilla sugar or vanilla extract

Instructions

  1. Squeeze the juice of two lemons into a large bowl.
  2. Add one glass of water to the lemon juice.
  3. Core and quarter the pears or apples.
  4. Place the pears or apples in the lemon juice and water mixture.
  5. In a large pan, combine half a liter of water, 200 grams of sugar, and vanilla sugar or extract.
  6. Heat the pan over medium-high heat, stirring until the sugar dissolves.
  7. Add the pears or apples to the syrup.
  8. Bring the syrup to a boil, then reduce heat to a gentle simmer.
  9. Cook the pears or apples for 5-10 minutes, or until tender.
  10. Remove the pears or apples from the syrup and place them in a clean bowl.
  11. Strain the syrup through a fine-mesh sieve or cheesecloth, lined with paper towels, to remove any impurities.
  12. Let the syrup cool to room temperature, then refrigerate.
  13. Serve the pears or apples cold, drizzled with the syrup.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=InS5SCOobGE

stuffed_bell_peppers.txt - Stuffed Bell Peppers

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare bell peppers for stuffing.
  • Create a flavorful, meat-free stuffing for bell peppers.
  • Bake stuffed bell peppers to perfection.

Ingredients

  • 4 bell peppers
  • Olive oil
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • 1 1/2 tablespoons olive oil
  • 1 onion, chopped
  • 2 tablespoons garlic, minced
  • Toasted nuts (optional)
  • Sultanas (raisins)
  • Parsley, chopped
  • Rice
  • Tomatoes, chopped
  • Smoked paprika
  • Water
  • Almond milk or ground almonds (optional)
  • Breadcrumbs (optional)

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 200 degrees Celsius (400 degrees Fahrenheit).
  2. Cut bell peppers in half, leaving the stem intact.
  3. Gently remove seeds and ribs from the bell peppers.
  4. Brush the inside and outside of the bell peppers with olive oil.
  5. Season with salt and pepper.
  6. Place bell peppers in the oven and bake for 15 minutes.
  7. While the peppers are baking, heat olive oil in a pan over medium heat.
  8. Add chopped onion and cook for 10 minutes until softened.
  9. Add minced garlic and toasted nuts (optional) and cook for 1 minute.
  10. Remove peppers from oven and transfer to a baking dish.
  11. Combine the onion mixture with sultanas, parsley, rice, tomatoes, smoked paprika, and a tablespoon of olive oil.
  12. Season the stuffing with salt and pepper.
  13. Fill the bell peppers with the stuffing, leaving some space at the top.
  14. Pour a small amount of water into the bottom of the baking dish to prevent sticking.
  15. Bake for 20 minutes at 200 degrees Celsius (400 degrees Fahrenheit).
  16. Reduce oven temperature to 190 degrees Celsius (375 degrees Fahrenheit).
  17. After 20 minutes, check the peppers for dryness.
  18. Sprinkle with almond milk or ground almonds, and drizzle with olive oil.
  19. Return to the oven and bake until golden brown.
  20. Serve hot and enjoy.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=HmfN6Qkerrk

stuffed_cabbage.txt - Stuffed Cabbage

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a stuffed cabbage recipe using a savory cabbage.
  • Understand the difference between the complex and easy ways to make stuffed cabbage.
  • Learn how to prepare the cabbage, blanch the leaves, and make the stuffing.

Ingredients

  • 1 Savoy cabbage
  • 1 tablespoon olive oil
  • 1 onion
  • 300 grams shredded cabbage hearts
  • 2 tablespoons of salt
  • 1/2 bacon
  • 4 juniper berries
  • Thyme
  • 50ml chicken stock
  • 1 tablespoon olive oil
  • Celery
  • Carrot
  • Garlic
  • Bay leaf
  • Tomato puree
  • Chicken stock

Instructions

  1. Discard the ugly leaves of the cabbage.
  2. Detach the good looking leaves from the cabbage by making a cut where the leaf is attached.
  3. Trim, chop, and mince the heart of the cabbage.
  4. Blanch the leaves in boiling salted water for 2 minutes.
  5. Fry the onion with olive oil in a cast iron pan for 10 minutes.
  6. Brown the pork in the pan on high heat.
  7. Add half the bacon to the pan and mix with the onions, pork, and bacon.
  8. Add juniper berries and thyme to the pan.
  9. Add half of the shredded cabbage hearts to the pan, mix, and let it reduce.
  10. Add the remaining shredded cabbage hearts and cook for 10 minutes on medium heat.
  11. Add salt and pepper to the stuffing.
  12. Add 50 ml of chicken stock to the stuffing and cook for 15 minutes.
  13. Let the stuffing cool.
  14. Take a portion of the stuffing and roll it into a parcel.
  15. Tie the parcel with string.
  16. Preheat the oven to 200 degrees Celsius.
  17. Heat 1 tablespoon of olive oil in a cast iron pot.
  18. Add celery, carrot, garlic, bay leaf, juniper berries, and thyme to the pot and cook for a few minutes.
  19. Add the remaining bacon to the pot and cook for another 2 minutes.
  20. Add tomato puree to the pot and reduce the heat.
  21. Place the cabbage rolls on top of the mixture in the pot.
  22. Pour chicken stock into the pot, ensuring the cabbage rolls are submerged halfway.
  23. Drizzle olive oil over the cabbage rolls.
  24. Cover the pot with a lid and bake in the oven for 1.5 to 2 hours.
  25. Remove the cabbage rolls from the oven and let them cool.
  26. Remove the string from the cabbage rolls and add some of the reduced stock on top.
  27. Serve and enjoy.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=rLRs1gPto-A

stuffed_muscles_burgundy_butter.txt - Stuffed Muscles with Burgundy Butter

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare a classic French dish, stuffed muscles with Burgundy butter.
  • Master the art of making a flavorful and aromatic Burgundy butter.
  • Discover a simple and delicious way to cook mussels.

Ingredients

  • 125g soft butter
  • 10g garlic (germ removed)
  • 20g shallots
  • 20g parsley
  • Breadcrumbs
  • 1kg mussels
  • 40g shallots
  • White wine
  • Salt
  • Pepper

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Burgundy butter:
  2. In a bowl, combine softened butter, garlic (germ removed), shallots, parsley, and breadcrumbs.
  3. Mix well until all ingredients are thoroughly incorporated.
  4. Season with salt and pepper to taste.
  5. Cook the mussels:
  6. Heat a tablespoon of unsalted butter in a pan.
  7. Add 40g of shallots and cook for 1-2 minutes until softened.
  8. Add mussels, stir to coat with shallots and butter.
  9. Pour in a little white wine and cover the pan.
  10. Cook on high heat for 5-6 minutes until mussels open.
  11. Remove mussels from the pan and set aside to cool.
  12. Assemble the stuffed muscles:
  13. Remove the top shell from each mussel, discarding it.
  14. Using a spatula, coat the inside of each mussel with Burgundy butter.
  15. Place the mussels in a container.
  16. Sprinkle the top of each mussel with breadcrumbs.
  17. Grill the stuffed muscles:
  18. Preheat a grill to medium heat.
  19. Place the mussels on a plate lined with rock salt.
  20. Grill until the butter melts and becomes foamy.
  21. Serve immediately with a squeeze of lemon.

stuffed_mushroom_champion.txt - Stuffed Mushroom Champion

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a vegetarian stuffed mushroom dish.
  • Understand the process of preparing the duxelles mushroom stuffing.
  • Discover tips for enhancing the visual appeal of stuffed mushrooms.

Ingredients

  • Mushrooms (various sizes, including large ones for stuffing, smaller ones for the duxelles, and oyster mushrooms)
  • 1 onion (finely sliced)
  • 1 shallot (finely sliced)
  • Butter
  • Parsley (chopped)
  • Lemon (for juice)
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Olive oil
  • Tomato sauce (optional)
  • Breadcrumbs (optional)
  • Farmhouse goat cheese (optional)
  • Tomato paste (optional)
  • Dill (optional)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the mushrooms: Select large mushrooms for stuffing, remove the stems, and reserve them. Trim smaller mushrooms and place them in a food processor.
  2. Make the duxelles: Finely slice the onion and shallot. In a pan, melt butter over medium heat. Add the onion and shallot and sweat for 2 minutes.
  3. Add the mushrooms to the pan and cook until well combined. Season with salt, pepper, and a hint of lemon juice.
  4. Simmer the mixture over low heat until it is totally dry (about 15 minutes).
  5. Stir in chopped parsley. The duxelles is now ready.
  6. Prepare the garnish: Heat olive oil in a pan over high heat. Fry forest mushrooms and oyster mushrooms until they are lightly browned.
  7. Place the fried mushrooms on a kitchen towel to absorb excess oil.
  8. Stuff the mushrooms: Brush olive oil on a baking tray. Fill the large mushrooms with the duxelles, creating a mound. Add a small amount of tomato sauce or breadcrumbs on top (optional).
  9. Repeat the stuffing process for all the large mushrooms and any fancy mushrooms you have.
  10. Bake the stuffed mushrooms in the oven at 170°C (340°F) for 30 minutes.
  11. Optional: Add breadcrumbs to larger mushrooms to absorb excess moisture.
  12. Arrange the stuffed mushrooms on a platter with the garnish and other desired ingredients.
  13. Add a bit of color and texture to the platter by arranging olives, lemon slices, bread, and other ingredients. 14.

stuffed_tomatoes_provence.txt - Stuffed Tomatoes from Provence

Objectives

  • Learn to make stuffed tomatoes, a classic Provençal dish.
  • Understand the importance of choosing the right tomatoes for this recipe.
  • Discover the secrets to creating a flavorful and moist stuffing.

Ingredients

  • Large, juicy tomatoes
  • Pork, chicken, and beef stuffing mix (raw)
  • Duck set of mushrooms (or other mushrooms)
  • Parsley
  • Garlic
  • Madeira wine (or cognac or Armagnac)
  • Lamb cutlets (optional, for sauce)
  • Vegetable stock
  • Breadcrumbs
  • Salt
  • Black pepper
  • Olive oil
  • Butter

Instructions

  1. Cut the top off the tomatoes, leaving a thick base and a decent-sized "hat".
  2. Carefully remove the inside of the tomatoes with a spoon, leaving some flesh inside.
  3. Sprinkle salt inside the tomatoes and place them upside down in a dish to drain.
  4. Prepare the stuffing by mixing the meat, parsley, salt, mushrooms, and tomato flesh.
  5. Add Madeira wine (or cognac or Armagnac) and garlic to the stuffing.
  6. Mix well and taste to adjust seasoning.
  7. Stuff the tomatoes with the mixture, filling all cavities.
  8. Top each tomato with breadcrumbs.
  9. Place the stuffed tomatoes in a buttered dish.
  10. Bake the tomatoes without the "hats" at 180°C (356°F) for 20-25 minutes.
  11. While the tomatoes bake, prepare the sauce by browning lamb cutlets, deglazing with tomato juice, adding vegetable stock, rosemary, and black pepper.
  12. Simmer the sauce for 15 minutes.
  13. Drain any excess juice from the tomatoes during baking.
  14. After 20-25 minutes, place the tomato "hats" on top and continue baking for another 10 minutes.
  15. Serve the stuffed tomatoes with the lamb sauce.

Note: This recipe was unsuccessful due to the type of tomatoes used. The video recommends using tomatoes specifically for stuffing and avoiding fan-forced ovens.

stuffed_turnip_mushroom.txt - Stuffed Turnip with Mushrooms

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare and cook stuffed turnips with mushrooms.
  • Discover a unique and flavorful recipe using turnips as the main ingredient.
  • Master the technique of emptying and carving turnips for a beautiful presentation.

Ingredients

  • Turnips
  • Mushrooms
  • Shallots
  • Butter
  • Vegetable Stock
  • Breadcrumbs

Instructions

  1. Wash and trim the turnips.
  2. Use a dough cutter to remove a circle from the top of the turnip.
  3. Use a melon baller to carve out the flesh of the turnip, leaving a hollow shell.
  4. Blanch the turnip shells in boiling water for a short amount of time to remove bitterness and pre-cook them.
  5. While the shells are blanching, prepare the turnip flesh by finely chopping it or using a food processor.
  6. In a pan, melt butter and cook the chopped turnip flesh for 5-6 minutes.
  7. In a food processor, combine mushrooms and shallots.
  8. Cook the mushroom mixture in a pan for 6-8 minutes, removing excess moisture until they are dry.
  9. Combine the cooked turnip flesh and mushroom mixture.
  10. Fill the blanched turnip shells with the mushroom and turnip mixture.
  11. Add a tablespoon of vegetable stock to each turnip.
  12. Sprinkle breadcrumbs over the filled turnips.
  13. Place the turnips in a baking tray and pour a half-glass of vegetable stock into the bottom of the tray.
  14. Bake the turnips for 40 minutes at 210 degrees Celsius (or 190 degrees Celsius for a non-fan oven).
  15. Baste the turnips with the stock every 15 minutes during baking.
  16. After baking, let the turnips rest for 15 minutes before serving.

sufle_flambe_omelet.txt - Soufflé Flambé Omelette

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a classic French Soufflé Flambé Omelette.
  • Understand the importance of proper pan size and heat control for successful cooking.
  • Learn how to create a visually impressive and delicious dessert.

Ingredients

  • 2 egg yolks
  • 1/4 cup sugar
  • 1 tablespoon Cointreau or other orange liquor
  • 3 egg whites
  • 1/2 teaspoon lemon juice
  • Pinch of salt
  • 1 teaspoon sugar
  • 2 tablespoons butter
  • 20 grams butter for the pan
  • Additional butter for greasing the plate

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 200°C (400°F).
  2. Prepare a mixing bowl and a stand mixer with a whisk attachment.
  3. In the mixing bowl, whisk together the egg yolks, sugar, and Cointreau until the mixture is light and frothy.
  4. In the stand mixer, whisk the egg whites with a pinch of salt and lemon juice on low to medium speed until the mixture doubles in volume.
  5. Gradually add the remaining sugar to the egg whites and increase the speed to high until stiff peaks form.
  6. Gently fold the egg white meringue into the egg yolk mixture using a rubber spatula, being careful not to deflate the meringue.
  7. Heat a 24 cm (9.5 inch) non-stick pan over high heat.
  8. Add 20 grams of butter to the pan and swirl to coat.
  9. Pour the omelet mixture into the hot pan and spread it evenly.
  10. Immediately reduce the heat to low and cook for 2-3 minutes, or until the bottom of the omelet is lightly browned.
  11. Grease a heat-proof plate with butter.
  12. Carefully slide the omelet onto the prepared plate using a spatula.
  13. Fold the omelet in half, then fold it in half again.
  14. Place the folded omelet in the preheated oven for 4-5 minutes, or until puffed and set.
  15. While the omelet is in the oven, warm the Cointreau (or other liquor) over low heat without boiling.
  16. Remove the omelet from the oven and immediately pour the warmed liquor over the top.
  17. Carefully light the liquor with a match or lighter, and flambé the omelet.
  18. Allow the flames to die down before serving immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=W-ljYW3aleA

sun_tart.txt - Sun Tart

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a French sun tart appetizer.
  • Discover different filling options for the sun tart.
  • Understand the importance of cold ingredients and proper baking techniques.

Ingredients

  • 2 discs of puff pastry
  • 3 slices of ham
  • 2 onions
  • 100-150 ml of cream
  • Grated cheese (amount to taste)
  • 1 egg (for egg wash)
  • Butter (for sauteing onions)

Instructions

  1. Cut two equal-sized discs of puff pastry. Place them on plates and freeze them.
  2. Prepare the filling:
    • In a food processor, combine ham, onions, and cream.
    • Saute onions in butter until softened.
    • Add cooked onions to the food processor and blend until finely chopped.
  3. Spread the filling on one puff pastry disc, leaving a small edge for sealing.
  4. Sprinkle grated cheese over the filling.
  5. Brush the edges of the filled pastry disc with egg wash.
  6. Remove the second puff pastry disc from the freezer and place it on top of the filling.
  7. Press the edges of the top pastry disc to seal it to the bottom.
  8. Use a glass to press a circle in the center of the top pastry disc.
  9. Cut the pastry around the circle, stopping before reaching the center.
  10. Twist each cut section to create the sun-like shape.
  11. Brush the entire sun tart with egg wash for a golden color.
  12. Bake the sun tart at 180 degrees Celsius for 25-30 minutes, until golden brown and the filling is cooked through.
  13. Let the sun tart cool slightly before serving.
  14. To serve, pull apart the sun tart sections to create individual slices.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=jMnLN4eZTh4

supreme_of_orange.txt - Supreme of Orange

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare a supreme of orange, a skinless quarter of fruit.
  • Understand the technique for peeling and cutting the orange.
  • Discover a simple dessert idea using the supreme of orange.

Ingredients

  • 1 orange

Instructions

  1. Wash the orange thoroughly.
  2. Cut both ends of the orange to expose the flesh.
  3. Peel the orange, following the shape of the fruit, removing the skin and a small amount of flesh.
  4. Use a sharp knife with a thin blade to cut just before the skin on each side of the orange, separating the quarters.
  5. Discard any untidy quarters.
  6. Squeeze any remaining juice from the orange and discard.
  7. Place the supreme of orange quarters in a glass.
  8. Garnish with your preferred toppings, such as a sprig of mint.
  9. Enjoy your simple dessert!

supreme_sauce.txt - Supreme Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a classic French Supreme Sauce
  • Master the techniques of making a roux, velouté, and transforming a mother sauce into a small sauce
  • Understand the versatility of this sauce for poultry dishes

Ingredients

  • 15 grams plain butter
  • 15 grams plain flour
  • Clear chicken stock
  • Heavy cream
  • Lemon juice
  • Salt
  • Cayenne pepper
  • Nutmeg
  • Optional: Roasting pan drippings (from chicken or turkey)

Instructions

  1. Melt 15 grams of plain butter in a saucepan over medium heat.
  2. Add 15 grams of plain flour to the melted butter and whisk until combined.
  3. Reduce heat to low and cook the roux for 4-6 minutes, stirring occasionally, until it turns a light blonde color.
  4. Remove the roux from the heat and set aside to cool.
  5. Bring the chicken stock to a boil.
  6. Gradually whisk the cooled roux into the boiling chicken stock, ensuring all the roux is incorporated and dissolved.
  7. Return the mixture to medium heat and bring to a simmer.
  8. Simmer for 2-3 minutes, allowing the sauce to thicken slightly.
  9. Add heavy cream to the simmering sauce.
  10. Continue simmering for 3-4 minutes, stirring occasionally, until the sauce reaches a desired consistency.
  11. Reduce heat to low and add optional ingredients, such as roasting pan drippings, salt, cayenne pepper, and white pepper.
  12. Stir in a few pieces of butter to finish the sauce.
  13. Add a squeeze of lemon juice and a pinch of grated nutmeg.
  14. Stir gently and allow the sauce to infuse for 2-3 minutes on very low heat.
  15. Strain the sauce through a fine-mesh sieve into a clean saucepan to remove any lumps or particles.
  16. Serve the sauce warm over chicken, turkey, or other poultry dishes.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=zNAbP9Ycolg

sweet_and_sour_sauce.txt - Sweet and Sour Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple sweet and sour sauce
  • Transform the base sauce into three variations: orange, mint, and port
  • Use the sauces to enhance dishes like pulled pork and lamb

Ingredients

  • 100g Coconut sugar or raw sugar
  • 100ml White wine vinegar
  • 50ml Water

Instructions

  1. Combine the sugar, vinegar, and water in a saucepan.
  2. Heat over medium heat, stirring occasionally.
  3. Bring the mixture to a simmer and continue cooking until the sugar dissolves and the sauce thickens.
  4. Once the sauce reaches a syrupy consistency, remove from heat and let cool.
  5. The base sauce is ready to be used on its own or transformed into other variations.

Orange Sauce

  1. Reduce orange juice by half.
  2. Combine the reduced orange juice with the base sauce.
  3. Adjust the sweetness and tanginess to taste.

Mint Sauce

  1. Chop fresh mint leaves.
  2. Stir the mint leaves into the base sauce.
  3. Let the sauce infuse for at least 30 minutes.
  4. Strain the sauce to remove the mint leaves.

Port Sauce

  1. Reduce port wine by half.
  2. Combine the reduced port wine with the base sauce.
  3. Adjust the sweetness and intensity of the port flavor to taste.

sweet_shortcrust_pastry.txt - Sweet Shortcrust Pastry (Pâte Sucrée)

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a sweet shortcrust pastry dough using a food processor
  • Understand the importance of cold butter and proper mixing techniques
  • Prepare the dough for blind baking

Ingredients

  • 250 grams plain flour
  • 100 grams confectionery sugar (icing sugar)
  • 150 grams plain butter, cubed
  • 1 egg
  • 1 tablespoon water
  • Pinch of salt

Instructions

  1. In a food processor, combine 250 grams of plain flour and 100 grams of confectionery sugar.
  2. Pulse the mixture briefly to combine the ingredients.
  3. Add 150 grams of cubed cold butter to the food processor.
  4. Pulse the mixture for about a minute, until it resembles coarse crumbs.
  5. In a separate bowl, whisk together 1 egg, 1 tablespoon of water, and a pinch of salt.
  6. Pour the egg mixture into the food processor and run it continuously until a dough forms.
  7. Stop the food processor as soon as a dough forms.
  8. Remove the dough from the food processor and shape it into a disc.
  9. Wrap the dough tightly in plastic wrap and refrigerate for at least 2 hours.
  10. Once chilled, the dough is ready for blind baking.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=jvTl8nLvKL4

tarte_provencal.txt - Tarte Provençal

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple and delicious summery tart.
  • Create a rustic dish using a pre-made puff pastry.
  • Combine the flavors of tomatoes, mustard, and herbs in a savory tart.

Ingredients

  • 1 kilo fresh red tomatoes, sliced
  • 1 pre-rolled puff pastry
  • Dijon mustard (2 tablespoons)
  • Passata (tomato sauce)
  • Breadcrumbs
  • Salt
  • Cracked pepper
  • Italian herbs
  • French herbs

Instructions

  1. Preheat the oven to 200 degrees Celsius (420 degrees Fahrenheit).
  2. Place the puff pastry on a baking tray and sprinkle with flour.
  3. Fold the edges of the pastry to create a dish shape.
  4. Spread Dijon mustard evenly over the pastry base.
  5. Add a small amount of passata and mix it with the mustard.
  6. Sprinkle breadcrumbs over the mustard mixture.
  7. Arrange the sliced tomatoes over the breadcrumbs.
  8. Season with salt, cracked pepper, and herbs.
  9. Bake for 45 minutes.
  10. Let cool slightly before slicing and serving.

tartiflette.txt - Tartiflette

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a traditional French Tartiflette dish.
  • Understand the importance of using Reblochon cheese and its unique characteristics.
  • Discover the proper layering technique for a delicious and cheesy result.

Ingredients

  • 500 grams Reblochon cheese
  • 200 grams smoked bacon
  • 1 medium onion
  • 1 kilo waxy potatoes
  • Olive oil

Instructions

  1. Slice the potatoes into thin pieces, about half a centimeter thick, and dry them thoroughly with a clean towel.
  2. Heat olive oil in a pan over medium heat.
  3. Add the bacon and cook until crispy.
  4. Add the sliced onion and cook until translucent, about 5-7 minutes.
  5. Add the potatoes to the pan in layers, mixing them with the bacon and onion.
  6. Reduce the heat to low, cover the pan, and cook for 30-40 minutes until the potatoes are almost cooked through.
  7. Preheat the oven to a medium temperature.
  8. Slice the Reblochon cheese in half.
  9. Scrape off the white rind from the cheese to reveal the orange cheese underneath.
  10. Place a layer of the cooked potatoes in a baking dish.
  11. Top the potatoes with half of the Reblochon cheese, making sure the crust is on top.
  12. Add another layer of potatoes, covering the cheese completely.
  13. Place the remaining half of the Reblochon cheese on top.
  14. Bake in the preheated oven for 15-20 minutes until the cheese is melted and bubbly.
  15. Serve hot and enjoy!

tart_tatan.txt - Tart Tatan

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French apple tart, the Tart Tatan.
  • Understand the process of making a shortcrust pastry and caramel.
  • Master the technique of turning the tart upside down for presentation.

Ingredients

Dough - 250g plain flour - 125g unsalted butter - 25g caster sugar - 1 egg yolk - 50ml water (or 1/4 cup)

Caramel - 100g sugar - 100g plain butter - Squeeze of lemon juice

Apples - 5 apples (or more)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the dough:
  2. Combine flour and butter in a food processor using the pulse function until the mixture resembles coarse sand.
  3. In a separate bowl, whisk together the egg yolk, water, and sugar until the sugar dissolves.
  4. Add the wet ingredients to the food processor and pulse until the dough comes together.
  5. Wrap the dough in plastic wrap and refrigerate for at least 2 hours.
  6. Prepare the apples:
  7. Peel and core the apples.
  8. Using a lemon half, brush the apples to prevent browning.
  9. Make the caramel:
  10. Heat a cast iron pan over medium heat.
  11. Add the sugar and let it melt, stirring occasionally, until it turns a dark brown color.
  12. Remove from heat and immediately add the butter and a squeeze of lemon juice.
  13. Assemble the tart:
  14. Cut the apples into quarters.
  15. Add the apple quarters to the hot caramel, stirring to coat them evenly.
  16. Let the apples cool in the caramel for a few minutes.
  17. Roll out the dough:
  18. Sprinkle flour on a work surface.
  19. Roll out the dough into a rectangle or square large enough to cover the bottom of the cast iron pan.
  20. Carefully transfer the dough to the pan, tucking the edges underneath the apples.
  21. Make a small hole in the center of the dough to allow steam to escape during baking.
  22. Bake the tart:
  23. Preheat the oven to 200°C (400°F).
  24. Bake the tart for 25 minutes, or until the crust is golden brown and the caramel is bubbling.
  25. Turn the tart upside down:
  26. Let the tart cool for 5-10 minutes before attempting to turn it over.
  27. Place a plate over the top of the pan.
  28. Carefully flip the pan and tart onto the plate.
  29. Remove the pan.
  30. Serve:
  31. Dust the tart with powdered sugar for presentation.
  32. Slice and serve warm.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6r69j-LSdTM

thirty_clove_garlic_chicken.txt - 30 Clove Garlic Chicken

Objectives

  • Modify a classic French recipe with modern twists
  • Create a flavorful garlic sauce using cream and cognac
  • Pan-fry croutons in duck fat for a delicious side

Ingredients

30 cloves garlic 1 whole chicken (broken down) Duck fat Cognac (optional) White wine Cream Salt and pepper Flour Parsley Bread (for croutons)

Instructions

  1. Remove the shells and any loose leaves from the garlic cloves.
  2. Season the chicken pieces with salt and pepper.
  3. Heat duck fat in a pan over medium heat.
  4. Sear the chicken wings and neck, then remove and reserve.
  5. Add the garlic cloves to the pan and cook until lightly browned.
  6. Remove the garlic cloves and reserve.
  7. Add more duck fat to the pan and heat over moderate heat.
  8. Coat the chicken pieces with flour and sear gently until golden brown.
  9. Return the seared wings, neck, and garlic cloves to the pan.
  10. Add 30 ml of cognac to the pan and let it bubble up.
  11. Cover the pan and cook for 20 minutes.
  12. Remove the chicken breasts and continue cooking the remaining pieces.
  13. While the chicken cooks, prepare the croutons by pan-frying bread in duck fat until golden brown.
  14. Drain the croutons on paper towels.
  15. Once the chicken is cooked, remove and reserve.
  16. Discard any leftover bits from the pan and scoop the cooked garlic cloves into a bowl.
  17. Press the garlic cloves with a fork to extract the flesh and remove the skins.
  18. Add the garlic flesh to a pan with cream and heat over medium heat.
  19. Reduce the sauce until thick and coat the spoon.
  20. Stir in the remaining cognac, parsley, and season with salt and pepper.
  21. While the sauce is reducing, warm the chicken in the oven.
  22. Briefly broil the chicken to crisp up the skin.
  23. Spread the cooked garlic flesh on the croutons.
  24. Pour the sauce over the chicken and garnish with parsley.
  25. Serve the chicken with the garlic croutons and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kWjVGGI9wCI

tian_courgette_tomato.txt - Tian de Courgette et Tomate

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a classic Provençal dish called Tian de Courgette et Tomate.
  • Understand the importance of thin slicing for the vegetables and the role of slow cooking.
  • Discover how simple ingredients can create complex and delicious flavors.

Ingredients

  • 1 large onion, thinly sliced
  • 1 clove garlic, crushed
  • 1 bay leaf, crushed
  • 1 courgette (zucchini), thinly sliced
  • 4 tomatoes, thinly sliced
  • Olive oil
  • Salt and pepper

Instructions

  1. Thinly slice the onion, courgette, and tomatoes.
  2. Heat olive oil in a pan over medium heat.
  3. Add the sliced onion to the pan and cook for 10-15 minutes until softened.
  4. Crush the garlic clove and rub it inside a baking dish.
  5. Spread the cooked onions evenly at the bottom of the baking dish.
  6. Layer the courgette and tomato slices in the dish, alternating between the two.
  7. Season each layer with salt, pepper, and a sprinkle of crushed bay leaf.
  8. Drizzle generously with olive oil.
  9. Preheat the oven to 200°C (400°F).
  10. Bake the tian in the preheated oven for at least 1 hour, or until the vegetables are softened and reduced, almost like a jam.
  11. Remove from the oven and let cool slightly before serving.
  12. Serve warm or cold with a drizzle of olive oil.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vrd0XFyt5PM

tomate_a_la_provencale.txt - Tomate à la Provençale

Objectives

  • Learn to make the classic French side dish, Tomate à la Provençale.
  • Prepare tomatoes by removing seeds and juice and replacing them with a breadcrumb mixture.
  • Understand the importance of pre-cooking the tomatoes before finishing in the oven.

Ingredients

  • 6-8 tomatoes
  • 1/2 cup flat-leaf parsley
  • 2-3 cloves garlic
  • 1/2 cup breadcrumbs
  • Olive oil
  • Salt
  • Pepper

Instructions

  1. Chop the parsley and garlic.
  2. Cut the tomatoes in half and remove the seeds and juice.
  3. Combine breadcrumbs, chopped parsley, garlic, and a drizzle of olive oil in a bowl.
  4. Season the halved tomatoes with salt and pepper.
  5. Heat a pan over medium heat and add a drizzle of olive oil.
  6. Place the halved tomatoes face down in the pan and cook for 3-4 minutes.
  7. Flip the tomatoes and cook for another 3-4 minutes.
  8. Preheat oven to 180 degrees Celsius (356 degrees Fahrenheit).
  9. Fill the halved tomatoes with the breadcrumb mixture.
  10. Place the tomatoes in the oven and bake for 5-6 minutes, or until the breadcrumb topping is golden brown and crispy.
  11. Serve warm.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=r3RZLnd5IRk

tomato_chorizo_chicken.txt - Tomato and Chorizo Chicken

Objectives

  • Create a French-inspired chicken dish with a Spanish twist.
  • Utilize chorizo sausage for a flavorful and unique addition.
  • Master the art of braising chicken for tender and juicy results.

Ingredients

  • 1 diced onion
  • 1 tablespoon smoked paprika
  • 6 cloves garlic
  • 2 bay leaves
  • 1/2 cup olive oil
  • 1 cup Madeira wine
  • Salt and pepper
  • 1 whole chicken or 4-6 chicken thighs
  • 1/2 cup chorizo, sliced
  • 1 can whole peeled tomatoes
  • 1/4 cup plain flour

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 190 degrees Celsius (375 degrees Fahrenheit) with fan force on.
  2. Dice onion, mince garlic, and slice chorizo.
  3. Chop the top off the tomatoes and remove seeds if desired.
  4. Season chicken pieces with salt, pepper, and paprika.
  5. In a cast iron pot or casserole dish, heat olive oil over medium heat.
  6. Brown chicken pieces on all sides, reserving them on a plate once browned.
  7. Add onions to the pot and cook until softened, about 5 minutes.
  8. Deglaze the pot with Madeira wine, scraping up any browned bits.
  9. Add garlic, bay leaves, and chorizo to the pot and cook until fragrant.
  10. Add chopped tomatoes and cook for 5 minutes, reducing the heat if necessary.
  11. Add the browned chicken pieces back to the pot, ensuring they are coated in the sauce.
  12. Add a small amount of water if the sauce is too dry.
  13. Cover the pot and bake for 30-45 minutes.
  14. Remove the lid and add chicken breasts to the pot.
  15. Cover the pot again and bake for an additional 15 minutes.
  16. Remove the chicken from the oven and serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=WryzkccfVVs

tomato_tapenade.txt - Tomato Tapenade

Objectives

  • Learn to make a delicious tomato-based tapenade.
  • Understand the importance of ingredient selection and balance in a chef's recipe.
  • Discover a delicious alternative to the classic black olive tapenade.

Ingredients

  • 12 sun-dried tomatoes, roughly chopped
  • 2 garlic cloves, pressed
  • 1/2 cup green olives, pitted
  • 1 tablespoon capers
  • 1 tablespoon Dijon mustard
  • 2 tablespoons lemon juice
  • 1/4 cup olive oil
  • Salt and pepper to taste

Instructions

  1. Roughly chop the sun-dried tomatoes.
  2. Add the chopped tomatoes to a food processor and pulse until finely chopped.
  3. Add the green olives, capers, garlic, lemon juice, and mustard to the food processor.
  4. Pulse until the ingredients are roughly chopped but not completely smooth.
  5. Add the olive oil and pulse until combined.
  6. Taste the tapenade and adjust the seasoning with salt and pepper as needed.
  7. Transfer the tapenade to a serving dish.
  8. Serve the tapenade with toasted bread, grilled lamb, or grilled fish.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=JOUk2iIjRmU

tomato_tian.txt - Tomato Tian

Objectives

  • Create a simple and delicious tomato dish using minimal ingredients.
  • Learn the traditional French technique for preparing a Tian.
  • Discover how to maximize flavor by incorporating garlic and herbs into the olive oil.

Ingredients

  • 1 kg tomatoes
  • 1 sprig Rosemary
  • 3 cloves garlic
  • Parsley
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Olive oil
  • Breadcrumbs (optional)

Instructions

  1. Slice the tomatoes into thick slices, removing the core and stem.
  2. Season the tomato slices generously with salt, pepper, and parsley.
  3. Combine olive oil and garlic in a bowl.
  4. Drizzle the garlic-infused olive oil over each tomato slice.
  5. Place a sprig of rosemary in the bottom of a baking dish.
  6. Arrange the tomato slices in the baking dish, layering them in a circular pattern.
  7. Drizzle additional olive oil over the tomatoes.
  8. Sprinkle with fresh rosemary leaves, parsley, and breadcrumbs (optional).
  9. Preheat oven to 200 degrees Celsius (400 degrees Fahrenheit).
  10. Bake for 20-25 minutes, until the tomatoes are golden and shriveled.
  11. Serve immediately. The tomatoes will release juices that can be used for other dishes.
