tomato_topping.txt - Simple Tomato Topping for Toasted Bread

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple tomato topping for toasted bread.
  • Understand the importance of proper tomato preparation.
  • Discover a delicious and easy recipe for a French bruschetta.

Ingredients

  • 1 tablespoon olive oil
  • 2 types of vinegar (e.g., red wine vinegar, balsamic vinegar)
  • 1 clove garlic
  • 1 teaspoon capers
  • 1 spring onion
  • 1/2 teaspoon toasted coriander seeds
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • Fresh basil leaves
  • Ripe tomatoes

Instructions

  1. Peel the tomatoes using the "monde" technique:
    • Make a cross-shaped cut on the top of each tomato.
    • Remove the core.
    • Plunge the tomatoes into boiling water for 20 seconds.
    • Transfer them to cold water.
    • The skin should easily detach.
  2. Cut the peeled tomatoes in half and remove the seeds.
  3. Roughly chop the tomatoes into cubes.
  4. Press the garlic clove using a garlic press and mix it with the olive oil.
  5. Thinly slice the spring onion.
  6. Crush the coriander seeds using a mortar and pestle, the back of a pan, a rolling pin, or a knife.
  7. Prepare the dressing:
    • In a bowl, combine the vinegar, salt, and pepper.
    • Whisk until the salt dissolves.
    • Gradually add the olive oil while whisking continuously.
  8. Add the chopped capers, tomatoes, and garlic-infused oil to the dressing.
  9. Mix well.
  10. Add the spring onion and toasted coriander seeds to the mixture.
  11. Chop the basil leaves just before serving.
  12. Add a few whole basil leaves to the mixture and let it infuse for at least 15 minutes.
  13. Before serving, drain some of the excess juice from the mixture.
  14. Serve the tomato topping on toasted bread.
  15. Garnish with additional basil leaves, a drizzle of olive oil, or lemon zest.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=DJqpXJSlBG4

tort_a_la_fermier.txt - Tort a la Fermier

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French pastry dish, Tort a la Fermier.
  • Master the technique of sealing puff pastry for a perfect result.
  • Discover a versatile recipe that can be adapted with various fillings.

Ingredients

English | Chinese ------- | -------- Flour | 面粉 Butter | 黄油 Milk | 牛奶 Nutmeg | 肉豆蔻 Salt | 盐 Pepper | 胡椒 Ham | 火腿 Cheese | 奶酪 Eggs | 鸡蛋

Instructions

  1. Prepare the bechamel sauce:
  2. Melt butter in a saucepan over medium heat.
  3. Whisk in flour and cook for 2 minutes, creating a roux.
  4. Gradually whisk in cold milk, ensuring no lumps form.
  5. Increase heat to medium-low and stir until thickened.
  6. Season with salt, pepper, and a pinch of nutmeg.
  7. Allow the bechamel to cool completely in a shallow tray in the refrigerator.
  8. Roll out the puff pastry:
  9. Dust your work surface with flour.
  10. Roll out the puff pastry into a thin rectangle, about 3-4 millimeters thick.
  11. Use a plate or a round object to cut out two circles from the pastry.
  12. Place one circle on a baking sheet lined with parchment paper.
  13. Assemble the tort:
  14. Spread a layer of bechamel sauce over the pastry circle.
  15. Arrange slices of ham on top of the bechamel.
  16. Sprinkle with grated cheese.
  17. Repeat the layers of bechamel, ham, and cheese.
  18. Brush the edges of the pastry with egg wash.
  19. Place the second circle of pastry on top, ensuring the edges meet.
  20. Use your fingers to press the edges together, creating a seal.
  21. Trim any excess pastry and tuck the edges in.
  22. Brush the top of the tort with egg wash.
  23. Decorate the top with a simple design using the back of a knife.
  24. Bake the tort:
  25. Preheat oven to 180 degrees Celsius (350 degrees Fahrenheit).
  26. Bake for 30 minutes, or until golden brown and puffed.
  27. Serve immediately:
  28. Enjoy the tort while it's warm and the cheese is melted and gooey.

tournay_potatoes.txt - Tournay Potatoes

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare different sizes of Tournay potatoes
  • Understand the differences between Pomme Cocotte, Pomme Vapeur, and Pomme Chateau
  • Master the technique of carving potatoes into an oval shape

Ingredients

None

Instructions

  1. Cut a small amount off the top and bottom of the potato to create a flat surface.
  2. Hold the paring knife with your thumb on the tip, using only the end of the blade.
  3. Curve the blade into the potato, creating an oval shape.
  4. Turn the potato and continue carving, making small cuts to form seven faces.
  5. Adjust the shape as needed, aiming for a smooth oval.
  6. Reserve the carved potato in water.
  7. Repeat steps 1-6 for each potato.

trout_fillet_creamy_sorrel_sauce.txt - Trout Fillet in Creamy Sorrel Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare a classic French recipe, Trout Fillet in Creamy Sorrel Sauce.
  • Understand the importance of reducing sauces for flavor concentration.
  • Master the technique of removing trout skin for a traditional presentation.

Ingredients

  • Fresh sorrel
  • Trout fillets
  • 1 shallot
  • Double cream or heavy whipping cream
  • White wine
  • Fish stock
  • Butter

Instructions

  1. Finely chop the shallot.
  2. Prepare the sorrel by removing the stems.
  3. Melt butter in a saucepan over medium heat.
  4. Add the chopped shallots and cook for 1-2 minutes, until softened.
  5. Add the white wine and reduce by two-thirds.
  6. Add the fish stock and reduce by two-thirds.
  7. Add the cream and reduce until the sauce thickens.
  8. While the sauce reduces, remove the skin from the trout fillets.
  9. Add the sorrel to the sauce and cook for 20-30 seconds.
  10. Gently cook the trout fillets in the sauce for 30 seconds, or until just cooked through.
  11. Remove the trout fillets from the sauce and set aside.
  12. Add a piece of butter to the sauce and stir until melted.
  13. Plate the trout fillets and pour the sauce over them.
  14. Garnish with a sprig of sorrel and serve immediately.

tucked_orders.txt - Tucked Orders

Objectives

  • Explore a simple French home-cooked meal
  • Learn to make a savory pastry dish similar to quiche
  • Understand the difference between Gruyere and Emmental cheese

Ingredients

  • 1 roll of puff pastry
  • 4 eggs
  • 100 grams plain yogurt
  • 2 tablespoons cream
  • 100 grams Emmental cheese
  • 2 types of ham (cooked and raw)
  • 2 tablespoons mustard
  • Butter
  • Flour
  • Salt and pepper

Instructions

  1. Grease a quiche pan with butter and dust with flour.
  2. Place the puff pastry into the pan, pressing the edges down to prevent sticking.
  3. Refrigerate the pastry while preparing the savory mix.
  4. Preheat oven to 180 degrees Celsius (356 degrees Fahrenheit).
  5. In a bowl, whisk together 4 eggs, a dash of black pepper, and 100 grams of plain yogurt.
  6. Add 2 tablespoons of cream and mix well.
  7. Stir in 100 grams of Emmental cheese.
  8. Add the cooked and raw ham to the mixture.
  9. Spread a thin layer of mustard on the bottom of the pastry crust.
  10. Pour the savory mixture over the mustard.
  11. Bake for 40-45 minutes in the oven on the middle rack, without using the fan setting.
  12. Let cool slightly before slicing and serving.

turbulent_togo.txt - Turbulent Togo

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a traditional French rice pudding called Turbulent Togo.
  • Understand the historical context of the recipe's ingredients.
  • Discover the unique cooking method that creates a creamy, crust-topped rice pudding.

Ingredients

  • 1.5 liters of milk (6 cups)
  • 1 teaspoon of cinnamon powder
  • A few drops of vanilla essence
  • 200 grams of Arborio rice (1.75 cups)
  • 200 grams of castor sugar (1.75 cups)
  • Pinch of salt (optional)

Instructions

  1. In a bowl, combine the Arborio rice, cinnamon powder, castor sugar, and a pinch of salt (optional).
  2. Mix the ingredients together with your hands, ensuring everything is well blended.
  3. Heat the milk in a saucepan over medium heat.
  4. Add the vanilla essence to the milk and bring it to a boil.
  5. Remove the milk from the heat.
  6. Pour the warm milk slowly over the rice mixture in an earthenware glazed dish or a metal pie dish, making sure not to stir or mix the ingredients.
  7. Preheat the oven to 150 degrees Celsius (300 degrees Fahrenheit).
  8. Place the dish in the oven and cook for three hours (or two hours if using two dishes).
  9. Once cooked, the rice pudding will have a brown crust on top.
  10. Gently scoop out the rice pudding to reveal the creamy, milky rice underneath.
  11. Serve the rice pudding in a bowl, adding a dollop of cream on top for extra richness.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ezU923QQMW0

twice_baked_cheese_souffle_with_pancetta_and_thyme_sauce.txt - Twice Baked Cheese Souffle with Pancetta and Thyme Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn to make a twice-baked cheese souffle with a Pancetta and Thyme sauce.
  • Understand the importance of proper ramekin preparation.
  • Master the technique for making a smooth, flavorful base for the souffle.

Ingredients

  • 25g butter
  • 25g flour
  • Cold milk
  • Salt
  • 1 bay leaf
  • Nutmeg
  • 60g cheese
  • 2 egg yolks
  • 2 egg whites
  • Pinch of salt
  • 500ml pure cream
  • Thyme
  • Pancetta

Instructions

  1. Prepare the ramekins:
  2. Coat the bottom and edges of the ramekins with butter using a paintbrush.
  3. Make stripes from the bottom of the ramekin to the top with the butter to help the souffle rise evenly.
  4. Dust the ramekins with flour, tapping out any excess.
  5. Make the base (Bechamel):
  6. Melt butter in a pan over medium heat.
  7. Add flour and whisk until combined, cooking for 1-2 minutes until the mixture is white and free of floury taste.
  8. Gradually whisk in cold milk.
  9. Increase heat to medium-high and stir until the mixture is smooth and thickened.
  10. Season with salt, add a bay leaf, and a pinch of nutmeg.
  11. Remove from heat and stir in cheese until melted and smooth.
  12. Remove the bay leaf.
  13. Whisk in egg yolks off the heat.
  14. Beat the egg whites:
  15. Beat egg whites with a pinch of salt until stiff peaks form.
  16. Combine the base and egg whites:
  17. Gently fold a quarter to half of the base into the egg whites, using a circular motion.
  18. Continue folding in the remaining base until the mixture is evenly blended and pale yellow.
  19. Fill the ramekins:
  20. Pour the mixture into the prepared ramekins, leaving a small edge at the top.
  21. Wipe any excess mixture from the rim.
  22. Bake the souffles:
  23. Preheat oven to 180°C.
  24. Place the ramekins on a baking sheet lined with parchment paper.
  25. Bake for 25 minutes.
  26. Make the sauce:
  27. While the souffles bake, heat cream in a pan over medium heat.
  28. Season with salt and add thyme sprigs.
  29. Bring to a boil.
  30. Quickly fry slices of pancetta until crisp.
  31. Add pancetta to the cream sauce and reduce heat.
  32. Unmold the souffles:
  33. Carefully remove the souffles from the oven and allow them to cool slightly.
  34. Run a knife around the edges of the ramekins to loosen the souffles.
  35. Invert the ramekins onto a plate to unmold the souffles.
  36. Prepare the souffles for the second bake:
  37. Place the unmolded souffles on a plate and let them cool completely.
  38. Assemble and bake the souffles again:
  39. Preheat oven to 180°C.
  40. Spoon a little sauce onto the bottom of each ramekin.
  41. Place the souffles on top of the sauce, upside down.
  42. Drizzle more sauce over the souffles.
  43. Sprinkle with cheese.
  44. Bake for 10-15 minutes until the souffles are golden brown and crusty.
  45. Finish and serve:
  46. Remove the souffles from the oven and garnish with pancetta and thyme.
  47. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_O7qBmw_4YM

vanilla_slice.txt - Vanilla Slice

Objectives

  • Learn to make an easy, French-style vanilla slice.
  • Understand how to prepare pastry cream with vanilla bean.
  • Discover a simple technique for preventing puff pastry from rising.

Ingredients

  • 1/2 liter milk
  • 1-2 tablespoons sugar
  • 1 vanilla bean
  • 4 egg yolks
  • 2 tablespoons sugar
  • 2 tablespoons flour
  • 1 tablespoon corn flour
  • 2 sheets of pre-rolled puff pastry
  • Caster sugar (for sprinkling)
  • Rum (optional)

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 200 degrees Celsius (400 degrees Fahrenheit).
  2. In a saucepan, combine milk, 1-2 tablespoons sugar, and vanilla bean (split and seeds extracted).
  3. Heat the milk mixture over medium heat, stirring occasionally, until it just begins to boil.
  4. While the milk is heating, whisk together egg yolks and 2 tablespoons sugar until pale and fluffy.
  5. Sift flour and corn flour together and gradually whisk into the egg yolk mixture.
  6. Gradually pour half of the heated milk into the egg yolk mixture, whisking constantly.
  7. Pour the mixture back into the saucepan, add the remaining milk, and whisk until smooth.
  8. Cook the mixture over medium heat, whisking constantly, until it thickens.
  9. Reduce heat and simmer for 1.5 minutes, stirring constantly, until the custard reaches a thick, custard-like consistency.
  10. Pour the custard into a cold tray, cover with cling film, and refrigerate until completely cool.
  11. Place puff pastry sheets on a baking tray.
  12. Use a fork to poke holes in the pastry to prevent it from rising.
  13. Sprinkle the pastry with caster sugar.
  14. Place another baking tray on top of the pastry and weigh it down.
  15. Bake for 15-20 minutes, or until the pastry is golden brown.
  16. Let the pastry cool completely.
  17. While the pastry is cooling, whisk the cooled custard with rum (optional).
  18. Spread the custard evenly over one sheet of pastry.
  19. Place the second sheet of pastry on top of the custard.
  20. Trim the edges of the vanilla slice with a knife to create a neat, even shape.
  21. Sprinkle the vanilla slice with caster sugar.
  22. Serve immediately or refrigerate until ready to eat.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZY-wZPBvDz0

veal_steak_leon.txt - Veal Steak Leon Style

Objectives

  • Learn to cook veal steaks in the "Leon" style, a regional French cooking method.
  • Understand the concept of "appellation" in French cuisine and how it relates to regional ingredients and cooking techniques.
  • Create a simple, flavorful bistro dish using readily available ingredients.

Ingredients

  • Veal steaks
  • Onions
  • Butter
  • Vinegar
  • Parsley
  • Tomatoes
  • Salt and pepper
  • Salad dressing

Instructions

  1. Chop onions and set aside.
  2. Melt butter in a pan over medium heat.
  3. Add onions to the pan and cook for 10 minutes, stirring occasionally.
  4. While the onions cook, trim and season the veal steaks with salt and pepper.
  5. Heat a separate pan over medium-high heat.
  6. Add a small amount of butter to the pan and swirl to coat.
  7. Sear the veal steaks for 1-2 minutes on each side, aiming for a light browning.
  8. Remove the veal steaks from the pan and set aside.
  9. Add the cooked onions to the pan with the veal steaks.
  10. Deglaze the pan with vinegar, scraping up any browned bits from the bottom.
  11. Add parsley to the pan and stir to combine.
  12. Remove the pan from the heat.
  13. Plate the veal steaks with a generous amount of the onion mixture.
  14. Garnish with a tomato and a small salad.
  15. Drizzle with salad dressing and sprinkle with additional parsley.
  16. Serve immediately.

veloute_sauce.txt - Velouté Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a classic French velouté sauce.
  • Understand the versatility of velouté sauce in various dishes.
  • Discover how to enhance velouté sauce with additional ingredients.

Ingredients

  • 1 tablespoon of white roux
  • 1 cup of chicken stock
  • Salt
  • White pepper
  • Mushrooms (cooked)
  • Double cream (optional)
  • Parsley (optional)

Instructions

  1. Combine the white roux and half of the chicken stock in a saucepan.
  2. Stir continuously until the roux is fully dissolved.
  3. Add the remaining chicken stock and bring the mixture to a boil.
  4. Reduce the heat to low and simmer for 10-15 minutes, allowing the sauce to thicken.
  5. Season the sauce with salt and white pepper to taste.
  6. Add the cooked mushrooms to the sauce.
  7. Stir in a tablespoon or two of double cream for a richer flavor and color (optional).
  8. Garnish with chopped parsley (optional).
  9. Serve over chicken, fish, or use as a base for soups or pies.

vichy_carrots.txt - Vichy Carrots

Objectives

  • Learn to make a simple and delicious vichy carrots dish.
  • Understand the importance of using fresh ingredients and high-quality sparkling mineral water.
  • Explore a classic French recipe with a modern twist.

Ingredients

  • Carrots
  • Vichy Célestins Sparkling Mineral Water
  • Butter
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Fresh Thyme (optional)

Instructions

  1. Wash and peel the carrots.
  2. Cut the carrots into thin slices, about 1/4 inch thick.
  3. Heat a large saucepan over medium heat.
  4. Add butter to the saucepan and melt.
  5. Add the sliced carrots to the saucepan and cook for about 5 minutes, stirring occasionally.
  6. Pour the Vichy Célestins Sparkling Mineral Water into the saucepan.
  7. Season with salt and pepper to taste.
  8. Add fresh thyme sprigs (optional) for extra flavor.
  9. Bring the mixture to a boil, then reduce heat to low and simmer for about 15-20 minutes, or until the carrots are tender.
  10. Serve the vichy carrots hot as a side dish or as part of a larger meal.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=RH3fZmet7XU

white_beans_tomato_sauce.txt - White Beans with Tomato Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn to cook white beans from dry.
  • Master the art of soaking and blanching beans for optimal texture.
  • Create a flavorful tomato sauce with bacon, duck fat, and chicken stock.

Ingredients

  • 1 large pan
  • White beans (quantity not specified)
  • Water (for soaking and blanching)
  • Chicken stock
  • 1/2 onion, large pieces
  • 1 carrot, large pieces
  • 1 garlic clove
  • Bay leaves
  • Piece of ham, cured with pepper
  • Leftover duck fat
  • Thyme
  • Shallots
  • Garlic clove
  • Pork belly
  • Tomato paste
  • 400 grams tomato puree (no skin)
  • Sugar
  • Black pepper
  • Parsley (for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Soak the white beans in cold water for 2 hours.
  2. Blanch the beans by bringing them to a boil in cold water for 3 minutes.
  3. Drain the blanched beans and rinse with cold water.
  4. In a large pan, bring water to a boil.
  5. Add the beans, half onion, carrot, garlic clove, bay leaves, and ham to the boiling water.
  6. Reduce heat to a simmer and cook for 1.5 to 2.5 hours, depending on the type of beans and soaking time.
  7. While the beans are cooking, prepare the tomato sauce.
  8. Heat duck fat in a pan over medium heat.
  9. Add thyme, shallots, and a garlic clove to the hot duck fat and cook for 2-3 minutes.
  10. Add tomato paste and cook for 1 minute.
  11. Add tomato puree and cook for 2-3 minutes until it reaches a simmer.
  12. Add chicken stock, sugar, and black pepper to the tomato sauce and simmer for 15-20 minutes.
  13. After the beans have cooked for 1.5 hours, add salt and cook for an additional 10 minutes.
  14. Remove the aromatics (onion, carrot, garlic, bay leaves, and ham) from the beans.
  15. Drain the cooked beans and add them to the tomato sauce.
  16. Add the cooked pork belly to the sauce.
  17. Add more pepper, salt, and parsley to the sauce.
  18. Simmer the beans in the sauce for 10 minutes.
  19. Serve hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=9E2bilO8NiI

white_cabbage_salad.txt - White Cabbage Salad

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare a white cabbage salad in the style of Paul Bocuse
  • Understand the importance of using fresh, homegrown ingredients
  • Discover the unique flavor combination of cabbage, bacon, apple, and creamy dressing

Ingredients

  • 1 white cabbage
  • 1 tablespoon of vinegar
  • 1 tablespoon of oil
  • 50 ml of cream
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • 1 tablespoon of butter
  • 1 apple
  • Bacon (amount not specified)
  • Chives (optional)
  • Lemon juice (optional)

Instructions

  1. Remove the outer leaves of the white cabbage, leaving only the white leaves.
  2. Trim off the hard core of the cabbage.
  3. Rinse the cabbage leaves in cold water with a bit of vinegar.
  4. Cut the cabbage leaves into thin julienne strips.
  5. Combine the vinegar, oil, cream, salt, and pepper in a bowl.
  6. Whisk the dressing until it has a whipped cream-like texture.
  7. Pour the dressing over the cabbage and mix well.
  8. Refrigerate the cabbage salad while preparing the bacon and apple.
  9. Pan-fry the bacon until crispy and set aside on a kitchen towel to absorb excess fat.
  10. Melt butter in a pan over high heat.
  11. Add the apple slices to the pan and caramelize until lightly browned.
  12. Add the bacon and apple to the cabbage salad and mix well.
  13. Garnish with chives and a squeeze of lemon juice, if desired.
  14. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=N8bMINTEC9w

white_chicken_stock.txt - White Chicken Stock

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a simple white chicken stock using Escoffier style.
  • Understand the importance of blanching the chicken bones for a clear stock.
  • Learn how to make a bouquet garni and use it for flavoring the stock.

Ingredients

  • 1.5 kg chicken bones and carcass
  • 200 g leeks, celery, onion, and carrots
  • 1 piece of clean cheesecloth
  • A few cloves
  • 1 piece of thyme
  • 1 piece of bay leaf
  • A few sprigs of parsley
  • String

Instructions

  1. Prepare the bouquet garni:
  2. Wrap the thyme, bay leaf, and parsley in the cheesecloth.
  3. Tie the bundle tightly with string.
  4. Blanch the chicken bones:
  5. Bring a pot of water to a boil.
  6. Add the chicken bones and carcass to the boiling water.
  7. Boil for a few minutes, then remove the bones and rinse under cold water.
  8. Make the stock:
  9. Return the blanched chicken bones to the pot.
  10. Add enough water to cover the bones.
  11. Bring the water to a boil, then reduce heat to low.
  12. Add the bouquet garni, onions, leeks, celery, and carrots.
  13. Simmer for 45 minutes.
  14. Cool and filter:
  15. Remove the bouquet garni and vegetables from the stock.
  16. Let the stock cool down for about an hour.
  17. Filter the stock through a fine-mesh sieve to remove any remaining impurities.
  18. Use the stock:
  19. The white chicken stock can be used for a variety of purposes, including making sauces, cooking pasta, rice, or stews.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=uDVhNwuPj8E

white_chocolate_mousse.txt - White Chocolate Mousse

Objectives

  • Make a simple white chocolate mousse with just two ingredients.
  • Learn a foolproof method for melting chocolate.
  • Create a beautiful and delicious dessert presentation.

Ingredients

  • White chocolate (pellets or tablet)
  • Heavy whipping cream (33-35% fat content)
  • Frozen berries (optional)
  • Lemon juice (optional)
  • Sugar (optional)
  • Mint (optional)
  • Roasted nuts (optional)

Instructions

  1. Melt the white chocolate using a bain-marie.
  2. Bring water to a boil in a saucepan.
  3. Turn off the heat.
  4. Place a heat-proof bowl on top of the saucepan, ensuring it doesn't touch the water.
  5. Add the white chocolate to the bowl and let it melt naturally.
  6. Warm the cream slightly.
  7. Heat the cream in a microwave for 20 seconds or gently warm it in a saucepan.
  8. Combine the melted chocolate and warm cream.
  9. Add the warm cream to the melted chocolate while it's still on the bain-marie.
  10. Gently mix the chocolate and cream together until combined.
  11. Whip the cream.
  12. Chill a bowl in the freezer.
  13. Pour the cold cream into the chilled bowl.
  14. Use a whisk to whip the cream until it forms stiff peaks.
  15. Fold the whipped cream into the chocolate mixture.
  16. Add a small amount of whipped cream to the chocolate mixture and fold it in gently.
  17. Continue folding in the whipped cream until it's fully incorporated.
  18. Chill the mousse.
  19. Transfer the mousse to a container and refrigerate until it sets.
  20. Prepare the berry sauce (optional).
  21. Blend frozen berries in a blender.
  22. Heat the berry mixture in a saucepan until melted.
  23. Strain the berry mixture through a sieve to remove seeds.
  24. Add lemon juice and sugar to taste.
  25. Chill the berry sauce.
  26. Plate the mousse.
  27. Use a spoon to create a canal on the plate.
  28. Garnish the plate with mint, roasted nuts, and berry sauce.
  29. Gently spoon the mousse into the canal.
  30. Chill the plated mousse until firm.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=B9h8Sbj20ac

whole_fish_bake.txt - Baked Whole Fish with Fennel and Potatoes

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare and bake a whole fish with simple ingredients.
  • Understand how to remove scales and fins from a fish.
  • Discover a simple and delicious way to cook a whole fish.

Ingredients

  • 1 Black Brim (or similar fish) 800g-1kg
  • 1 fennel bulb
  • 1 onion, thinly sliced
  • 2-3 potatoes, cut into quarters
  • 2-3 tomatoes, cubed
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 1 handful of parsley
  • 1-2 cloves garlic
  • Olive oil
  • Dry herbs (optional)
  • Salt and pepper
  • Red wine (optional)
  • Water

Instructions

  1. Clean the fish by removing the scales and any remaining gills.
  2. Carefully trim the fins, paying special attention to the sharp ones near the tail.
  3. Prepare the vegetables:
    • Remove the tough outer layers of the fennel bulb and discard.
    • Thinly slice the fennel bulb.
    • Cut the potatoes into quarters.
    • Cube the tomatoes.
  4. Preheat the oven to 180 degrees Celsius.
  5. Combine the prepared vegetables in a baking dish.
  6. Add the bay leaf, parsley, garlic, salt, pepper, and dry herbs (optional).
  7. Drizzle with olive oil and add a small glass of water (approximately 100-150 ml).
  8. Place the baking dish in the oven and bake for 30-40 minutes.
  9. While the vegetables are baking, prepare the fish:
    • Score the fish with a knife to help with cooking.
    • Season the inside of the fish with salt, pepper, and a small amount of the onion, fennel, and parsley from the baking dish.
    • Place the fish in the refrigerator until the vegetables are done.
  10. After 30-40 minutes, remove the baking dish from the oven.
  11. Gently mix the vegetables and place the prepared fish on top.
  12. Drizzle with olive oil and add a little water or red wine (optional).
  13. Bake the fish for another 30 minutes at 180 degrees Celsius.
  14. Once the fish is cooked, carefully remove it from the baking dish.
  15. Use a fish spatula to gently remove the flesh from the bones.
  16. Serve the fish with the baked vegetables and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Nq9uYw-8N3g

yellow_pilaf_rice.txt - Yellow Pilaf Rice

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare French-style pilaf rice
  • Understand the importance of slow cooking and gentle stirring
  • Master the art of presenting rice for a visually appealing dish

Ingredients

  • 200 grams of rice
  • 200 grams of water
  • 75 grams of finely chopped onions
  • 40 grams of butter
  • Salt and pepper
  • Bouquet garni (in a paper diffuser)
  • 1 teaspoon of curry powder
  • 1 teaspoon of turmeric

Instructions

  1. Bring 200 grams of water to a boil and keep it warm for later.
  2. Melt 40 grams of butter in a pan over low heat.
  3. Add 75 grams of finely chopped onions to the melted butter and cook until translucent (about 3-4 minutes).
  4. Add 200 grams of unwashed rice to the onions and butter.
  5. Gently stir the rice to coat it in the butter and onions.
  6. Let the rice sit in the pan for 1-2 minutes, until it becomes slightly translucent.
  7. Pour the boiling water into the pan with the rice.
  8. Season with salt, pepper, and a mix of 1 teaspoon curry powder and 1 teaspoon turmeric.
  9. Stir the rice and water mixture.
  10. Increase the heat slightly and bring the mixture to a simmer, just before it starts to boil.
  11. Preheat oven to 200 degrees Celsius (420 degrees Fahrenheit).
  12. Cover the pan with a lid or aluminum foil.
  13. Bake the rice in the oven for 20 minutes.
  14. Remove the pan from the oven and discard the bouquet garni.
  15. Fluff the rice with a fork to separate the grains.
  16. Serve the rice in a bowl or on a plate.
  17. Garnish with chopped coriander and dried shallots for a visually appealing presentation.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Y_rSu40WXmA
